# Welcome | Knowledge Base

Welcome to the Lunch Money knowledge base! 👋![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2)

Here, you can find detailed information on the different app features, step-by-step instructions, and answers to frequently asked questions.

Navigating the Knowledge Base

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/#ask-or-search)

Ask or Search

At the top right corner of any page within this Knowledge Base, you can click on the search bar to search any keyword, or type a question:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FIDRwuH1oaL2JL0S57K44%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D914ebf0f-0322-464e-aeb6-a7a34d106c6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49521e11&sv=2)

The search engine will scan through the Knowledge Base and summarize an answer in seconds, with references to help you find out more information.

You could also search any topic or question directly the search field below:

# Getting Started | Knowledge Base

Congratulations on starting your 30-day trial with Lunch Money! 🎉

In this article, we’ll take you step-by-step to get you all set up, through the onboarding process, connecting your accounts, setting up your categories and budget, and the tools available to analyze your spending!

circle-info

If you haven’t signed up yet, head over to [lunchmoney.apparrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/)
 to register and follow along!

Shall we begin? ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) 🫴

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Step 1: Getting started**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-1-getting-started)
    
*   [**Step 2: Add transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-2-add-transactions)
    
*   [**Step 3: Categorize your transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-3-categorize-your-transactions)
    
*   [**Step 4: Set up recurring items**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-4-set-up-recurring-items)

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-1-getting-started)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 1: Getting Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first step after you sign up to Lunch Money is to select your onboarding path. You will have the option to choose between the following:

*   **Start fresh -** This is the recommended option for following along with this Quick Start Guide. By going through the "Start fresh" path, you will be taken through some first steps to set up some categories and your date and currency display preferences.
    
*   **Set up demo -** This option will set up a demo budget account with pre-filled data so that you can play around with the different features before adding your personal bank accounts and transactions. Once you are done with the demo account, you can then create a new budget account to get started with your personal data.
    
*   **Import from Mint -** If you are migrating from Mint and have a CSV file containing your existing data, we recommend going with this option to import your transactions into Lunch Money. For a quick start guide on migrating from Mint, please [see here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint)
    .
    
*   **Skip the walkthrough -** This option will skip all the basic setup steps, giving you a completely blank slate to work with. There will be no categories set up, and you’ll be set with default date and display preferences.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfyFwbl7f_nEo1OGtUPyZ0NWpPwfXiBuo-EhBZtX69W9rnM-O-BPUc5OfnLgA-V9BRctVTBT3URZWplBM-_rKKl8xyPfu4CpqkVYBEtzp11dGoHMk7QwFQMZ8T-WjlKm3ZM-Ob0_nrTR2ZnKQIC1rWGY5YY%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af81a340&sv=2)

In this guide, we'll be working off of the "Start fresh" path, meaning that after you've gone through onboarding, you’ll already have your basic categories, display and currency settings set up. On Step 3 of the onboarding process, we recommend linking at least one synced bank account:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXekltlaNXknOSy0WByN0J4E_5Ou7Llkg0OhkeK0sNB_91EGXlSWhNwiekLDz8hyhCmWC-ZpjNfWvdaYIs0kdUKkyXlByQLFv9h9-T_Vg7ckdEZxndmA21eBeNbwrAEzlnDISceySSrUYUnuzDaByYTYUT8r%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=419be04c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-2-add-transactions)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 2: Add transactions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are various options for adding your transactions into Lunch Money. Transactions can be added manually, [imported via CSV file](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#import-transactions-via-csv)
, or [automatically imported](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports)
 from synced bank accounts.

**If you have already added an account for automatic bank syncing** and see your transactions on the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
 page, you’re ready to start categorizing your transactions and can skip to [Step 3](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-3-categorize-your-transactions)
 of this article.

**If you didn't add an account for automatic bank syncing** at the end of onboarding, you'll want to head over to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page and start by adding some of your most frequently used accounts — this could be a credit card or a checking/savings account.

By adding a synced bank account, your transactions will automatically sync into Lunch Money, yet you can also set up manually-managed accounts for any institutions not currently supported for automatic syncing. For manually-managed accounts, you can either [add transactions manually](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-actions#manual-creation)
, or [import transactions in bulk with a CSV file](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#import-transactions-via-csv)
.

**How to add a synced bank account**

1.  Open the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page
    
2.  Click on the "Add account" button to open the 'Add Account or Asset' panel on the right-side of the screen:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXevQQ9a3ItDNQAYs_XynyREiFfWEHTA6r5AZle1KsRw9aOualO5InAAWKSg74Ac76UxaTHOWHVTz399_Y9A1_7DeSGFtSHdZWDIbYgEf7A7gkvMF-Zbk5weHK4Fp1tO_SccmrsfCBZW0QW0CpSFglv11YcQ%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=400ddaaf&sv=2)

1.  Next, click on "Auto-import from my bank", select the relevant country, and click on "Continue":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdVRlonhlDf0T9ULwrvIwjzWXPPv2CmHyIqjtqXOLxQnsNMH8fnYIaV3UF0MbDNu1RBJ6-x9jVHtUGi-J2Lm7pYTag24SpX_DHJATB5Bw52YnThx3sis87voNdWUh1OUmT8mKKrQx8ITamSYewied65dOEA%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6f7ff74&sv=2)

1.  Once the Plaid dialogue loads, click on "Get Started" and log in (or continue as guest)
    
2.  In the search bar, type the name of your institution and select the relevant option from the list:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfo8a5fMW3WQ36FhxUBVebBDnxqsNpCTZkYmi04a5M-d3SyQdFV1VOSSGiA5yEh0HVXQJypB08CkUUueSFluNKlkRdQibyyrjmm2ncyL3nchUsSaahncsxY8x9N41bPT5hZQ952j6EFAhFTe5i59Dl79rS8%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e92c950&sv=2)

1.  Follow the instructions on the screen to enter your credentials
    
2.  Once your login is confirmed, check all accounts that you’d like to connect from the institution, and click on "Continue". If the connection was successful, you'll see a confirmation screen and can click on "Continue" again.
    
3.  Next, you'll choose how you'd like to set up this new account within Lunch Money. You will set the display name, and since this is your first account, toggle the option for "No, this is a new account or I will merge it later" and click on "Start Importing":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcx1I-_z-9LVOwJo3bN3iX8RtOO0dLtI5qhpJd_sD1qBkOYIjgAoLevg3VfbkeayY7JHf9JrACBqaMvA_ISRYe9jSxH3dR8X4aNDoX-9UbMZ5wkGmflWqI_OI9FoPPazHbjT5N4np0RSPueL4uYdEvBeAk%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1b997cb&sv=2)

Your synced accounts will be added to the table on the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page and a confirmation message will appear on the bottom left of the screen:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfuDXJ4mC-HZqImekFZTTKUSXU9QUejE6BTg0GutHoTYR7V09dCxQvaFb5e5bRUUFSmKvS2LGnjRcJUOLotRsVV3-td0a3It_Z1tLTRp8Ja1R6xyzyua8d-J0mG0fdkWoIe3a2QDL5ab78Fif3el3h4YwkU%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4cba940&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#set-up-manually-managed-accounts-and-assets)

**Set up manually-managed accounts and assets**

If you use banking institutions not currently supported within Lunch Money, you can head back to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page to add them. Manually-managed account balances are updated automatically when you add, remove or update a transaction assigned to that account.

Manually-managed accounts are also great for tracking cash in your wallet, assets (eg. car or real estate), gift card or loyalty account balances, and crypto-currency.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfSyOKMuEuQMhsjRAk-ALKdkseSmHkaggJMhKwqVMctN3RkJ70AsQTqNDGhbGwrvmiYnL8EIBomOiyjeGv1Rgw2DDAGXk5PEZTpMNjsKd-26gqr4mljKcD95suOITLUZptAJJKn9WTv2Vjjep0ZWedoQ_T8%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac8dbf87&sv=2)

Once you've added your manually managed-account, you can [manually create transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-actions#manual-creation)
 on the Transactions page, or [bulk import transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-1-upload-csv)
 with a CSV file.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#import-transactions-via-csv)

Import transactions via CSV

CSV importing is a popular choice for getting bulk transactions into Lunch Money. This is a quick way to import historical transaction data for synced accounts, or current transaction data for manually-managed accounts. To read more about the CSV Import feature, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXe4DL10LqrItauYzHcnTsYIkmqwfO6hIF35FSSvxdjfhtgn8BrH8cri0uF1edKRgRJ9cUGUuvfrUG4KL82w305xwLcXHWoUyDJlEsOPfPYb9WTMibZHpucg1GaiXeWPhvkSBHFQ7fD1SpQksvp-zs29wvE%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e11fd934&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-3-categorize-your-transactions)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 3: Categorize your transactions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Categories are set up and managed on the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
 page, and are an essential way to organize your transactions. Categories also dictate how associated transactions will be treated throughout Lunch Money.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fa80RathF7yzcjJX59KpQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ca537b0-6265-4541-953e-a7e2c92956f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d47557c&sv=2)

circle-info

To successfully work within Lunch Money, it’s important to understand the difference between income, expense and transfer categories. To read about category properties, [click herearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#the-category-properties)
.

While you should already have your basic categories set up from the onboarding stage, we also recommend checking out the Auto-Categorization tool on the Categories page to help create and automatically assign categories to your synced transactions. To learn more about Auto-Categorization, [click herearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories)
.

If you wish to manually categorize or simply review your categorized transactions, you can head over to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page. Categorizing manually may take some time initially but eventually, you'll barely need to do manual work to organize transactions as the system will automatically create rules to auto-categorize future similar transactions.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdhjEPinqCDYj9GO49DWjPv6hQ6Qrkeufmq_TRBgJ8KoWQ009CzbYEwUN9fZJ4616b2y1c-Wr7ygSo70RqspeUJM6Pl3pgFTCgo37T_lwh8ApKMhW17bvPhYNiG1h1tny-AuWNvp1f82yoM7k3DX1bgt8Y%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0c2bbfa&sv=2)

circle-info

If you'd like to prevent rules from being created when you update categories, you can disable this option under 'Rule preferences' on the [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-4-set-up-recurring-items)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 4: Set up recurring items


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recurring Items are helpful when you want to track transactions that repeat regularly, whether they are expenses (eg. subscriptions, rent) or income (eg. monthly salary).

Recurring items represent repeating income or expenses transactions, with either fixed or fluctuating amounts, that would generally occur on a regular cadence with predictable dates (eg. twice a month, every 6 months, annually, etc.).

**Some examples of recurring income include:**

*   Monthly fixed salary
    
*   Bi-weekly salary
    
*   Monthly credit card money-back rewards
    

**Some examples of recurring expenses include:**

*   Annual streaming service subscription (eg. Netflix, Spotify, etc.)
    
*   Gym membership that renews every 4 weeks
    
*   Monthly rent payments
    
*   Annual land tax payments
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXek6X9OrFzENrJcsREelr0823bckWD63uIooKcinHzyGoL7B9qAv5oo6ImQXrfaJ7yRRG8RwQ6oznNc6pynrmvdb7JcuG3hl28H3KOKkZv0Ml9gUyRhh672lhndpcq3d_1dJ2HWKuP9oxwR6LAxqd3evrb3%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72c0ff7c&sv=2)

Having Recurring Items set up helps you plan ahead, and if an expected expense or income is missed, you'll be able to see it marked as missing in the recurring item details, so that you can review and fix it if necessary. The projected spending and income defined by your Recurring Items are also important to consider when planning your budget.

Rules are automatically created when a recurring item is set up. The rules will automatically link transactions to a recurring item if the cadence, amount and payee are a match. Additional rules to link transactions to recurring items can also be set up manually via the [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#how-to-set-up-a-recurring-item)

How to set up a Recurring Item

The process to set up Recurring Items is the same for Income and for Expenses, but the step below describe it with the wording specific to recurring expenses:

1.  Open the [Recurringarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring)
     page
    
2.  Click on "Add New Recurring Item" to open up the 'Create Recurring Item' panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Fill in the recurring item details starting with the merchant name and set the transaction category.
    
4.  For the estimated billing date, select the day in the month when you expect the payment to generally occur
    
5.  For the repeating cadence, select the relevant value from the list (eg. "monthly", "twice a month") or select "Custom" to set your own cadence
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcvh2W710I1QelpImmG5rKENWsIlP04VjeRznBKE46LzrlyeQeeAy9wseKwi4QDvtLRQh47Vszm8fKDLGApBryCg7EEU07umHZh4KGjNcejWAiS_aLiJNOaO90gKbJAfjX-99t3t7dgyH_rAjfGao29LrAk%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb2cbc04&sv=2)

1.  Under "Optional Properties", you can also select an account in the "Paid from account" field. If this is set to a specific account, Lunch Money will know to look for the transaction under that specific account.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfV6xHbqZ5BtVQTFNhJrA-ng6Acs3l1rGtHfQcckIZLHlVJ9p81qCbFpw1ivhkhs2BrwSMfNvM3-pLegwgF4K9N9U9TiQA8oHfT8quNjS9787HAori0hxvQ3i7oYurC6e8Y5tolXKZ7crQkZ2fzt9lybSc%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=551343ab&sv=2)

1.  Click "next", and on the next page you will enter either a fixed amount, or a range (if the amount tends to fluctuate):
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeuJMOEuLwYB0qQIJyw9byxeqWctExqRBePP6E5RNtXwQctN4qOXX-bzJ3u1lwg_aibNiWTQTy5-RVsnyLVLT3Rv9J5v4D0F2v7-OyGry8E6LxfzDpl9g7cbcx9V69_PUj1V12ZLVm3wIN6LJuJkUVU3yw%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=570ae372&sv=2)

1.  Finalize by clicking on "Create".
    

Once set up, all recurring items will appear in the table. If you have yearly recurring items, they will only appear in the table for the month on which they are due.

If you have automatically-syncing accounts connected, Lunch Money will automatically search through new transactions as they sync, based on the [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 that you have set up, and once a transaction matches, it will automatically be linked to the relevant Recurring Item. If a recurring transaction doesn’t link automatically, you can learn more about manual linking by [clicking here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/recurring-transactions#manual-linking)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-5-define-your-budget)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 5: Define your budget


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that you have all of your transactions categorized and recurring items set up, it's time to set up your budget. Setting up and managing the budget is done via the [Budgetarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/budget/2024/03)
 page.

There's no "right" or "wrong" way to budget in Lunch Money, and you get to set it up in the way that works for you. We give you the tools, and you decide how to use them! We recommend going through the complete Budgeting Guide to configure your budget period, manage your income and rollover options, and familiarize yourself with all the features.

[arrow-rightGo to Budgeting Guide](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-1-intro-to-budgeting)

Once you have the budget set up, you will be able to start analyzing your spending and control your savings!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-6-whats-next)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 6: What’s next?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#invite-your-partner)

**Invite your partner**

Do you share your expenses with a partner? Invite them to collaborate on your budget on Lunch Money! You can invite any number of collaborators from the [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page and they will have full access to your Lunch Money data while each having their own individual login.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdJ8oMmxCsMwyeIhr3_iwpCuuq357fIHPbrXqaQCCt_ZhnKCBVtmorDM8cOK2CwReKsw8rqqhS1I-r5Tf0ioG840O-ZHsVRhC58dMlnU3LqCTz6FE5Cx2oej0wTDCj9MfqGkS88mzUM5QvbrMndAG4793c%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa8e1931&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#analyze-your-spending)

**Analyze your spending**

Once your transactions are organized properly, you can view your spending breakdown and budget breakdown on the [Overviewarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/overview)
 page. To switch between the spending breakdown and budget breakdown, click on the little gear icon on the right side of the box and change the "show again" option:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdb1jxONM6cdJhz732wDtQIegFl5wIGEulLFRAjs-XNneRqeXrUGvbF5TmQEEagvPgBtMGOa0tQx7jNIdc3WrBXmQLOkrA58LrmH1ZEa1KA0WoIXtjf9bs-6XIZ7K58YT01pueYHwS4mTL59lph7D8mEMw%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52d99bab&sv=2)

You can also get quick insights from the [Net Wortharrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/net-worth)
, [Statsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/stats)
 and [Trendsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/trends)
 pages.

For a more curated view of your data, you can head over to the [Analyzearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/analyze)
 page. The Query Tool will give you a detailed view of your income and expense data. You can also switch between the different graphs and charts and compare datasets. Understanding your spending habits and trends will help you figure out what your goals are, where you may need to cut down to save, or where you might have mis-organized transactions that need your attention.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#create-another-budget-account)

**Create another budget account**

In Lunch Money, you can create unlimited budget accounts per subscription. If you’d like to create a new budget to manage separately from your first budget, you can certainly do so!

To set up a new budget account, click on the circle next to the "Logout" button to open the 'Switch Accounts' menu. Then, click on "Create new budget account":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcNEglTiruOnmGaCDf5bdQfARdKjetW2SuDPTYFD5l3C8LRY6E3ok0uGnBGylq1RR5opOIszdZDaeh13WbLzMkJV_fsb5XPb6H9M1g3yIdAsCos7TjHDYdwMrgY0KunNs_zwMEp3dwjjlHwNSo_nIYqsAUk%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bdde9e4&sv=2)

You will then enter a budget account name, and can toggle whether you’d like to copy the categories and tags from the current budget or not. To confirm, click on "Create new budget".

You will then be presented with the onboarding menu ([see Step 1](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-1-getting-started)
) and can choose between starting fresh, setting up a demo, importing your data from CSV, or starting with a blank slate.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-7-getting-help)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjkyGoHm4vS0vQt3UXvy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5e7d31-17c9-4f04-86d2-908897977590&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed80e959&sv=2) Step 7: Getting help


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you run into any questions, would like to share feedback, or report an issue that you are experiencing, you can use the in-app support menu located at the top of the page anywhere within Lunch Money:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcvVHfxvuXRFm1eqoipyECfSN_M94rGjznqK1jMKGe4m-8W7YunHl41wci2KVcllR8OTx_eTGgXREwCrKYwIqgxF5bHJco-tPl7N2BoiyWTorX5-qovZgYzdmn3NpSlyVTg7okZtvLtW-5RnUvd_rjt1b6S%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12c427b6&sv=2)

You will then see the following menu options:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeWJi8nKIqvY0YPeXO3H2OA6ixaVieaFZKF5sSZE5MM8eUgZ8F2Z-wtfLwwqaoepmNZ59hSo1wo0OG3SQB-DwuYKkEtJ8wqEqCHXtMknVg17pxAI53nVOgfW9ju9IiK7G4yFEr55gPllCThzFBQT_hkD4z-%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a23f0e12&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#submit-a-bug-or-feedback)

Submit a bug or feedback

Select "**Submit a bug or feedback"** to report an issue or to share feedback for specific Lunch Money features.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfMjx9hbZApKQCYk-zxucDOWgkrm2Mjr4vm9_DUaw4kFyv5cdNrfz4wp0rZSFgSUxUGvLraAiQmVmIwWYoHcMcjWFnTdHPQOO2jX8InzhnC5PjJQuk9zCx2NlSlgRqtsgEe6FsfytPbK4_xOydDV8xh2btS%3Fkey%3DsTMs6N4OfsM4fUgod3Ua5g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aec06fa&sv=2)

# Migrating to Budgeting v2 🆕 | Knowledge Base

After months of feedback, testing, and refinement, we’re excited to share that the new Lunch Money budgeting feature is officially here! 🎉

The new budgeting system brings powerful flexibility while maintaining the simplicity you love. Here's a quick overview of what's new and what's changed:

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#whats-new)

**What's new**

*   🗓️ [**Custom budgeting periods**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#how-do-i-configure-my-custom-budgeting-period)
    : Break free from monthly budgets! Set cycles that match your life, whether that's weekly, bi-weekly, or the 1st and 15th of each month.
    
*   🛼 [**Smart rollover options**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#defining-rollover-options)
    : Take control of what happens to extra funds or overspending in each category.
    
*   📥 [**General pool**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#rollover-options-for-the-general-pool-income)
    : All income now flows to one central pool that you distribute to your categories, making it easier to see and manage your total available funds.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#whats-changed)

**What's changed**

*   📋 [**Streamlined interface**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#historical-spend)
    : Historical spending data (last 3 periods) now appears on hover over the Activity number, keeping your budget view clean and focused.
    
*   ⭐ [**"Budget suggestions" are now "budget presets"**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budget-presets)
    : Same helpful functionality, clearer name. Your existing suggestions will transfer automatically.
    
*   🗃️ [**Category group budgeting**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#enabling-category-group-budgeting)
    : Set budgets and rollover options at the category group level.
    

circle-check

**Automatic Migration:** Your existing budgets and most settings are automatically migrated, but category group budgets and income rollovers may need a quick manual update. Please review the migration information below to ensure a smooth transition.

* * *

If you were a beta tester and previously tried the new budgeting feature, please review the information below to ensure a smooth transition for your category group budgets and income rollovers settings:

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#category-group-budgeting)

1️⃣ Category Group Budgeting

If you had category-group level budgets in v1 that weren't carried over to v2, you'll need to manually enable category group budgeting for those category groups.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#how-to-enable-category-group-budgeting)

**How to Enable Category Group Budgeting**

1.  Navigate to the [Budgetarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/budget)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FF2hpwa2Xsyb1m7Vbh0EH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0090dc4-679d-492c-8ffe-f74ce8561949&width=37&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39f1d421&sv=2)) on the far-right of the category group row
    
3.  In the right-side panel, toggle on "**Enable Category Group Budgeting**":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FARSJ2pDAZad8M62hpJEO%252F61db3c83e657ff2800c705127ce04b16.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e65155c-d316-427f-885c-4b3491d15ae1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1f412c3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#when-category-group-budgeting-is-disabled)

**When category group budgeting is disabled:**

*   Budgets and rollover options can only be set at the subcategory level
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#when-category-group-budgeting-is-enabled)

**When category group budgeting is enabled:**

*   You can set budgets at both the category group level AND the subcategory level
    
*   Rollover options are only available at the category group level
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#income-rollover-options)

2️⃣ Income Rollover Options

In Budgeting v2, all income flows towards the general pool by default. If you previously had individual rollover options configured for individual income categories, you'll need to enable general pool rollover settings to maintain similar functionality.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#how-to-enable-income-rollover)

How to Enable Income Rollover

1.  Navigate to the [Budgetarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/budget)
     page and click on ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2)
    
2.  Under "General Pool Rollover Setting", toggle on "**Roll over 'Left to Budget' and 'Overbudgeted' amounts**":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FQbEJWnVeeBViWM4mAKNo%252F164cae531b9ceac88c6e5afa2919814b.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da5feb174-1018-4d13-adaa-8bb2f8a6ea5e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=286195b2&sv=2)

After enabling the rollover options, you'll need to configure:

1.  **Reset Balance To:** Set your desired starting balance (e.g., 0)
    
2.  **Starting On:** Choose your rollover start date (e.g., 2025-7-1)
    

Once configured, click "**Start rolling over**" to activate the feature.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F8P0qI5ki6utzgVF1SNRA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1245acbc-f284-49f7-b5e6-255daab94080&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff8939c0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#understanding-the-change)

Understanding the Change

*   **Before (v1):** Individual rollover options for each income category
    
*   **Now (v2):** A single rollover setting for the general pool, which includes all income
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2#have-any-questions)

You can also click on "**Help**" at the top of the page next to the logout button, and send an in-app ticket with the "**Submit a bug or feedback**" option.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FOsr34EhNH8yQLElexrww%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93cc5646-e2aa-40ec-ab95-e82173275b98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e21e1f56&sv=2)

# Reference/Glossary | Knowledge Base

Term

Definition

Budget page

Where you budget within the Lunch Money app, accessible via the navigation bar under “Finances”.

Budget Settings

The configuration pop-up where you set up core budgeting options like your budget period, income settings, general pool rollovers, and other preferences. Access it from the top right of the Budget page.

General Pool

Your total money available to budget. Includes current period's income, and rollovers from previous periods ([if you have rollovers enabledarrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#defining-rollover-options)
).

Budgeting period

The time frame for your budget (usually monthly). All income and expenses reset at the end of each period.

Income Settings

Options that control how your budgetable income is calculated: using budgeted amounts (Expected), actual income received, or the larger of the two.

Income category

Categories for money coming in (salary, freelance income, etc.). All income flows into your general pool.

Expense category

Categories for spending (Rent, Groceries, etc.). You assign budgeted amounts to these each period.

Budgeted (amount)

The amount you plan to spend in a category this period.

Activity

What you actually spent (or received) so far this period.

Available

The balance in a category showing how much you can still spend. Includes your budgeted amount, minus what you've spent (activity), plus any rollovers.

Expected

Income you anticipate receiving this period (shown in income categories).

Available to Budget

The total money in your general pool ready to be assigned to categories. Includes income, rollovers, and adjustments minus what you've already budgeted.

Left to Budget

The amount in your general pool that hasn't been assigned to categories yet. Shows as positive (green) when you have money to assign.

Overbudgeted

When you've assigned more money to categories than you have available. Shows as negative (red) in your Left to Budget amount.

Net Total Available

The sum of all Available amounts across your categories plus any unbudgeted money. Represents the minimum liquid cash you need to cover your entire budget. For zero-based budgeters, this should match your actual bank balances.

Rollover

A feature that carries Available balances between periods - whether positive (savings) or negative (overspending).

Rollover option

The setting for each category that controls how Available balances are handled at period end: do nothing, rollover to same category, or rollover to general pool.

Balance adjustment

A way to manually set new Available balances for categories or your general pool, starting from a specific date. Useful for corrections or fresh starts.

Budget presets

Settings that automatically fill in budget amounts each period based on your chosen method (fixed amount, previous spending, etc.).

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

---

# Step 5: Miscellaneous Features | Knowledge Base

circle-check

You're on Step 5 of Lunch Money's Budgeting Guide!

**Jump to:**

*   [**Historical Spend**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#historical-spend)
    
*   [**Settings View**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#settings-view)
    
*   [**Hide categories with no activity and no budget**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#hide-categories-with-no-activity-and-no-budget)
    
*   [**Budget Notes**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#budget-notes)
    
*   [**Budget Breakdown (Overview page)**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#budget-breakdown-overview-page)
    
*   [**Monthly Summary (Transactions Page)**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#monthly-summary-transactions-page)
    

* * *

Congratulations! You've learned the fundamentals of budgeting in Lunch Money - from [setting up your budget periods](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#setting-your-budgeting-period)
 and categories to [managing rollovers](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#defining-rollover-options)
 and [making adjustments](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#available-balance-adjustments)
.

As you continue your budgeting journey, you might find these additional features helpful. They're not essential for getting started, but they can make your budgeting experience even smoother and more tailored to your needs.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#historical-spend)

Historical Spend


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Want to see your spending patterns? The Activity column gives you two ways to dive into your transaction history:

*   **Quick view**: Click the magnifying glass icon to see all transactions for the current period.
    
    ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdlSrOsNAQya9zVCA2pw9r5NimOqLC_Qw63XbxyRHkiV1GuCeQFiMJnXbrL4q_3WIuczM-wQRsNhtrlVbysOERzfweFPENiyaP43UbKfP6TeTPHZmlHxby65geM5JshOXB94nLq%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14942510&sv=2)
    

*   **Historical trends**: Hover over the Activity amount to see the 'Historical Activity' tooltip. This shows:
    
    *   Past spending for this category
        
    *   Percentage changes between periods
        
    *   Quick access to historical period's transactions (click the magnifying glass)
        
        ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdbPTXx2JhOk33Xvae8bzEg2lc9VYkAFN-ojR-I6y-71EiUKcfaSU3WlIUozIm97D6brvxRw3yM99y8kAfTMTVHkyvzKn9PvGrB7amBKk5Z5CT04Hf6eaQ2c_t9_Qu4DBhzeN0b%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe2cfc9b&sv=2)
        
    

Use these trends to make smarter budgeting decisions - if you spent $290 on food last period but only $150 the period before, you'll know what's realistic for your current budget.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#settings-view)

Settings View


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Need a quick overview of all your budget settings? Switch to Settings View to see your budget presets and rollover configurations at a glance - no need to check each category individually.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf_sLD22GLhaverQGwqm9pR79fv2AM-y6Hw6D2_tTYdnyYGi3m8AxIorSqtUriUC1glndH-jB3u4LjvKdVe9gxVpKjG2Ta0zsbBspM-YicJSMFrFBQ9j6t1Pu9OI6wzhBpKn6YIgA%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6061e827&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#hide-categories-with-no-activity-and-no-budget)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FuFM1xw0KGoAGM8I27VUF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3e5e2f9-d3ec-4ee8-bfe3-bf8c465f8fac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33cdb4dc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#budget-notes)

Budget Notes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Notes can be added at the category level each period, to add additional context and personal reminders for your budgets. Whether it's explaining a one-off expense, tracking seasonal patterns, or clarifying adjustments, this makes it easier to understand past budgets, plan smarter for the future, and stay aligned when collaborating with others.

You will find the Notes field on the right-side panel when editing categories on the Budget page:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F42NYWX30w14S10EGIQf4%252F8b83df91d5cba1e15bd4ccb707e5fe6c.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85cfffa9-3fc9-4699-90a2-b1e8f0fc5fa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=733c9b5a&sv=2)

Once you add a note, you can view it by hovering on the note icon next to the category name:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FpIS9ICZ93kZECvtyUQ4N%252Fbudget%2520notes.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60383c12-d6c6-4254-8aac-92ab5df7a2a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fc6b87c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#budget-breakdown-overview-page)

Budget Breakdown (Overview page)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Want to see where every dollar goes? The Budget Breakdown on the Overview page shows your spending across all categories in a visual format. Click the cog icon (top right, above the income bar) to customize what you see:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcf3Xh5ZxeaghbMyvZrR5jhMQhQs3lcz-zOCkw7fB2o2r_jo9u1SZXygzfONbHugoaaIjTpLV1Ob80BgVMRcukAYW9Gy5zzElCtZ8neLW2n17_AxTnw8H4rqWo_O03QyQLVOqeX3A%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9a58228&sv=2)

Monthly Summary (Transactions Page)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Track your budget progress at a glance! The Monthly Summary on the Transactions page shows how much of your budget you've used with progress bars and percentages for each category.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FIrNhRC1DJvikLQtGps1u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5943de9b-a5b2-4727-824f-6242aded2e2a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1d9f8b3&sv=2)

Green means you're under budget, red means you're over. The percentages show exactly how much you've spent compared to what you budgeted.

# Handling Syncing Issues | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [How does bank syncing work?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-does-bank-syncing-work)
    
*   [How do I know I have the latest data available from Plaid?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-know-i-have-the-latest-data-available-from-plaid)
    
*   [How can I check the connection status of institution?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-can-i-check-the-connection-status-of-an-institution)
    
*   [How does Lunch Money handle bank syncing issues?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-does-lunch-money-handle-bank-syncing-issues)
    
*   [How do I create a bank syncing support ticket?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-create-a-bank-syncing-support-ticket)
    
*   [How do I safely disconnect and reconnect my bank connection?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-safely-disconnect-and-reconnect-my-bank-connection)
    
*   [Can I manually import transactions in the meantime?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#can-i-manually-import-transactions-in-the-meantime)
    
*   [How do I open an in-app bank syncing support ticket?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-open-an-in-app-bank-syncing-support-ticket)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-does-bank-syncing-work)

How does bank syncing work?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before we get into troubleshooting syncing issues, it's important to understand exactly how bank syncing in Lunch Money works.

We use a third-party service called Plaid to retrieve bank data from numerous institutions. Plaid can be thought of as the middleman, taking data from institutions in various countries and normalizing the data to a common format. From there, Plaid shares this cleaned-up data with Lunch Money and other personal financial apps.

At times, Plaid works directly with the institution and is able to integrate with them directly. At other times, Plaid employs other methods to retrieve your data without a working relationship with the institution.

**In all cases, Plaid receives data from the institution, and passes it down to Lunch Money.** Being downstream from this process, Lunch Money has very little control or means to fix syncing issues. Such issues can arise from (but not limited to):

*   a broken connection between Plaid and your bank, perhaps from a back-end update made by your bank
    
*   limitations imposed by your bank
    
*   issues or downtime experienced by Plaid
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-know-i-have-the-latest-data-available-from-plaid)

How do I know I have the latest data available from Plaid?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Look for the following timestamps under 'Status':

1.  Lunch Money's last successful import - This is the last time we were able to successfully import new data into your Lunch Money account from Plaid.
    
2.  Plaid's last successful fetch - This is the last time Plaid is reporting they received latest updates from your bank.
    
3.  Lunch Money's last successful fetch - This is the last time Lunch Money received latest updates from Plaid.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FD2onlyzcmFW8UYBrpMzv%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202024-02-02%2520at%252010.39.28%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b59eac4-3003-4476-85b6-80967bba44ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c1bee18&sv=2)

Hitting the **Trigger Refresh for this Account** button basically resets the last successful fetch timestamp of 19 hours ago to just a few seconds ago. This lets you know that our systems are operational and getting the latest from Plaid, but Plaid doesn't have the latest from your bank.

We don't have a way to tell Plaid to go to your bank since that's dictated by however their integration is done. Being downstream from this syncing process means all we can do is report problems upstream. This is why we tell users to create bank syncing support tickets, since the more of these we open for a particular problem, the more that Plaid will notice user impact and prioritize accordingly!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-can-i-check-the-connection-status-of-an-institution)

How can I check the connection status of an institution?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can easily check the connection status of any institution in our app by using the **/status** command on Discord. To join the Discord server, [click herearrow-up-right](http://lunchmoney.app/discord)
.

The **/status** command will call up our faithful Lenny to show you how many successful or relinked connections have occurred with that institution in the last 30 days. This can help you determine whether an issue you are experiencing is specific to your account or if it’s a more widespread problem.

This can also give you an idea of which institutions are currently supported within Lunch Money.

To try it out, head over to [Discord arrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/discord)
and type **/status** + **institution name** in the message bar anywhere on discord (eg. in the "General" channel):

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fix961DuaInHERrLoMq40%252Fabb51cb137ab395d45c1a88bedf53b33.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0c15ecd-ceea-4e89-9825-aba69eeca4fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf90fb73&sv=2)

circle-info

If another institution with a similar name exists, and you end up receiving the status for a different institution than intended, check the small text at the bottom. Sometimes Lenny will suggest other similar institutions and their institution numbers, eg. "TD Canada Trust - WebBroker (ins\_133003)". You can then repeat the /status command with the specific institution number, eg. "/status ins\_133003"

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-does-lunch-money-handle-bank-syncing-issues)

How does Lunch Money handle bank syncing issues?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unfortunately, the only thing we can do, being downstream from this process between your bank and Plaid, is bringing up syncing issues to Plaid to aid them in prioritizing issues based on user impact.

When you create a bank syncing support ticket, we relay the same information to Plaid. While an immediate or even short-term solution may not always be available, it's important to make your voice heard that this is an issue that is affecting you.

Our awesome customer support reps will reach out directly to Plaid on your behalf and keep you posted whenever Plaid responds.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-create-a-bank-syncing-support-ticket)

How do I create a bank syncing support ticket?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have already connected the account in question:

1.  Go to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page and click on the account in question
    
2.  Scroll down to where it says "I need help with this account"
    

If you have not been able to connect the account in question:

1.  Create a general bank syncing support ticket by clicking on 'Help' at the top right corner of the app
    
2.  Select 'Open bank syncing support ticket'
    
3.  Choose 'I am having trouble with a new connection'.
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-safely-disconnect-and-reconnect-my-bank-connection)

How do I safely disconnect and reconnect my bank connection?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We sometimes find that a new bank connection can get fresh data while an existing data stays stuck. You may find it helpful to attempt to create a new connection to your bank. Here's how we recommend doing it:

1.  Note the date of the last transaction that was imported from your current connection. This will come in handy later on to prevent duplicates.
    
2.  Go to the Accounts page and click on 'Add Account' and select 'Auto-import from my bank'.
    
3.  Follow the instructions to link to your bank.
    
4.  When prompted, deselect 'Import all historical transactions' and input the date from Step 1. to prevent importing duplicate transactions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#did-you-get-new-transactions)

Did you get new transactions?

**If so, congratulations!** You can now merge together your old connection to your new one. To do so, you first need to convert your old connection to be a manually-managed account as opposed to a synced account.

1.  Select any account within the old connection from the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page.
    
2.  Scroll down to select 'Remove or troubleshoot this account'
    
3.  Select the option to convert to a manually-managed account and keep all data.
    

Once the manually-managed account is created, you can then merge it with the synced account. Note that your connection may have yielded multiple accounts, like 2 credit cards and 1 savings account. At this stage, you will be matching them 1-to-1 with the newly created manually-managed accounts.

1.  Select a newly-created manually-managed account.
    
2.  Scroll down and select 'Merge with synced account'.
    

This will now merge your transactions from the previous transaction, which were moved to a manually-managed account, into your newly-created synced account.

**If you didn't get new transactions,** you should delete the newer connection and [create a bank syncing ticket](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-create-a-bank-syncing-support-ticket)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#can-i-manually-import-transactions-in-the-meantime)

Can I manually import transactions in the meantime?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your synced bank account has an active connection but new transactions stopped syncing, it is best to [create a bank syncing ticket](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-create-a-bank-syncing-support-ticket)
 first to understand the cause of the issue. If you are waiting on a resolution or update from Plaid and wish to manually import new transactions in the meantime, you can follow the steps below:

1.  [Download a CSV file](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#how-do-i-download-my-transactions)
     with the missing transactions from your bank (eg. bank statement).
    
2.  On the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page, click into the account to open the '_Edit Account_' panel, and under '_Advanced Settings_', set the '**Earliest import date**' to that of the last transaction in the file (this is to prevent duplicate transactions when automatic syncing resumes). Also under 'Advanced Settings', enable "**Allow modifications to transactions**".
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FrFNhsqLhDUhYTTEa8Eeo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D278390ea-e890-48ad-93c7-77b2acf2338e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2a7f6bc&sv=2)

1.  Go to the [Transactions arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
    page, and click on "Import" (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FSWwqvrYFLpyzyhkPbNRI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dede69e8d-f4f4-4c37-b33a-dcee2b48e6b8&width=130&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8db1cab&sv=2)), and then choose "Upload a new CSV". Select the relevant synced bank account from the dropdown menu, click to choose the file from your computer, and click on "Upload" to go through the CSV upload process.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FVSOEJ6D1zOc92eq01sgO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01a61668-526a-42b4-b3ef-c715aac3dc03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa7afd8c&sv=2)

For a complete step-by-step guide of the CSV upload process, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-1-upload-csv)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#how-do-i-open-an-in-app-bank-syncing-support-ticket)

How do I open an in-app bank syncing support ticket?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For bank syncing issues, we highly recommend [creating a bank syncing support ticket directly in the apparrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
. This helps us quickly gather all the details we need to know in order to investigate the issue.

[Open a new bank syncing support ticket ➜](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#if-you-have-already-connected-the-account-in-question)

**If you have already connected the account in question:**

1.  Go to the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
    
2.  Click on the account in question to open the 'Edit Account' panel
    
3.  Scroll down and click on 'I need help with this account':
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FKden2Jd14wTWCL0Wpdzp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83cc6176-de36-40d6-9ab6-84555124441c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=371674fe&sv=2)

1.  Select the relevant issue and fill in the requested information to submit the ticket:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Ffruupc9ngcJmC05tr77T%252F6a54191a51bf54ca64742e8a4a8e10c7.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63c04731-d0ef-4a45-a596-eca651491e43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=471d5730&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#if-you-have-not-been-able-to-connect-the-account-in-question)

If you have not been able to connect the account in question:

1.  Create a general bank syncing support ticket by clicking on 'Help' at the top right corner of the app:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F69qTC1Eg53GU6sgqRuZZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0a9beb4-3dcc-4d42-8a65-58f189c090b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c77f9a&sv=2)

1.  Select 'Open bank syncing support ticket'
    
2.  Choose 'I am having trouble with a new connection'
    
3.  Select the associated recent connection attempt from the listed options
    

circle-info

If the recent connection attempt doesn't appear in the list, please attempt creating the connection again before submitting the ticket. Still having trouble? Please open the ticket using the 'Submit a bug or feedback' option instead.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FazRKHIom1Qs0L1ek123x%252F2130e0b7e0301c0639c643a2056db6ff.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De98ce344-980e-4449-9b51-be5f0c623899&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=994b1dbe&sv=2)

Once you've submitted the ticket, our awesome customer support reps will reach out directly to Plaid on your behalf and get in touch with you from there! 🙂
