# Migrating from Mint | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Before you start**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#before-you-start)
    
*   [**Step 1: Export your existing transactions from Mint**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-1-export-your-existing-transactions-from-mint)
    
*   [**Step 2: Ready your account for migration**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-2-ready-your-account-for-migration)
    
*   [**Step 3: Go through the Mint migration tool**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-3-go-through-the-mint-migration-tool)
    
*   [**F**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#faqs)
    [**AQs**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#faqs)
    
    *   [I've imported my historical transactions. How do I get my accounts to sync now?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-imported-my-historical-transactions.-how-do-i-get-my-accounts-to-sync-now)
        
    *   [I've created new categories. What should I do to ensure compatibility within Lunch Money?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-created-new-categories.-what-should-i-do-to-ensure-compatibility-within-lunch-money)
        
    *   [I'm having trouble, where can I get support?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#im-having-trouble-where-can-i-get-support)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#before-you-start)

Before you start


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide will take you through the steps to get your Mint data imported into Lunch Money. If you are an existing Lunch Money user, you have a few options to consider:

chevron-rightOption 1: Create a new budget to test the Mint migration tool[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#option-1-create-a-new-budget-to-test-the-mint-migration-tool)

Hesitant to import it your Mint data to your existing Lunch Money budget account? No worries! You can test out the migration tool separately from your existing data first, with a new budget account!

In Lunch Money, you may create unlimited budgeting accounts per subscription. Click on the circle next to the "Logout" button to open the 'Switch Accounts' menu, and then click on "Create new budget account". After creating a new budget, select '_Import my data from Mint_' and then continue to follow [step #3 of this article](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-3-go-through-the-mint-migration-tool)
.

chevron-rightOption 2: Import the Mint data directly into an existing synced account[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#option-2-import-the-mint-data-directly-into-an-existing-synced-account)

Have you already started syncing a bank account within Lunch Money, for which you have historical transactions from Mint? You can import your historical transactions directly into a synced account for a complete view of your finances!

First, you'll need to enable the option to "Allow modifications to synced accounts" on your synced account. Go to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page, click into the account in question to open the '_Edit Account_' panel, and under '_Advanced Settings_', enable "Allow modifications to transactions":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FdPlS0FSfcUNP5d74HRN2%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202023-11-11%2520at%25203.04.09%2520PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39a83bb7-4007-40d6-a48c-f2404bfb38d9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28312eb9&sv=2)

Next, you can jump to Step 2 of this article to go through the process of importing your transaction data and when you reach the "Review Accounts" stage, assign the transactions to the relevant existing synced account.

Keep in mind that depending on the banking institution, you may already have historical transactions synced for as far back as two years. In that case, it's recommended to revise the CSV file before uploading to remove transactions beyond that date, to prevent duplicates.

If you've already imported your historical transactions via CSV and now wish to set-up account syncing to automatically import new transactions, click the link below:

[👉 **I've imported my historical transactions. How do I get my accounts to sync now?**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-imported-my-historical-transactions.-how-do-i-get-my-accounts-to-sync-now)

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-1-export-your-existing-transactions-from-mint)

Step 1: Export your existing transactions from Mint


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get started, you'll need a CSV (comma-separated value) file of your historical transactions from Mint. As Mint only supported exporting up to 10,000 rows at a time, if you have more than 1 CSV file, you can repeat the import process as necessary.

circle-info

As of mid-2024, Intuit no longer supports exporting Mint transaction data to CSV.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-2-ready-your-account-for-migration)

Step 2: Ready your account for migration


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you haven't signed up for a Lunch Money account yet, now is the time to do so! [You can register herearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/register)
. After registration, you will be prompted to import your data from Mint:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F6cuImtIJ2orS6TcLBLhq%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202023-11-10%2520at%25205.32.53%2520PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a43a19e-af9a-46dc-9852-f13ca8d55525&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=839fb78e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-3-go-through-the-mint-migration-tool)

Step 3: Go through the Mint migration tool


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Mint migration tool is part of the CSV importing tool. You can get there by [clicking on this linkarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/import)
, or by going to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
 page and clicking on the import icon:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fl4e3Y83uS5EpbuLvSMXY%252FMint%2520-%2520Import%2520CSV.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9662e9a2-623d-4f07-893d-2c87ff8cd032&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e1c4473&sv=2)

In general, importing a CSV will consist of the following steps:

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-a-upload-a-file)

**Step A: Upload a file**

To use the Mint migration tool, select '_Migrate from Mint_'.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FsbYc4Ft7LKCuCKMLtTWT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df59241d3-d3dd-4369-90fd-157fa5d1d026&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95ebb509&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-b-assign-columns)

**Step B: Assign columns**

This is where you map the columns of your CSV data to the relevant columns within Lunch Money. For the Mint migration tool, we do this automatically for you and this step is skipped. If you would like to view the columns assigned, you can click 'Back' from the Review Settings step.

The Mint migration tool will import all the columns exported from Mint, which include:

*   Date
    
*   Description (known as 'payee' in Lunch Money)
    
*   Original description (known as 'original name' in Lunch Money)
    
*   Amount
    
*   Amount Type
    
*   Account
    
*   Category
    
*   Notes
    
*   Labels (known as 'tags' in Lunch Money)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-c-review-settings)

**Step C: Review settings**

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#review-notations)

**Review Notations**

As a quick confidence check, double-check to ensure that the date formats and transaction amount notations are correct. This involves ensuring no dates are being converted into "Invalid Date"s, and that debits and credits are properly assigned.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#review-categories)

**Review Categories**

This step will display the list of categories that have been detected within your CSV file. If you have existing categories that match, the tool will map them accordingly. If not, you have the option to:

*   create a new category with a different name
    
*   assign to an existing category
    
*   leave blank to create a category of the same name
    
*   leave uncategorized
    

circle-exclamation

If you're creating new categories, you'll want to do some additional set-up to ensure a smooth transition to Lunch Money. Please see the following FAQ at the end of this article: [I've created new categories. What should I do to ensure compatibility within Lunch Money?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-created-new-categories-via-the-tool.-what-should-i-do-to-ensure-compatibility-within-lunch-money)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#review-tags)

**Review Tags**

Similar to reviewing categories, this step will display the list of tags that have been detected within your CSV file, If you have existing tags that match, the tool will map them accordingly. If not, you have the option to:

*   create a new tag with a different name
    
*   assign to an existing tag
    
*   leave blank to create a tag of the same name
    
*   leave untagged
    

circle-exclamation

**Important note regarding exporting labels from Mint**

When exporting files from Mint, please note that tags are separated by spaces. However, Mint also permits spaces within individual tags, which can complicate accurate parsing of your data.

This CSV import tool assumes multiple tags are delimited by a comma (','). If your transactions involve multiple tags, we strongly advise using a tool like [Google Sheetsarrow-up-right](https://sheets.new/)
 to manually insert commas between each tag to ensure accurate data interpretation in Lunch Money.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#review-accounts)

**Review Accounts**

Similar to reviewing categories and tags, this step will display the list of accounts that have been detected within your CSV file. You have the option to:

*   assign to an existing account
    
    *   Note that if you want to assign this to a synced account, you'll need to ensure the 'Allow modifications to transactions' setting is enabled for that account from the Accounts page)
        
    
*   create a new account
    
    *   We recommend this option. Just set the account type and you're good to go! You can modify accounts and add more information later from the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
         page.
        
    
*   leave blank to assign transactions to the default 'Cash' account
    
    *   This is the fastest option but we don't recommend it as there will be no way to differentiate your transactions between accounts.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#final-settings)

**Final Settings**

The final step will display the malformed lines in your CSV that will not be imported. This will typically include the first line, which is the header.

You also have the option to run these transactions through our Rules engine, if you have any set up, and to de-duplicate as needed.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-d-review-transactions)

**Step D: Review Transactions**

This step will display the transactions exactly as they will appear within Lunch Money once the import process is finished. Ensure that the data is correct. You also have the option to deselect any transactions if you want to exclude them from the import.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#step-e-insert-transactions)

**Step E: Insert Transactions**

If you have over 500 transactions to import, this will be done through a background job and the system will email you within just a few minutes when that's finished. Otherwise, you can go straight to your transactions!

If you are not importing into a synced account, you will also have the option here to review and update your account balances if necessary. You may also skip this step and update the balance anytime from the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page.

**Congratulations! You've imported your historical data from Mint to Lunch Money! 🎉**

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#faqs)

FAQs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-imported-my-historical-transactions.-how-do-i-get-my-accounts-to-sync-now)

I've imported my historical transactions. How do I get my accounts to sync now?

If you created accounts as part of the Mint migration or CSV import process, you will now see these accounts on the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page. These created accounts are all manually-managed accounts and are not synced.

To start syncing for these accounts, you'll need to set up syncing with your banking institution. On the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page, click on "Add account", and then click on "Auto-import from my bank" in the right-side panel. Go through the Plaid flow to authenticate with your bank.

Once you've gone through the process, you'll reach the 'Setup Account' step. In this dialog, make sure to choose "_Yes, I am merging this with an existing account_":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F2NaVyjbNWAlmUPBr6nxK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03f24f2f-f04c-4103-b68c-0871c6153f18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19d20209&sv=2)

The system will automatically detect the date of the last transaction in the manually-managed account and only transactions on that date and onwards will be synced.

circle-exclamation

As the auto-sync is inclusive of the date of the last transaction, it may result in duplicates for that specific date. Make sure to check the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
 page to review the newly auto-imported transactions for that specific day.

In the case where you have some transactions that were mis-dated or in the future, you can always update the **earliest import date** for the synced account via the '_Edit Account_' panel on the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FoqJngxiv3qnUF7Knt6SJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D480e4bfd-7ca2-41ea-b7c5-aceb44d951bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=508336e&sv=2)

By changing the earliest import date, you'll tell the system to automatically begin fetching transactions starting from that new date onwards.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#ive-created-new-categories.-what-should-i-do-to-ensure-compatibility-within-lunch-money)

I've created new categories. What should I do to ensure compatibility within Lunch Money?

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#set-category-properties)

Set category properties

In Lunch Money, new categories will generally be created as expense categories by default. To define a category as an **income** category, you will need to enable the "**Treat as income**" property for that category via the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
 page. You may also set other category properties, such as "**Exclude from totals**" and "**Exclude from budget**".

To learn more about category properties, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories#category-properties)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#set-up-autocategorization)

Set-up autocategorization

If you plan to sync transactions automatically from your bank, you'll want to ensure your [auto-categorizations](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization)
 are set up properly. This involves mapping your existing categories to Plaid's taxonomy.

Imported transactions include metadata from Plaid including their best-guess as to the category of the transaction. Within Lunch Money, we also have a rules engine where you can create more complex rules to categorize or otherwise modify these transactions. However, auto-categorization is an easy first step to avoid a slew of uncategorized transactions when you start syncing.

To set up auto-categorization, [click herearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories/auto)
 or follow the link from the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
 page. Note that the button link only appears if you have actively-syncing accounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/migrating-from-mint#im-having-trouble-where-can-i-get-support)

I'm having trouble, where can I get support?

If you need any assistance or have any questions, feel free to email us at [\[email protected\]](https://support.lunchmoney.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 or open an support ticket from the 'HELP' menu at the top right within the Lunch Money app! 😊

You can also [join our community Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/vSz6jjZuj8)
 to ask questions, share feedback, and interact with other Lunch Money users!

Last updated 1 year ago

Does Lunch Money have a mobile app?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes! While Lunch Money is primarily a [web-first experiencearrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/features/web-first)
, there is an official companion app that’s available for download on both iOS and Android:

[![Logo](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fapps.apple.com%2Fassets%2Ffavicon%2Ffavicon-180.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b2ed090&sv=2)Lunch Money App - App StoreApp Storechevron-right](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/lunch-money/id6739028463)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/faq#does-lunch-money-use-ai)

Does Lunch Money use AI?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We understand that AI brings excitement as well as valid privacy concerns. While Lunch Money does not currently offer AI-powered features, any such features that may be introduced in the future **will always be opt-in.** We will never share your data with AI systems without your explicit consent, and you will always be in full control of whether AI plays any role in your experience.

If you're interested in AI-powered tools to enhance your experience, you can explore some great community-built options here:

*   [Community Newsletter #11arrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2025-05-01-community-newsletter)
     : AI Meets Budgeting: Incredible Tools Built by Our Community
    
*   [Community Newsletter #16arrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2025-10-09-community-newsletter)
    : AI-Powered Financial Assistant: Lunch Money MCP Server
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/faq#how-do-i-delete-my-account)

How do I delete my account?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are a few ways to initiate the complete deletion of your account and all its data from our servers:

First, the quickest way to achieve this is to head over to the [Billing pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/billing)
 on the web app, and click on 'Cancel subscription & delete entire account' to go through the cancellation flow:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FauGHEbfRi2f5T0f23NsV%252Ffront_attachment.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D790b02fe-01c2-4de4-a8d8-27ed02d0a6df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7ba555e&sv=2)

Second, all accounts that are 5 days past their trial expiration dates which do not have any billing information associated, will automatically be purged.

Lastly, if you have trouble with the above two options, feel free to email us directly at [\[email protected\]](https://support.lunchmoney.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 and we'll delete your account within 48 hours.

Last updated 1 month ago

# Budgeting 🆕 | Knowledge Base

At Lunch Money, we don’t force you to use a specific budgeting method — instead, we provide all the different tools and flexibility you need to budget your way!

# Institution-specific Issues | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Canada**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#canada)
    
    *   🏦 [**CIBC**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#cibc-ca)
        
    *   🏦 [**Coast Capital Savings**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#coast-capital-savings)
        
    *   🏦 [**EQ Bank**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#eq-bank-ca)
        
    *   🏦 [**National Bank of Canada**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#national-bank-of-canada)
        
    *   🏦 [**President's Choice Financial**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#presidents-choice-financial)
        
    *   🏦 [**Tangerine**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#tangerine-ca)
        
    *   🏦 [**Wealthsimple**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#wealthsimple-ca)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#canada)

Canada


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Canadian bank connections are particularly prone to bank syncing issues today, as many of Canada’s major banks, including RBC, TD, Scotiabank, CIBC, Tangerine and others, are still operating on older authentication methods while awaiting final open banking and OAuth regulatory guidance.

Lunch Money was intentionally built to accommodate this by offering a dedicated support team to actively escalate sync issues and keep users informed, in addition to a reliable [CSV and PDF importer](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv)
 that allows you to effortlessly upload transactions and keep your budget clean and accurate. Our robust [Developer APIarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.dev/#getting-started)
 has also enabled expanded connectivity through solutions like [Lunch Flowarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/the-only-personal-finance-app-canadians-need)
, a third-party solution built by a Lunch Money user, that let’s you connect to even more institutions for automatic transaction syncing (via Plaid alternatives, such as MX), including:

*   [Canada Lifearrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/canada-life)
    
*   [EQ Bankarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/eq-bank)
    
*   [Questradearrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/questrade)
    
*   [Flinksarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/)
    
*   [MBNAarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/mbna-credit-cards-canada-)
    
*   [Canadian Tire Bankarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/canadian-tire-bank)
    
*   [Kohoarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/koho)
    
*   [Neo Financialarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/neo-financial-01d98d-)
    
*   [Rogers Bankarrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/rogers-bank-canada-)
    
*   [Tangerinearrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/tangerine-personal)
    
*   [Manulifearrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage/manulife)
    
*   And many more! [Check out the whole list herearrow-up-right](https://www.lunchflow.app/coverage)
    .
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#cibc-ca)

🏦 CIBC (CA)

**Latest update from Plaid (** **February 17, 2026):**

> **Known Issue KI123004: Invalidated MFA with CIBC & Simplii Financial**
> 
> An issue is occurring where Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA) will become invalidated shortly after the end-user’s initial Item creation. This issue is occurring with CIBC & Simplii Financial. This issue occurs with products that have background updates, such as transactions, investments, and liabilities and may impact new connections or background updates on existing items.
> 
> This issue will require collaboration with the financial institution or data partner to resolve. Plaid has reached out to them to move toward a resolution. Because this issue requires assistance from the financial institution, we do not have an estimated fix date.

circle-exclamation

Plaid highly prioritizes fixes based on user impact, so user reports are an integral part of the resolution process. If you are experiencing sync issues, please open an in-app bank syncing support ticket. You can do so by [**clicking here**arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
.

**What can I do in the meantime?**

1.  **Try reconnecting:** Often, creating a brand new connection and merging with the existing accounts works well to pull in new transaction imports. [You can follow the steps here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports#creating-a-new-connection-to-merge-with-an-existing-connection)
    .
    
2.  **Run a CSV/PDF import:** Lunch Money has a streamlined import feature so that you can bulk import transactions with a CSV or a PDF bank statement. [You can learn more here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#can-i-manually-import-transactions-in-the-meantime)
    .
    
3.  **Check out** [**Lunch Flow**arrow-up-right](https://lunchflow.app/)
     **(paid):** This is a third-party tool that supports CIBC through an integration with MX & Finicity (Plaid alternatives). It works with a "set it and forget it" system, so once you have your accounts set up in Lunch Flow, your transactions are automatically imported daily into Lunch Money! Lunch Flow has a cost, which is used to cover operation fees, but there's a discounted annual plan and a free trial available! To learn more, check out [this blog postarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2024-12-27-community-newsletter)
    .
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#coast-capital-savings)

🏦 Coast Capital Savings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Latest update from Plaid (** **February 3, 2026):**

> **Issue KI537252: Migration in progress for Coast Capital Savings (MyCardInfo Credit Card)**
> 
> Our team is currently migrating Coast Capital Savings (MyCardInfo Credit Card) to a new integration, which will address current issues. For this reason, our engineering team will not be fixing issues on the previous integration. Follow this known issue to be notified when the migration is completed.

circle-exclamation

Plaid highly prioritizes fixes based on user impact, so user reports are an integral part of the resolution process. If you are experiencing sync issues, please open an in-app bank syncing support ticket. You can do so by [**clicking here**arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
.

**What can I do in the meantime?**

1.  **Create a manually-managed account:** You can [create a manually managed account](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-add-manually-managed-assets-or-accounts)
     and use the CSV/PDF Import feature to quickly add your transactions in bulk. [You can learn more here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv)
    .
    
2.  **Check out** [**Lunch Flow**arrow-up-right](https://lunchflow.app/)
     **(paid):** This is a third-party tool that supports Coast Capital Savings through an integration with MX (Plaid alternative). It works with a "set it and forget it" system, so once you have your accounts set up in Lunch Flow, your transactions are automatically imported daily into Lunch Money! Lunch Flow has a cost, which is used to cover operation fees, but there's a discounted annual plan and a free trial available! To learn more, check out [this blog postarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2024-12-27-community-newsletter)
    .

🏦 National Bank of Canada

**Latest update from Plaid (** **February 18, 2026):**

> **Issue KI670897: Erroneous User Setup Required Errors for National Bank of Canada**
> 
> There is an issue occurring for some users when creating a new connection for National Bank of Canada. Users are told that action is required on their account, such as completing initial account setup or accepting new terms. However, this error is inaccurate, and no setup is actually necessary. This issue may impact new connections or background updates on existing items.
> 
> This issue will require collaboration with the financial institution or data partner to resolve. As of 2/18/26, this issue is affecting 20-40% of daily traffic to National Bank of Canada.

circle-exclamation

Plaid highly prioritizes fixes based on user impact, so user reports are an integral part of the resolution process. .

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#tangerine-ca)

🏦 Tangerine (CA)

There are definitely ongoing syncing issues between Tangerine and Plaid for some time now as many Tangerine users report. The general understanding is that Tangerine seems to send transaction updates once every 5 to 9 days, and a frequent relink (re-entering your one-time passcode) is required to get those updates.

Plaid is aware of the issue with Tangerine but no fix date has been issued.

**Latest update from Plaid (** **February 3, 2026):**

> **Issue KI122553: Invalidated MFA with Tangerine - Personal**
> 
> An issue is occurring where Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA) will become invalidated shortly after the end-user’s initial Item creation, causing background data updates to fail, resulting in missing or stale data. This issue is impacting Tangerine - Personal. This issue may impact new connections or background updates on existing items and any products that have background updates, such as transactions, investments, and liabilities.
> 
> This issue will require collaboration with the financial institution or data partner to resolve. Because this issue requires assistance from the financial institution, we do not have an estimated fix date.

circle-exclamation

Plaid highly prioritizes fixes based on user impact, so user reports are an integral part of the resolution process. If you are experiencing sync issues, please open an in-app bank syncing support ticket. You can do so by [**clicking here**arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
.

**What can I do in the meantime?**

1.  **Try reconnecting:** Often, creating a brand new connection and merging with the existing accounts works well to pull in new transaction imports. [You can follow the steps here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports#creating-a-new-connection-to-merge-with-an-existing-connection)
    .
    
2.  **Run a CSV/PDF import:** Lunch Money has a streamlined import feature so that you can bulk import transactions with a CSV or a PDF bank statement. [You can learn more here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#can-i-manually-import-transactions-in-the-meantime)
    .
    
3.  **Check out** [**Lunch Flow**arrow-up-right](https://lunchflow.app/)
     **(paid):** This is a third-party tool that supports Tangerine through an integration with MX & Finicity (Plaid alternatives). It works with a "set it and forget it" system, so once you have your accounts set up in Lunch Flow, your transactions are automatically imported daily into Lunch Money! Lunch Flow has a cost, which is used to cover operation fees, but there's a discounted annual plan and a free trial available! To learn more, check out [this blog postarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2024-12-27-community-newsletter)
    .
    

circle-info

**A Lunch Money user (shout out to Masha!) has shared this technique in our community Discord for getting Tangerine to sync. They write the following:**

I think I finally found a reliable way to force Tangerine to import transactions! Requires having 2 accounts. Ideally you don’t care much about the second one (in case something gets messed up). For me, the main one is Checking, and the burner one is Savings. From the Accounts screen:

1.  “Add or remove accounts from this bank.” - “Relink to Tangerine”.
    
2.  Click through Plaid screens with “Continue” and “Allow”.
    
3.  Enter one-time code.
    
4.  Uncheck Savings account.
    
5.  You will get a pop-up alert that Tangerine has lost the connection to the Savings account. Don’t close the window yet!
    
6.  From the same alert window, “Relink to Tangerine”.
    
7.  Click through Plaid’s Continue/Allow pages once again.
    
8.  Enter new one-time code.
    
9.  Make sure both accounts are checked.
    
10.  LM will detect a new account (Savings). Set earliest import date to today (or whenever it imported transactions last) and confirm you want to merge with an existing deactivated Savings account.
    
11.  This will trigger a pull for the latest transactions from Checking as well.
    

I believe this has to do with the fact that Tangerine will not release new transactions without entering a one-time code. It was the same way with Mint, refreshing the account prompted for a verification code. What does NOT work for transactions and at best updates the balance:

*   “Trigger refresh for this account” from the account’s screen.
    
*   “Refresh” button from the Transactions screen.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/institution-specific-issues#wealthsimple-ca)

🏦 Wealthsimple (CA)

**\[**✅ **Resolved\]** **Latest update from Plaid (** **February 16, 2026):**

> **Issue KI471864: Invalidated MFA with Wealthsimple (Canada)**
> 
> Our engineering team has completed adjustments and resolved the issue and we have verified that the underlying error is no longer occurring for new connections. It is now expected behavior for users to re-authenticate Wealthsimple Items every 30 days, but not persistently.
> 
> Please ask your user try connecting again via Link, or request they use Link update mode to repair any existing connections.

circle-exclamation

Plaid highly prioritizes fixes based on user impact, so user reports are an integral part of the resolution process. If you are experiencing sync issues, please open an in-app bank syncing support ticket. You can do so by [**clicking here**arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
.

**What can I do in the meantime?**

1.  **Try reconnecting:** Often, creating a brand new connection and merging with the existing accounts works well to pull in new transaction imports. [You can follow the steps here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports#creating-a-new-connection-to-merge-with-an-existing-connection)
    .
    
2.  **Run a CSV/PDF import:** Lunch Money has a streamlined import feature so that you can bulk import transactions with a CSV or a PDF bank statement. [You can learn more here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports/handling-syncing-issues#can-i-manually-import-transactions-in-the-meantime)
    .
    
3.  **Use a third-party tool:**
    
    1.  [**Lunchsimple**arrow-up-right](https://sr.ht/~colbyhub/lunchsimple/)
         **(free)**: This is a Python-run tool that lets users import their transaction data from Wealthsimple into Lunch Money. To learn more, check out [this blog postarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2025-02-28-community-newsletter)
        .
        
    2.  [**Sandwich Sync**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/vpnda/sandwich-sync)
         **(free):** This is a command-line tool for fetching transactions from Wealthsimple, which stores the transactions locally and then let's you sync them to LunchMoney.
        
    3.  [**Lunch Flow**arrow-up-right](https://lunchflow.app/)
         **(paid):** This is a third-party tool that supports Wealthsimple through an integration with MX & Finicity (Plaid alternatives). It works with a "set it and forget it" system, so once you have your accounts set up in Lunch Flow, your transactions are automatically imported daily into Lunch Money! Lunch Flow has a cost, which is used to cover operation fees, but there's a discounted annual plan and a free trial available! To learn more, check out [this blog postarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/2024-12-27-community-newsletter)
        .

# Step 3: Navigating the Budget Page | Knowledge Base

*   [**Sidebar: Budget Status Card**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-budget-status-card)
    
*   [**Sidebar: Action Buttons**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-action-buttons)
    
*   [**Sidebar: Budget Overview**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-budget-overview)
    
    *   [Understanding Net Total Available](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#understanding-net-total-available)
        
    

* * *

Now that you've got your budget all set up under the hood, it's time to explore the Budget page. This is where you'll get to see where your hard-earned money is going!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fhdubqm7jiiCWr7DCGAk0%252FNavigating%2520the%2520Budget%2520Page.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a596110-efa0-4ffc-95a2-fdaf6c4ae40c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ffa3dd6&sv=2)

Before we dive deeper, let’s get familiar with the layout. The Budget page can feel a bit overwhelming at first glance, so knowing what’s what will help you feel at home.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FEyEqsw5xWEbKtYSLuBbb%252Fbudget%2520page%2520elements.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ee89385-a9e3-463f-8d4d-53580798ceb1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f952e9d8&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#current-period-indicator)

Current Period Indicator


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At the top, you’ll see the time period you’re budgeting for. In the example above, we have set up our custom budgeting period to be every 2 weeks starting on September 1, 2024. You can navigate to future or previous periods using the arrows:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfSGlPDmVX3W3MBcCkLo16-r-vEQW5znzFKupgfiOa2HM1G-h_KQ6XgQOr5Agvh1DM3_OjFx_x6gGvEnNcIAYOvR6JatEstZZmS-SXvKTZaLCIupBRuGVuQmY3R5h9w1DrjUYak%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=283d1742&sv=2)

Remember that you can choose whatever period works best for you — monthly, bi-weekly, you name it!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#navigation-buttons)

Navigation buttons


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Underneath the Current Period Indicator, you’ll see the following buttons:

*   **Budget View vs. Setting View:** Located on the far left, this switch lets you flip between your actual budget and the summary of your category settings. This is helpful for quickly checking how you've set up each category without diving into all the details.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FUEE2qZ33bBoNIEAScsUb%252F9c127069f55a5e5347d1c7b5da3d988c.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8c0c5a1-be8e-469b-b63b-3cb31eaa5d3c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0c7366&sv=2)

*   **Feature Guide:** Provides a quick link to this guide!
    
*   **Budget Settings:** Located on the far right, this is where you can set your Budget Period (Monthly or Custom), enable the General Pool Rollover, [hide categories with no activity and no budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#hide-categories-with-no-activity-and-no-budget)
    , and choose what you will base your income on. You should already be familiar with this from [setting up your budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget)
    .
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#inflow-and-outflow-tables)

Inflow & Outflow Tables


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Budget View is made up of two sections:

*   **Inflow** (Income categories — shows all your money coming in)
    
*   **Outflow** (Expense categories — shows where your money is going)
    

Each table has rows for each budgetable category. For a cleaner view, you can choose to [hide categories that have no activity and no budgeted amount](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features#hide-categories-with-no-activity-and-no-budget)
. This is perfect for keeping things tidy if you have lots of categories.

circle-exclamation

Is your income category missing from the Inflow Table? Head over to the [Categories pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories/)
, and make sure that the 'Treat as income' category property is enabled, and that 'Exclude from budget' is disabled.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#what-each-column-means)

What each column means

In each category row in the Outflow table, you’ll find three important columns:

*   **Budgeted**: The amount you planned to spend for this period.
    
*   **Activity**: The amount you spent so far.
    
*   **Available**: The amount you still have left to spend. You can also think of this as the balance for your category. This number includes any rollovers, your budgeted amount, and your spending activity (transactions) to show you how much is safe to spend in the category for the rest of the budget period.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#rollover-breakdowns)

Rollover breakdowns

When you hover over any **Available** amount, you'll see exactly how it was calculated. This helps you understand where every dollar comes from.

**For expense categories with rollovers**: If a category is set to "rollover to same category", hovering shows:

*   Previous period's ending balance
    
*   Current period's activity
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf_CAEQS1cskUjhRbTLKYX_0H8WUZ1NB6OJbEzsaFki-f8i-3bP-cZIb53Ak9GIICeXPDGX8FwnIbbU33xaCcF4WOpcVsbVRZbCyDVXEFZ48_49ZUPuu8jsAXp57OQ6iWsmyezHAg%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d42644b&sv=2)

**For your general pool (in the Inflow section)**: The first line in your Inflow table shows your rollover pool. Hover over the number to see the breakdown:

*   Money rolled over from last period's general pool
    
*   Money from individual expense categories last period that rolled to general pool
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fwmtw9yKsTLbWCm8S35tR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19f5fb49-4a32-41c5-851d-f48b14c39ec9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcc48089&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-budget-status-card)

Sidebar: Budget Status Card


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At the top of the right-hand sidebar, you’ll see the Budget Status Card. Depending on your budget status, this card will either show:

Left to Budget

Balanced for this period!

Overbudgeted

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FHb1PPjceMv7mUJGUH6H2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b3d8af4-540f-4fe9-b275-b83b39a35712&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74dae88&sv=2)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FZgRUfHecXW5flZ5Bk3Uf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04420354-da61-4bfc-a9b9-3feb4d985119&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49fa8fc9&sv=2)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F9fzotwZQNS004QHrpczn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29f976ea-9bb4-4569-8d63-9b86fee5613e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34110c1&sv=2)

This is particularly useful if you are using a [zero-based budgetarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/zero-based-budgeting-simplified)
, and need to make sure every dollar is accounted for.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-action-buttons)

Sidebar: Action Buttons


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below that, you might see some Action Buttons, depending on your setup. These will make more sense when your budget is ready, but we’ve linked to them in case you want to read about them now:

*   [Budget Presets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budget-presets)
    
*   [Copy Budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#copy-budget)
    
*   [Clear This Period](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#clear-this-period)
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FpfPTLy4cdJVDGh0W2vTM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd38f1e9-6e50-4066-806b-6fd4ceca5e46&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67a4983b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#sidebar-budget-overview)

Sidebar: Budget Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the far right, you’ll see the Budget Overview. Think of this as a quick health check for your entire budget.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F3vyLWphIdrYtRB90ASoa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc48503c-fefc-4e6d-8d98-c2ad94933bad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cae9e2a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#heres-what-each-line-means)

**Here's what each line means:**

*   **Budgetable**: The total money you have to work with this period. This includes your income plus any money that rolled over from previous periods.
    
*   **Total Budgeted**: How much you've assigned to categories so far. This is the sum of all the amounts in your "Budgeted" column.
    
*   **Left to Budget**: The amount you still need to assign (Available to Budget - Total Budgeted). When this hits $0, you've given every dollar a job!
    
    *   Green ("Underbudgeted") = money left to budget
        
    *   Red ("Overbudgeted") = you've assigned more than you have available
        
    
*   **Budget Status**: A quick visual indicator that matches your Left to Budget amount
    
    *   Green ("Balanced") = you assigned exactly the amount that was available
        
    *   Orange ("Underbudgeted") = you still have money to assign
        
    *   Red ("Overbudgeted") = you've assigned more than you have available
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#understanding-net-total-available)

Understanding Net Total Available

Net Total Available deserves special attention because it helps you understand if you have enough money to execute your budget.

**Net Total Available** is calculated by combining your "Left to Budget" (from the General Pool) with the total "Available" (from the Outflow table). This is the total amount you have accounted for in your budget and you'll want to make sure that you have at least this amount of money in your accounts.

Simply put, it is the minimum amount of money you need in your bank accounts to cover your budget. It adds up all the Available balances in your categories plus any money you haven't budgeted yet.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#how-to-use-it)

How to use it:

*   This is the least amount of cash you need to have right now to cover your budget
    
*   Your actual bank balance might be higher (if you keep extra buffer money)
    
*   If you budget every dollar (zero-based budgeting), this number could be set up to match the total across all of your bank accounts (Est. Net Worth) pretty closely.
    

circle-exclamation

**Note**: Lunch Money doesn't offer a reconciliation feature to exactly match your bank account balances and your Lunch Money budget. The Net Total Available is the closest number we have to that, which is calculated based on all available funds in your budget, considering starting balances, rollovers, and the unallocated funds in your general pool.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#whats-next)

What's Next?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You know your way around the Budget page– now let's put it to use! In the next section, we'll explore how to make Lunch Money work for your budgeting style.

Ready to start budgeting? Let's go! 👇

[arrow-rightGo to Step 4: Budgeting](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting)

# Step 1: Intro to Budgeting | Knowledge Base

circle-check

You're on Step 1 of Lunch Money's Budgeting Guide!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FhxEWTO3BvdfQUSaDfMu6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0a5d224-2825-4ef2-92f4-055969adff2f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8919a024&sv=2)

Welcome to Lunch Money's budgeting feature guide! We're excited to walk you through it step by step, making sure you understand each feature along the way.

The best part? There's no "right" or "wrong" way to budget in Lunch Money. You get to pick what works for you. We give you the tools, and you decide how to use them!

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-1-intro-to-budgeting#heres-what-well-cover)

Here's what we'll cover:

1.  [**Setting up your budget foundation:**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget)
     Configure your budget period, income settings, and rollover options to match your financial life.
    
2.  [**Navigating the Budget page:**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page)
     Learn where everything lives and what all those numbers mean.
    
3.  [**Budgeting your money:**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting)
     Discover different ways to assign money to categories - from manual entry and budget presets that save you time, to moving money between categories and making adjustments as your needs evolve.
    
4.  [**Helpful extras:**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-5-miscellaneous-features)
     Explore additional features like historical spending views and budget breakdowns to elevate your budgeting game.
    

By the end of this guide, you'll understand not just how to use Lunch Money's features, but when and why to use them. We'll show you multiple approaches so you can find what works for your budgeting style.

circle-exclamation

**Note**: If you were a beta tester and previously tried the new budgeting feature, please review the [migration guide](https://support.lunchmoney.app/migrating-to-budgeting-v2)
 to ensure a smooth transition for your category group budgets and income rollovers settings.

Ready to take control of your money? Let's get started! 👇

[arrow-rightGo to Step 2: Settings up your budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?
