# CSV / PDF Importing | Knowledge Base

Lunch Money lets you import transactions in bulk using either CSV or PDF bank statements. This guide will take you step-by-step through the process.

circle-info

Migrating from Mint? For more details on the CSV import tool, [read the page on Mint migration tool.](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-1-upload-csv)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [What is a CSV file?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#what-is-a-csv-file)
    
*   [How do I download my transactions?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#how-do-i-download-my-transactions)
    
*   [Where is the CSV/PDF Import Tool?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#where-is-the-csv-pdf-import-tool)
    
*   [What format should my CSV be in?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#what-format-should-my-csv-be-in)
    
*   [Recommended course of action](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#recommended-course-of-action)
    
    *   [Step 1: Upload the CSV or PDF file](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-1-upload-the-csv-or-pdf-file)
        
    *   [Step 2: Match the columns](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-2-match-the-columns)
        
    *   [Step 3: Review settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-3-review-settings)
        
    *   [Step 4: Review transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-4-review-transactions)
        
    *   [Step 5: Import Transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-5-import-transactions)
        
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#troubleshooting)
    
*   [How we handle your files](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#how-we-handle-your-files)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#what-is-a-csv-file)

What is a CSV file?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most financial institutions will allow you to download a CSV export of your transactions. This is a plain-text file of your transactions details, such as date, amount and description, separated by a delimiter, typically a comma, hence, **c**omma-**s**eparated **v**alues.

With this file, you can import your transactions into Lunch Money quickly and easily.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#how-do-i-download-my-transactions)

How do I download my transactions?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your bank allows it, there will typically be a way to download your statements or transactions in CSV or PDF format directly from the bank's web portal, either for a specific period, or for a custom date range. Try searching in the area where you can download statements. If you need help locating this, you may need to contact your bank.

circle-info

Check below for guides on exporting transactions for:

*   [Apple Cardarrow-up-right](https://techcrunch.com/2020/01/21/apple-card-users-can-now-download-monthly-transactions-in-a-spreadsheet/)
    
*   [WeChat Pay and Alipay in Chinaarrow-up-right](https://www.notion.so/youngchingjui/Downloading-Transactions-in-China-185f49c2b39d427e9c82e10041e281a9)
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#where-is-the-csv-pdf-import-tool)

Where is the CSV/PDF Import Tool?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To import a CSV or PDF file with transactions, head over to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page and hit the "Import" button located next to the "Add to Cash" button:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FpzvhgAwcZqeuoUz28zzF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe122d94-6a2b-4a13-9e82-9637db904513&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59236dc5&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#what-format-should-my-csv-be-in)

What format should my CSV be in?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a fast and successful CSV import, we recommend that your file includes the following columns with the associated header name:

*   **Date of transaction** (required)
    
    *   Header name: `date`
        
    *   Format preferred: YYYY/MM/DD or YYYY-MM-DD
        
    *   All other formats are possible, but we may have a hard time parsing them. (It should still work, as there is an opportunity to teach our system which date format you're using. It just might take an extra step!)
        
    
*   **Name of transaction** (required)
    
    *   Header name: `payee` or `description`
        
    
*   **Transaction amounts**
    
    *   [See below](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#formats-supported-for-transaction-amounts)
        
    
*   **Transaction notes** (optional)
    
    *   Header name: `notes`
        
    
*   **Transaction categories** (optional)
    
    *   Header name: `categories`
        
    *   You will be asked to match the imported category with a new or an existing Lunch Money category
        
    
*   **Transaction tags** (optional)
    
    *   Header name: `tags`
        
    *   Comma-separated list of tag names
        
    *   You will be asked to match each imported tag with a new or an existing Lunch Money tag
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#formats-supported-for-transaction-amounts)

Formats supported for transaction amounts

We support three notations for indicating the amount for a transaction.

*   **Use single column:** Using one single amount column, with positive/negative notation denoting credit or debit. Recommended headers include
    
    *   `debit/credit`
        
    *   `amount`
        
    
*   **Use double column**: Using two columns, with values in one representing debits and values in the other representing credits. Recommended headers include:
    
    *   `debit` and `credit`
        
    *   `inflow` and `outflow`
        
    
*   **Use by type column**: Using one single amount column with an associated column denoting the type. The string in the type column must be one of: outflow, inflow, debit, credit. Recommended headers include:
    
    *   `debit/credit` and `amount`
        
    

The first two use three columns in the CSV while the last two uses a single column. The double column formats interpret all numbers in absolute format which means a negative will not flip the amount.

As of now, these 4 columns are the only ones that you're able to import using CSVs. However, you can always use [Rules](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
 to help you assign categories or update payee names according to your preferences and habits.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#recommended-course-of-action)

Recommended course of action


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If this is your first time using the CSV/PDF import tool, we recommend that you only import one month's worth of transactions to start. Then, go to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page and categorize and organize your transactions as you please. As you do this, Rules will be created to remember your changes and apply them to future similar transactions. You can always go to the [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 page to audit these and make sure they are accurate.

When you go back to the CSV/PDF import tool and upload a second month's worth of transactions, you'll notice in [**Step 4: Review Transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-4-review-transactions)
 that many of them will already be edited because you had rules set up from your first month! By uploading transactions in small batches, the less work you end up doing in the long run because your rules will get continuously refined. If you upload a year's worth in one go, you might get overwhelmed quickly.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-1-upload-the-csv-or-pdf-file)

Step 1: Upload the CSV or PDF file


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first step is to select the relevant account or asset that you'll be importing your transactions into. If you haven't set up any account yet, you can do so by going to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page and clicking on "Add Account".

circle-exclamation

If your account isn't showing up as an option in the dropdown, go to the [Accounts arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
page and check the 'Advanced Settings' under that account's details. For manually-managed assets, "Do not track transactions" must be disabled. For synced bank accounts, "Allow modifications to transactions" must be enabled.

After you select which asset the transactions are associated with, you can click on 'Additional settings' to define which currency the transactions are in, and finally, upload the file by clicking on "Process _\[number\]_ rows":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FdREhWlvMolUA7aQ0i0FR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D027344d6-f335-4249-ae04-d0e11eae5b33&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87557c0f&sv=2)

circle-info

Configurations can be saved during [Step 3](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-3-review-csv-settings)
 of the import process, so next time you upload CSVs to the same asset, you get to choose whether or not to use the saved configuration in order to skip the first 2 steps.

Note that there is a file size restriction of 3Mb and the CSV/PDF import tool will only upload 10,000 rows at a time.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-2-match-the-columns)

Step 2: Match the columns


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We need to match the column data from your uploaded file to the columns used by Lunch Money. To do so, click the header for each column to open the drop-down and select the corresponding field in Lunch Money. We already try to match some columns for you based on the header name—this works best when the file follows the recommended guidelines (see [**What format should my CSV be in?**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#what-format-should-my-csv-be-in)
).

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FT9HFwP6dIpuMJZ7ymqPo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e7e8478-4074-41e9-a5c5-474e10961962&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3fcddac5&sv=2)

Each column can only be mapped to one of the available options, and an option can only be used once. If you don't wish to import the data from a specific column, select "**Do not import"**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#handling-different-amount-notations)

Handling different amount notations

For files with a single amount column, use "**Amount**". You can also use "**Amount Type**" if you have a column that indicates debits vs credits.

For files with two separate columns, one for credits and one for debits, use "**inflow (amount)**" and "**outflow (amounts)**". While 'Amount' is marked as a required field, using the inflow and outflow options instead will fulfill this requirement.

circle-info

For more details, see [**Formats supported for transaction amounts**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#formats-supported-for-transaction-amounts)
).

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-3-review-settings)

Step 3: Review settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#checking-dates-and-amounts)

Checking dates and amounts

At the 'Review Notations' stage, your file has been parsed by our system based on your settings. Double-check to make sure our interpretation of the dates and amounts are correct. Specifically, make sure that the amounts are correct in what they represent:

> _Should a Starbucks expense be a credit? Nope! That's wrong– better flip the switch!_

This is very important to ensure that your transactions are imported correctly! To correct the date or amount type, click on 'Fix dates' or 'Flip types' buttons at the bottom of the table.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#checking-the-categories)

Checking the categories

At the 'Review Categories' stage, you will match the category names from the file to the categories that you have set up in Lunch Money. If there is an exact match for the category name between the file and Lunch Money, it will be automatically matched. Otherwise, you can click the field next to the category name to select the relevant category (or create a new one).

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#checking-the-tags)

Checking the tags

At the 'Review Tags' stage, you will match the tag names from the file to the tags that you have set up in Lunch Money. If there is an exact match for the tag name between the file and Lunch Money, it will be automatically matched. Otherwise, you can click the field next to the tag name to select the relevant tag (or create a new one).

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#malformed-lines)

Malformed lines

At the 'Final Settings' stage, you'll see a list a notice listings all malformed lines from your file. These represent lines in your file that we determined to be missing required data, such as a date, payee name, or amount. If you believe any of these were done in error, you can always go back to [Step 2](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-2-match-the-columns)
 and fix your column matches. You can also check your file to see if it's corrupted in any way. If you need assistance, we'd be more than happy to [help troubleshoot](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-7-getting-help)
!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FotVFannh902p4Ug9TQXO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c8c6616-ad83-4f3f-b3a7-21efda10b63f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1b40139&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#other-settings)

Other settings

You can choose to Apply Rules and Skip Duplicates. Both of these settings are recommended, so they are on by default.

Apply Rules will run your Rules against the transactions you import. Skip Duplicates will ensure that the same transaction will not be imported twice. We determine two transactions to be the same if the date, payee name, and amount all match exact.

Finally, you can choose to save your configuration. We will then remember your settings whenever you upload files for the same asset, letting you skip steps 2 and 3 of the import process!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FYUqPqPi2OeXhEmRKcVSR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b58dec3-c65d-4e64-bb1a-958879d92e3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=423b95c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-4-review-transactions)

Step 4: Review Transactions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On this page, you will be presented with a list of transactions ready to be imported into your Lunch Money account exactly as they appear. This list of transactions has run through your rules and been de-duplicated per your settings. Duplicated transactions are shown at the bottom for your personal debugging.

This is your chance to review the transactions you're about to import. If the dates look funny or something else looks off, you can always go back to fix any settings. To prevent some transactions from being imported, de-select them.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#step-5-import-transactions)

Step 5: Import Transactions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hurrah! Your transactions have been imported. We did a best guess as to what your updated balance should be, but if we were off, you can enter the correct balance on this page.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#im-having-issues-with-my-csv-file)

I'm having issues with my CSV file

Because there isn't a standard format for transactions in a CSV file, every bank exports transactions differently and we may sometimes encounter a CSV that we're unable to parse. However, we're working towards being able to support all variations and flavours of these CSV files. Please contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://support.lunchmoney.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#7f0c0a0f0f100d0b3f130a111c171210111a06511e0f0f)
 with a snippet of your file and we'll work on getting it supported.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#im-having-issues-with-my-pdf-file)

I'm having issues with my PDF file

PDF files tend to be content heavy and the layouts can differ significantly from bank to bank. If your PDF isn't parsing the data correctly, please contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://support.lunchmoney.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#11626461617e6365517d647f72797c7e7f74683f706161)
 and attach the file so we can work on getting it supported!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv#how-we-handle-your-files)

How we handle your files


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CSV imports are processed client-side. We do not store your CSV files and only reviewed transactions from the last step in our CSV importer are sent to Lunch Money servers. PDF imports are parsed using a trusted third-party partner, Bank Statement Converter (https://bankstatementconverter.com/). PDFs are not stored on our server and are sent to them directly. You can check their Privacy Policy here: https://bankstatementconverter.com/privacy. Notably, "Documents uploaded to Bank Statement Converter persist on our servers for 24 hours. After 24 hours they are deleted. We do not forward user uploaded documents to any third parties."

Last updated 1 month ago

# Stats | Knowledge Base

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#view-options)

View options


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#period-picker)

Period Picker

Use the period picker to choose any time period for your statistics page.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#include-recurring)

Include recurring

Toggle this on to include recurring items in your statistics. You may want to turn off recurring items to get rid of repetitive data. For example, if your rent or mortgage payment is consistently the most expensive transaction, this may clutter your "Top Expensive Purchases" list. Removing recurring items from your data helps you better identify anomalies in your spending.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#include-exclude-from-totals)

Include 'exclude from totals'

Toggle this on to include transactions categorized as 'exclude from totals'. You may want to keep this off to exclude large transactions such as paying off credit card bills from your statistics.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#elements)

Elements


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#top-expensive-purchases)

Top Expensive Purchases

This card shows your expenses in descending order by cost.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCgltF_j6MSh1vPNr%252Ftop-expensive.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1861aea3-7c2e-40e5-addf-e5fb34358321&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e919685&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#new-merchants)

New Merchants

This card shows you new merchants seen during this time period. It is also ordered in descending order by cost and shows how many transactions were recorded in parentheses. This is useful to identify new spending habits.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglq6qqevHQrrcnj%252Fnew-merchants.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85ad238a-c117-4e82-851d-1f61321069d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4b1cd86&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#top-merchants-by-total-cost)

Top Merchants by Total Cost

This card shows you which merchants you spent the most money with during this period. It doesn't take into account how many times you shopped there, only the total money spent.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglublKOa7iXdRzh%252Ftop-merchants-by-cost.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9118e1a9-10ba-4c0c-af72-e5424e481daf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=127f58a4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#top-merchants-by-of-transactions)

Top Merchants by # of Transactions

This card shows you which merchants you frequented the most during this period.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglvZM6hfI53r7ab%252Ftop-merchants-by-tx.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D412603fe-51fd-4085-98b8-0de942e55f1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63fad82c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#top-categories-by-total-cost)

Top Categories by Total Cost

This card shows you the categories where you had the most spending activity measured by total money spent.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglrPYnz3Jk9AxjG%252Ftop-categories-by-cost.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19b4c04b-5aac-419f-a1ff-c788567e0e12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67cb1ae5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#top-categories-by-of-transactions)

Top Categories by # of Transactions

This card shows you the categories where you had the highest spending activity measured by number of individual transactions.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglso1ZO-J4BrGi2%252Ftop-categories-by-tx.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac74d69e-1678-4c4b-aead-608413ed4633&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45401cdd&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/home/stats#monthly-email-digest)

Monthly email digest


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every month, you'll receive a monthly email delivered to your inbox with a summary of the above statistics.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZB9EoS95PaaZME9Zvz%252F-MZBCglp64BhAeqdoE9u%252Femail.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00f2c695-6dce-4929-8d52-e632b35bfbcf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9151b9a5&sv=2)

Last updated 4 years ago

# FAQ | Knowledge Base

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions

1.  [Can I have different periods for different categories?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#can-i-have-different-periods-for-different-categories)
    
2.  [How do I use envelope budgeting in Lunch Money?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-use-envelope-budgeting-in-lunch-money)
    
3.  [How do I zero-based budget in Lunch Money?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-zero-based-budget-in-lunch-money)

7.  [Can I budget using my total bank balance instead of just recent income?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#can-i-budget-using-my-total-bank-balance-instead-of-just-recent-income)
    
8.  [Why do I see "View not aligned with budgeting period" in the Budget Breakdown?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#why-do-i-see-view-not-aligned-with-budgeting-period-in-the-budget-breakdown)

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#can-i-have-different-periods-for-different-categories)

Can I have different periods for different categories?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, all categories share the same budget period.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-use-envelope-budgeting-in-lunch-money)

How do I use envelope budgeting in Lunch Money?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Envelope budgeting, also known as cash stuffing, divides your money into spending categories. In Lunch Money, you can achieve this by:

*   Setting up categories for each "envelope"
    
*   Using "rollover to same category" to keep money in each envelope
    
*   Tracking spending against each category's Available balance
    
*   Moving money between categories to prevent overspending
    

**Learn more:**

[bookA Beginner's Guide to Envelope Budgeting](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/beginners-guide-to-envelope-budgeting-cash-stuffing?utm_source=lm_knowledgebase)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-zero-based-budget-in-lunch-money)

How do I zero-based budget in Lunch Money?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Zero-based budgeting means assigning every dollar a job. In Lunch Money, you can achieve this by:

*   Turning on general pool rollovers
    
*   Budgeting until "Left to Budget" reaches $0
    
*   Using balance adjustments to align with your actual bank balance
    
*   Moving money between categories to prevent overspending
    

**Learn more:**

[bookZero-Based Budgeting Guide](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/zero-based-budgeting-simplified?utm_source=lm_knowledgebase)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-set-up-sinking-funds-in-lunch-money)

How do I set up sinking funds in Lunch Money?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sinking funds help save for future expenses. In Lunch Money, you can achieve this by:

*   Creating a category for each fund (e.g., "Car Repairs")
    
*   Budgeting money to it monthly
    
*   Using budget presets to regularly fund the category
    
*   Setting rollover to "same category" so funds accumulate
    

**Learn more**:

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-do-i-set-up-goals-in-lunch-money)

How do I set up goals in Lunch Money?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature will be coming soon! Stay tuned by upvoting [the feature request herearrow-up-right](https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/general-feature-request/p/savings-and-goals)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#how-can-i-adjust-the-starting-balance-for-the-period-without-using-rollovers)

How can I adjust the starting balance for the period without using rollovers?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have money available for budgeting that isn't new income (like cash gifts, loan repayments, or existing savings), you can:

1.  Create an income category (name it something like 'Starting Balance')
    
2.  Set it to 'Treat as income'.
    
3.  In ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FfwbwB2OdtuhAaNQIWiuW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3f28a32-0023-488d-b49b-7f82a2b6e14b&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d241f216&sv=2), set “Base income on” to “Larger of Budgeted and Actual Income Activity”.
    
4.  Enter the desired starting balance in the "Expected" column for that category. In the screenshot below, we’ve set it up so our starting balance is $10,000.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfZx4KVGkJ66V3ZR5ogRhEDPjEbeRY7A1v_45SU_TmIiUqB-mmsYTpVjucaUvB31mdjrqwU6dyXpl7AxbMjwvvVVmxvf5pmoJ3eBpD08vm664fnp1R-bb8hBeMWJOb5NkGChXIjUw%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e3e7736&sv=2)

This adds the money to your general pool without affecting your actual income tracking. You may also simply enter the amount in the "Expected" column of any existing income category.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#can-i-budget-using-my-total-bank-balance-instead-of-just-recent-income)

Can I budget using my total bank balance instead of just recent income?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes! To start with your existing bank balance:

1.  Enable "Roll over 'Left to Budget' and 'Overbudgeted' amounts" in ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2)
    
2.  Set a balance adjustment for your first period to match your current bank balance
    

> **Example:** If you wish to start budgeting from Jan 1, 2025 and had $15,000 in the bank on Dec 31, 2024, set your rollover balance to $15,000 starting Jan 1, 2025.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FRekLzjOrfndYP4ZYvKHn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf2f5936-8a50-421e-8c65-8623944e71ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb193435&sv=2)

From then on, your [Net Total Available](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-3-navigating-the-budget-page#understanding-net-total-available)
 will stay aligned with your actual bank balance.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#why-do-i-see-view-not-aligned-with-budgeting-period-in-the-budget-breakdown)

Why do I see "View not aligned with budgeting period" in the Budget Breakdown?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This indicates that the date range you are viewing doesn't match a full budgeting period.

For example, if you are budgeting by calendar month (i.e., July 1 - July 31), but looking at the "Month to date" filter (i.e. July 1 - July 28), it won't be possible to display the breakdown:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FlCeOC6UZtspcYonrLCxK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0439a43-46de-47b3-8dc2-d700cdacf494&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=111adb64&sv=2)

To resolve this, use the period picker to adjust the date range to cover the entire period you wish to view:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Feve0AOlBeqzooqdR4myx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da91d618e-775f-4b46-980a-ea8bd0fa410c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e66b50e8&sv=2)

circle-check

If you'd like to view the Budget Breakdown for multiple periods, you can do that by setting the date range to the first day of the first period, and the last day of the last period. The budget data will display as long as all periods fit perfectly within the date range.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#why-are-my-category-rollover-settings-not-activated)

Why are my category rollover settings "not activated"?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you enable category rollovers via the 'Settings View', the rollover options are set, but not activated. This is because you still need to set the starting date and amount for the rollover. If that's the case, you will see the text "(not activated)" next to the rollover option:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FTLYoTs5CKjEQh5wTS0JZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83eba8e7-c644-4b3c-8b54-98dffaff386e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cb996e2&sv=2)

To activate your rollovers, you will need to click on the arrow to the fair right of each category row to open the side panel. Under "Rollover options", you will need to click on "Add New" (for same category rollovers) or "edit" (for general pool rollovers) to set the starting balance and date:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FnMHvdh9UwFnQJMNwafE9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87a8985a-9524-482c-ac32-82d0bb23c402&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c72a8889&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#is-there-a-comprehensive-budgeting-video-tutorial)

Is there a comprehensive budgeting video tutorial?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This video tutorial below provides an in-depth overview of the budgeting page and all the main features:

# Step 4: Budgeting | Knowledge Base

circle-check

You're on Step 4 of Lunch Money's Budgeting Guide!

**Jump to:**

*   [**Manual budgeting**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#manual-budgeting)
    
*   [**Quick Budget Actions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#quick-budget-actions)
    
    *   [Budgeting suggestions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budgeting-suggestions)
        
    *   [Budget Presets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budget-presets)
        
    *   [Copy Budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#copy-budget)
        
    *   [Moving money between categories](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#moving-money-between-categories)
        
    
*   [**Available Balance Adjustments**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#available-balance-adjustments)
    
    *   [How to make balance adjustments](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#how-to-make-balance-adjustments)
        
    

* * *

Now that you're familiar with the layout of the Budget page, it's time to start budgeting!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FINEgIo0wU3OQPqpNELup%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9344b607-1f43-4452-bb07-85a346b02f15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15184b6b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#manual-budgeting)

Manual budgeting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The simplest way to set a budget is to do it manually:

1.  Find the category you want to budget for
    
2.  Click on the cell in that row under 'Budgeted'
    
3.  Type in the amount you want to budget
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FWCwIdUPEgPxqNzamg2qf%252F7987c58eee711796059b652c3006a65d.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D569f9b9e-04bf-4d35-bcb1-4778d8e43e0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f880731&sv=2)

That's it! Once you set your budget, everything else will update automatically, including how much you have left to spend and how much is left to budget (or overbudgeted) overall.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#quick-budget-actions)

Quick budget actions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budgeting-suggestions)

Budgeting suggestions

When you type in a budget amount, Lunch Money will make helpful suggestions to speed things up. Clicking any suggestion will automatically set the budget to that value. Let’s go over what these could be:

1.  **Left to budget**: Allocate all remaining unbudgeted money to this category. This will only show up if you have something left to budget—it won’t show if you are overbudgeted.
    
2.  **Zero out available**: Budget the amount needed to bring this category’s Available balance to $0.
    
3.  **This period’s spend**: Match what you’ve spent so far this period (set to the amount matching the Activity column.)
    
4.  **Last period’s spend**: Match what you spent in this category last period.
    
5.  **Avg spend last 3 periods**: Use the average amount you spent over the last 3 periods.
    
6.  **Last period’s budgeted**: Copy whatever you budgeted for this category last period.
    
7.  **Fixed amount/Fill to**: Manual setting if you have this set up in [budget presets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budget-presets)
    
8.  **Total expected recurring**: Use the sum of all recurring items expected for the period.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FySH7GrdrTLqJg1avevTC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c97898f-87e0-4dfc-8c15-58ea72178f71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20423a95&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budget-presets)

Budget Presets

Want to budget the same amounts each period? Budget Presets let you set up rules for categories with predictable spending (like rent or bills) so you don't have to type the same numbers every month.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#how-to-set-up-budget-presets)

**How to set up Budget Presets**

Click the arrow (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FF2hpwa2Xsyb1m7Vbh0EH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0090dc4-679d-492c-8ffe-f74ce8561949&width=37&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39f1d421&sv=2)) at the end of a category row to see your options:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F8ZBRuYR7VIcTuiD28JPL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1301fba-5965-488e-a365-63f22b251f71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a89e712&sv=2)

Similar to the [budgeting suggestions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#budgeting-suggestions)
 you saw earlier, you will find the following options:

1.  **Set fixed amount**: Always budget the exact same amount every period. For example, if you set rent to $1,500, it'll always budget $1,500.
    
2.  **Fill 'Available' up to a certain amount**: Tops up your Available balance to reach a target amount. For example, if you set the 'Dining Out' target to $200 and you have $50 rolled over, the preset will budget $150 to reach $200.
    
3.  **Set to this period's spend:** Match what you’ve spent so far this period (set to the amount matching the Activity column.)
    
4.  **Set to previous period's spend**: Match what you spent in this category last period.
    
5.  **Set to previous period's budget**: Use the same amount you budgeted for this category last period.
    
6.  **Set to average spend of last 3 periods**: Use the average amount you spent over the last 3 periods.
    
7.  **Set to total expected recurring amount**: Use the sum of all recurring items expected for the period.
    
8.  **Do nothing**: Skip budget presets for this category
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#applying-budget-presets)

**Applying Budget Presets**

Once you've set up your preferred method for each category, click the "Apply Budget Presets" button on the right sidebar. The button only appears when you have valid presets configured.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FrnLaHHAz31jhrdZIJGw8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ba3e892-2be8-416d-adaa-56c1622656fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2e4d11c&sv=2)

You can also trigger individual presets by clicking the checkmark icon next to any category with a preset:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FnzNnppKhAOuYmx8FZVSz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daffce46d-66ef-4c4b-bd76-c1247cd62893&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59009489&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#copy-budget)

Copy Budget

Want to keep things really simple? You can quickly copy the same budget values from a previous period using the "Copy Budget" button. When you click on it, you'll see which eligible periods you can copy from:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FdZGdfeQMIJS3JX3nEiyH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda21851c-05d7-4d49-bb4d-2b11791fbc30&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99afff18&sv=2)

**How it works**

Copy Budget copies category budgets from your selected period to the current period.

You can choose whether to overwrite your current budget values or keep what you've already set. For example, if you're setting up March and you've already budgeted $50 for 'Coffee' and $800 for 'Rent':

*   If "Overwrite all" is **not** selected: Your $50 coffee and $800 rent stay put. Only empty categories get filled with February's values.
    
*   If "Overwrite all" **is** selected: ALL your current budgets (including that $50 and $800) get replaced with February's values.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#clear-this-period)

Clear This Period

Need a fresh start? Clicking "Clear This Period" will remove all income and expense amounts from the 'Expected' and 'Budgeted' columns for the current period.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FEcYoS2KnRnY3dRvPTJ7p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe5e1c6c-67df-487c-8ea7-639a9a8968bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87bd4e49&sv=2)

circle-check

Note: This only affects the current period you're viewing - historical budgets remain unchanged. This action cannot be undone, so make sure you're ready for a clean slate!

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#moving-money-between-categories)

Moving money between categories

Overspent in one category but have wiggle room in others? No worries!

Moving money between categories is a core part of flexible budgeting - it lets you adapt to real life without starting from scratch. This is especially useful for envelope and zero-based budgeting approaches.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#heres-how-to-shift-money-between-categories)

Here's how to shift money between categories:

1.  Click the exchange icon next to the **Available** balance for a given category.
    
2.  Specify how much to move, from which category, and to which category. You may also choose to move money to or from the general pool (labeled as "Left to Budget").
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FTqloF3i9IfxjxdlTG2UK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad01f258-8b16-4de0-8ee3-002b378b84a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8e3eac1&sv=2)

This instantly adjusts both categories' budgets for the current period only. For example, if you move $100 from Entertainment to Dining Out, then Entertainment's budget decreases by $100 while Dining Out's increases by $100.

circle-check

**Tip**: This is perfect for those "borrowed from Peter to pay Paul" moments - when you overspend on groceries but underspend on gas, just move the difference!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#available-balance-adjustments)

Available Balance Adjustments


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes you need to reset your Available balances (the amounts that roll over between periods). This is called a balance adjustment.

When you create a balance adjustment, you're telling Lunch Money: "Start calculating the Available balance from this date forward with this new starting amount."

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#when-to-use-a-balance-adjustment)

When to use a balance adjustment?

Here are some reasons you might reset:

*   Switching from another budgeting app
    
*   Major life changes (new job, marriage, moving)
    
*   Fixing past mistakes or miscategorized expenses
    
*   Starting fresh for seasonal spending (holiday gifts or spring home maintenance)
    
*   Reconciling your actual spending with Lunch Money
    
*   Aligning your budget with your actual bank balance (especially important for zero-based budgeters)
    
*   Locking in current Available balances as a new starting point
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#how-to-use-a-balance-adjustment)

How to use a balance adjustment?

For example, if your "Dining Out" category is at -$150 after a few months of overspending, you can reset it to $0 (or any amount you choose). Your past spending stays in your records, but the Available balance calculates from the new date forward.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FPxeRfTx9fE40mIcYzn4D%252FBalance%2520Adjustments%2520Numbered.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49f34c6d-e2c1-484d-b796-2ad9ca4d1745&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72c967d3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#where-does-the-money-come-from)

Where does the money come from?

Balance adjustments don't move money from other categories - they create or remove money from your budgeting system. It's important to understand when to use each feature:

*   [**Moving money between categories**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#moving-money-between-categories)
    : Moves Available money between expense categories or general pool. Your Net Total Available stays the same - you're just shifting money around.
    
*   **Balance adjustments**: Adds or removes money from your overall budget. Changes your Available balance and Net Total Available amount.
    

circle-check

Tip: Use the "Move money" feature if you want to redistribute existing funds. Use balance adjustments only when you need to correct or reset your starting point.

circle-exclamation

Important: After making a balance adjustment, always make sure you have enough funds to cover your Net Total Available!

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#how-to-make-balance-adjustments)

How to make balance adjustments

You can create starting balance and date adjustments for the following:

*   **General Pool** \- Set both starting balance and date
    
*   **Same-category rollovers** \- Set both starting balance and date
    
*   **General pool rollovers** \- Reset the start date only (balance is managed at the General Pool level)
    

Lunch Money keeps a history of all adjustments while preserving your original data.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#for-individual-categories-with-same-category-rollovers-enabled)

**For individual categories with same-category rollovers enabled:**

1.  In the Outflow table, click the arrow (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FF2hpwa2Xsyb1m7Vbh0EH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0090dc4-679d-492c-8ffe-f74ce8561949&width=37&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39f1d421&sv=2)) to the right of any category
    
2.  In the 'Edit Category' panel, scroll down to "Rollover Options"
    
3.  Click on "Add New'" under "Adjustments History":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FvV0vkZ7zTO8wlfyh502F%252Fnew-category-balance-adjustment-addnew.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De711200b-9b59-4ef4-bb03-a4657f25a076&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=43a90346&sv=2)

1.  Enter the new balance and start date, and click on "Add adjustment":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjtXKOGpOXZruHqyXUxgc%252Fsame-category-rollovers-balance-adjustment.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e358723-a7af-421c-a68b-98f53337424f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b3aa521&sv=2)

1.  To finalize the change, click on "Save changes" at the bottom
    

circle-check

**Tip**: Lunch Money keeps a history of all adjustments — you'll see them listed under "Adjustments History" with an option to remove previous adjustments if needed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#for-individual-categories-with-general-pool-rollovers-enabled)

**For individual categories with general pool rollovers enabled:**

1.  In the Outflow table, click the arrow (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FF2hpwa2Xsyb1m7Vbh0EH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0090dc4-679d-492c-8ffe-f74ce8561949&width=37&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39f1d421&sv=2)) to the right of any category
    
2.  In the 'Edit Category' panel, scroll down to "Rollover Options"
    
3.  Click on "edit" next to the existing start date:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4B7vvhLSIZYzqdcHQ8Jk%252Fcategory-balance-adjustment-edit-generalpool.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2db83c24-b85c-46e8-b764-e9b6c6411e83&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=854809d3&sv=2)

1.  Enter the new start date, and click on "Reset":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FlQGyeaJ4VpsuJJ2Ksl0R%252Fnew-balance-adjustment-reset.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3c844b7-6789-458b-bef5-5d3d65a1e374&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ae54cb6&sv=2)

1.  To finalize the change, click on "Save changes" at the bottom
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#for-the-general-pool-rollover)

**For the general pool rollover:**

1.  Click on "Budget Settings" ( ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2) )
    
2.  Locate the "General Pool Rollover Setting" section
    
3.  Click on "Add new" under "Adjustments History":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4rDFFhkVW2wxuuyHg2OX%252Fgeneral-pool-adjustment-addnew.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f90d13f-2c8b-4120-bd25-dd9736779b98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ccd2fe0&sv=2)

1.  Enter the new balance and start date, and click on "Reset to...":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FYytw2y37eQnbSj5QXt5Y%252Fgeneral-pool-adjustment-reset.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D938aa2be-2004-4d9f-a61f-6143a30a9d3e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d587a0b&sv=2)

1.  To finalize the change, click on "Save changes" at the bottom
    

circle-exclamation

**Note**: The General Pool balance adjustment controls the overall "Left to Budget" / "Overbudgeted" amount, and will ignore any past amounts rolled over from categories into the General Pool.

circle-check

**Tip**: Lunch Money keeps a history of all adjustments — you'll see them listed under "Adjustments History" with an option to remove previous adjustments if needed.

# Analyze | Knowledge Base

The Analyze page is where you will find the Query Tool. This tool can be used to set up custom curated views of your income and expense data, in order to obtain insights beyond those offered in the default Lunch Money reports.

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/analyze#setting-the-view)

Setting the view


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Query Tool offers a number of ways to display your data, so that you can view the information in the way that best works for your needs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/analyze#the-data-viewing-options-include-report-pie-chart-bar-graph-line-chart-stacked-bar)

The data viewing options include: **Report****, Pie Chart, Bar Graph, Line Chart, Stacked Bar**

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcccnnItM9RSw2Z92TXZTo-zvqT62sJhtuiVJ3oopI4YO62aESPV1c8FoZgnfyztgnCuP24OA6TIro_rLKeqzn9eJB6bWZVQF0l3PTGb1gBc-pvXVatEw16zBy6_SUlFGf2WUblqC8vWHSDZWY0cq371SWF%3Fkey%3DqigELdhKiSzTlncHDzk55g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b3a0100&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/analyze#setting-the-date-range)

**Setting the date range**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To begin, set the date range for the data that you’d like to see. You can choose a predefined view from the drop-down menu, or enter a custom date range:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc_jCstNEprDYOBKcZqOlHSrdsWtauh_VQ-7M0LgQey-bXeIsmNT5AKKM48E8yC7IHxZMWh_nzt4pDRCQ3e-JJW5rH7XtQdhd0y24OhfTH27Oa9kpBJZBPtMepqhsKgLtTmAOnOtjWT1xNwsZX8YFue4hM%3Fkey%3DqigELdhKiSzTlncHDzk55g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42a29b67&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/analyze#setting-the-time-granularity)

Setting the time granularity


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can change the time granularity (day, week, month, or year) by which you’d like to display the data, using the drop-down menu above the table:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXd7KnZnhfVguHWy2gJjPM8jBohTrrLc7-O67Tj55LMng4XVa5JJok2FXQ4qBD9X4x22JC8UlVjJ80jWLVlHdstmuLVe8ChoBfmK55zIPyRbRdhvtHOPCUUiDAbQKdwtiTfQqiIyMqJpJpJ8xdqscrR-TXzD%3Fkey%3DqigELdhKiSzTlncHDzk55g&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8df7da9&sv=2)

# Creating Recurring Items | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Manual creation**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#manual-creation)
    
    *   [From the Recurring page](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#from-the-recurring-page)
        
    *   [From the Transactions page](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#from-the-transactions-page)
        
    
*   [**Suggested recurring (automatic detection)**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#suggested-recurring-automatic-detection)
    
*   [**Integration with rules**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#integration-with-rules)
    

* * *

In Lunch Money, recurring items are managed and tracked via the [Recurringarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring)
 page. The Recurring page is viewed on a month-to-month basis, meaning that you would only see the recurring items for the period in the active view (eg. May 2024). If you have recurring items that occur twice a month, you will see them appear as two separate entries on the page. On the other hand, if you have a recurring item that occurs once a year, it will only appear on its renewal month.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#manual-creation)

Manual creation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Creating new recurring items can be done both from the [Recurringarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring)
 page directly, or from an existing transaction on the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
 page.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#from-the-recurring-page)

**From the Recurring page**

1.  Go to Finances > Recurring
    
2.  Click on the ‘Add new recurring item’ button located above the table
    
3.  In the ‘Create recurring item’ panel that appears on the right side of the screen, fill in the obligatory fields for merchant name, estimated billing date, transaction category, and repeating cadence. Review the optional properties as well.
    
4.  Click on “Next” at the bottom
    
5.  Now, select whether the expected amount is fixed or fluctuating and enter the amount
    

circle-info

While some recurring payments have a fixed amount every time (eg. Netflix subscription), some recurring payments may have an amount that fluctuates from one month to another (eg. utility bill). As you create your recurring item, you'll be asked if this is a fluctuating item or fixed. You can always edit any rules later on to change these properties if you wish.

1.  To finalize, click on “Create” at the bottom
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#from-the-transactions-page)

**From the Transactions page**

1.  Go to Finances > Transactions
    
2.  Locate the recurring transaction and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit Transaction’ panel that appears on the right side of the screen, scroll down to the ‘I want to…” section and click on “Convert to recurring item”
    
4.  If there are existing recurring items, you will be able to review and select them if relevant. Otherwise, to continue creating a new recurring item, click on “Create new recurring item”
    
5.  Most of the details will be automatically filled in using the transaction data, so you will only need to fill in the repeating cadence. Review the rest of the data and optional properties.
    
6.  Click on “Next” at the bottom
    
7.  Now, select whether the expected amount is fixed or fluctuating. The amount will be filled in automatically, yet will require your input if you choose to enter a range (fluctuating).
    
8.  To finalize, click on “Create” at the bottom
    

Once created, Lunch Money will automatically search for all matching transactions to link with the newly created recurring item.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjWBJAKq90nX8wf9Jw538%252FRecurring%2520Item%2520-%2520Create%2520from%2520Transaction.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3a8443-89af-4e20-8d1e-a886a7d481cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9acfb99&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#suggested-recurring-automatic-detection)

Suggested recurring (automatic detection)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you use bank syncing or CSV imports, Lunch Money will automatically detect recurring transactions if there is a clear pattern of payee and amount that repeat over a regular cadence. If a recurring pattern is detected, a suggested recurring item will be created and those transactions will be linked to it.

Suggested recurring items are not immediately added to the Recurring page, and will appear on a separate page for suggested recurring items: [https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring/suggestedarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring/suggested)

The Suggested Recurring Items page can be accessed by clicking on the “Show suggestions (X)” button above the table:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXctdkRfK-AvIyeN_o8pcVSKWcgOZZtQ_Guh4OHaYcg42YRZYR0f2Ewaq6PjgjXNrhtqNs8cZ9EWFQrBb9T50frsHJOclkLqo3QNbQ1pkJThN1JhjmR4KORgYGS7YRaZPyOLmBKUo9Uvgh0QirdZZOLMlj1M%3Fkey%3D_VQCALLf2VI72xILJ2wvDA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70d912b6&sv=2)

The Suggested Recurring Items page can also be accessed by clicking on the “Review X recurring items” box on the right side of the page:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeW50X9L265u9rsdwzZw7YybP4k8ZozgmG0rJ8hg6YpjbZv0TNJ4qD3La56qsS9YxWkUrUMBeMmJ7dQ-tC7BlbXMiKFq-OQ2zZHyo-Tgh-peCcRMfrvTjbz3ueeoZ8wCDJGvVfMTBJk8bHHG2qpByc42NsO%3Fkey%3D_VQCALLf2VI72xILJ2wvDA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48428cf1&sv=2)

The suggested recurring items will need to be approved or rejected. If you accept the suggested recurring item, it will be added to the Recurring page. If you mark the suggested recurring item as "this is not a recurring item" it will be removed (the corresponding recurring rule will also be deleted).

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/creating-recurring-items#integration-with-rules)

Integration with rules


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recurring [rules](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
 will automatically be created when a recurring item is set up on the [Recurring arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring/)
page, or when a suggested recurring item is created.

The rule that is created helps Lunch Money identify future transactions as recurring and to automatically link them to the corresponding recurring items.

By default, the recurring rule will include parameters for the Payee, Amount and Date. If you also selected an account in the “Paid from account” field, then the rule will also include an Account to match by.

For example, if you created a new monthly recurring expense for "Pat's Gym" at $30 a month with the expected billing date to be around the 3rd of every month, then a rule will be created to match transactions that are expenses of $30 with the merchant name "Pat's Gym" occurring between the 1st and 5th of the month.

circle-info

The range in days is to allow room for possible time variance, given that transactions may not always post to your bank account on the exact day.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FfgDgl8Y5EIIfQauIwJ88%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91e94772-884b-465d-953d-a5d6503f231c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fae67751&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#which-cryptocurrency-tokens-are-supported-in-lunch-money)

Which cryptocurrency tokens are supported in Lunch Money?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lunch Money supports manual tracking for crypto assets and holdings in over 300 cryptocurrencies, with more being added every week by user demand! Lunch Money pulls the latest exchange rates every few minutes so you'll get the latest balances reflected properly as part of your net worth.

circle-info

If you don't see your cryptocurrency supported, please [let us knowarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts?show_feedback=cryptocurrency-request)
 and we'll work on adding it! 🙂

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FoZsQOoMBdXdkUqpVw37H%252Fe4fcdae6b3a69f91753fe5d533f1457e.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc18d4a3f-1041-4b55-9fa1-b05669af02ae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82930a63&sv=2)

For the step-by-step instructions to add your crypto assets in Lunch Money, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-set-up-manually-managed-crypto-assets)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#which-cryptocurrency-wallets-are-supported-in-lunch-money)

Which cryptocurrency wallets are supported in Lunch Money?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lunch Money supports the following cryptocurrency wallets for automatic balance syncing: [Coinbasearrow-up-right](https://www.coinbase.com/home)
, [Ethereumarrow-up-right](https://ethereum.org/en/)
, and [Krakenarrow-up-right](https://www.kraken.com/wallet)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FlgZ3ZvvtLsq3OrJfnfeG%252Fadc46d4d29c50bd3fc5cf5dcd8fb3074.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3024bf2-b3bc-4be9-98fc-0fea235d026f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20258bbb&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#how-do-i-generate-a-coinbase-api-key)

How do I generate a Coinbase API key?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To generate new Coinbase API keys to integrate with Lunch Money, follow these steps:

1.  In Coinbase, navigate to [API keysarrow-up-right](https://www.coinbase.com/settings/api)
     via Settings
    
2.  Click on "Create API Key" at the top right corner
    
3.  After naming your key, select the Portfolio to be tracked. You can also select "Default" and Lunch Money will automatically filter out zero-balance accounts.
    
4.  Leave the default "View (read only)" permission and leave the IP whitelist field blank. Then hit "Create & Download" and download the cdp\_api\_key.json file for future use.
    
5.  Hit the Copy icon to copy the API key name and paste it in the "API key name" field in Lunch Money
    
6.  Copy the Private key and paste it into the "Private key" field in Lunch Money
    

circle-info

Not sure where to enter the keys in Lunch Money? [Click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FvvVnenfEiPuaL2pHAhlr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D163ac6e5-9b7a-4d35-a998-685e645ccd7e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d87c661&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#where-do-i-find-my-ethereum-wallet-address)

Where do I find my Ethereum wallet address?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your Ethereum wallet address is a unique string of characters which represents your wallet on the Ethereum blockchain. A Ethereum address is 42-character's long that starts with **"0x"**, followed by a mix of numbers and letters (eg. `0x742d35Cc6634C0532925a3b844Bc454e4438f44e`).

You should be able to find your Ethereum wallet address in your crypto wallet app. Simply copy the address and paste it into Lunch Money to connect your Ethereum wallet:

circle-info

Not sure where to enter the wallet address in Lunch Money? [Click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FTRT2sud6Zzx2HTuubI2a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35034a4b-52fa-49b5-b7fc-3e6ae6ce1c13&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74cc43b0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#how-do-i-generate-a-kraken-api-key)

How do I generate a Kraken API key?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To generate new Kraken API keys to integrate with Lunch Money, follow these steps:

1.  In Kraken, navigate to the [API Settings Pagearrow-up-right](https://pro.kraken.com/app/settings/api)
    
2.  Click on the "Create API Key" button
    
3.  Give the key a name, like "Lunch Money". Then select only Query under Funds and ensure all other Permissions are unchecked. Leave the rest of the options toggled to Off and hit the "Generate Key" button.
    
4.  Hit the Copy icon to copy the API name and paste it in the "API key" field in Lunch Money
    
5.  Copy the Private key and past it into the "Private key" field in Lunch Money
    

circle-info

Not sure where to enter the keys in Lunch Money? [Click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FTy0E9R5VIZ0CwKMEE40Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5baae0a-b1f0-45d7-aad3-ffa73b94ba92&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=385126e8&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#can-i-sync-crypto-wallet-transactions)

Can I sync crypto wallet transactions?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Crypto wallet transactions are not currently supported in Lunch Money. You may only track the balance of crypto assets at this time.

circle-info

Please consider upvoting the [relevant feature request ticketarrow-up-right](https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/transactions/p/crypto-wallet-transactions)
 on the Feedback Board to show your support and be notified of any developments!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/crypto#why-is-my-synced-crypto-account-showing-not-supported)

Why is my synced crypto account showing "Not Supported"?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are seeing 'Not supported' or 'Relink' in the status column for a synced crypto account, this typically means that the original API key or address that was used to connect the account is no longer valid:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fk2NDaWFdQC9llGZC2zJC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6cfc9f7a-368d-4f64-b021-b2f73eba3b9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79ea5f4e&sv=2)

To fix this, simply [create a new connection with your wallet](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
. Once that's done, you may remove the original account and opt to merge the existing balance history with your new connection.

Last updated 11 months ago
