# FAQ | Knowledge Base

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions

1.  [What’s the difference between recurring transactions, items and rules?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#id-1.-whats-the-difference-between-recurring-transactions-items-and-rules)
    
2.  [Can I disable suggested recurring item detection?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#can-i-disable-suggested-recurring-item-detection)
    
3.  [How do I request a new feature for Recurring Items?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#id-2.-how-do-i-request-a-new-feature-for-recurring-items)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#whats-the-difference-between-recurring-transactions-items-and-rules)

What’s the difference between recurring transactions, items and rules?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Recurring Transactions** are any transactions that repeat on a regular cadence, with the same payee and amount. These are managed on the Transactions page.

**Recurring Items** hold the recurring transactions within them, and are managed on the Recurring page.

**Recurring Rules** define the transaction properties by which a transaction is considered recurring, and will automatically link the matched transaction to the relevant recurring item.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#can-i-disable-suggested-recurring-item-detection)

Can I disable suggested recurring item detection?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can effectively prevent transactions from being associated with suggested recurring items by creating a 'Don't link to recurring' rule on the [Rules pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
:

**Here's how to set up the rule:**

1.  Go to the [Rules pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
    
2.  Click on 'Add a new rule'
    
3.  Under "If..", click on 'Add condition' and choose 'Matches day'
    
4.  Set the condition to "Day is between (inclusive) 1 & 31"
    

circle-check

This condition ensures that the rule triggers for any transactions with a date within that range, meaning, all transactions!

1.  Under "Then..", click on 'Add action' and scroll down to select 'Don't link to recurring item'
    

circle-check

This action doesn't prevent existing recurring item rules from triggering, and your own recurring items will still work as expected. This action will only prevent the automatic creation of new suggested reucrring items.

1.  To save the new rule, click on 'Create'
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4IVDUsQucypYOZ3zx6v1%252Fdisable%2520suggested%2520reucrring%2520rule.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6670986-a5bc-4043-83de-90103a832ec5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4abd57d&sv=2)

circle-info

Once you've set this rule up, make sure to also clear out any existing suggested recurring items as well, by approving or rejecting them. If you have pending suggested recurring items to review, you will see a 'Show suggestions' button on the [Recurring pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring/)
. You can also [click herearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring/suggested)
 for a direct link.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/faq#how-do-i-request-a-new-feature-for-recurring-items)

How do I request a new feature for Recurring Items?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are always looking for feedback on new features, and recommend opening a feature request ticket on the Feedback Board here: [https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/recurring-itemsarrow-up-right](https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/recurring-items)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcmlXhuGWC6JPYuGn15MQ65o7Ef24Qb1_AA-gEeik0qmVwqw9t_-k9Yi8lQUOO0Hx0G7WvQtLSKU9HCJ2tD4J0h3kw7eyB7tn-y3zE6ezMRcyhAQtYH74urxyi6kyxEK3flT7jBExDjE8ITTidJP_X4tQtk%3Fkey%3D_VQCALLf2VI72xILJ2wvDA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca51b767&sv=2)

Last updated 12 days ago

Was this helpful?

# Transactions | Knowledge Base

Transactions are the building blocks for your Lunch Money experience! A transaction represents the movement of money, whether that's between existing accounts or from your credit card to a merchant.

# Transaction Status | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Reviewed vs. unreviewed**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#reviewed-vs.-unreviewed)
    
    *   [How to mark a transaction as "reviewed"](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-reviewed)
        
    *   [How to mark a transaction as "unreviewed"](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-unreviewed)
        
    
*   [**Automatic review settings**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#automatic-review-settings)
    
    *   [Auto-review transactions on update](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#auto-review-transactions-on-update)
        
    *   [Auto-review transactions on manual creation](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#auto-review-transactions-on-manual-creation)
        
    
*   [**Automatic transaction status updates with Rules**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#automatic-transaction-status-updates-with-rules)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#reviewed-vs.-unreviewed)

Reviewed vs. unreviewed


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction status serves as a safety measure implemented to help prevent erroneous transaction data and ensure that all transactions are categorized properly, with correct dates, payees, etc.

When transactions are automatically synced into Lunch Money, some data may not always perfectly match up, so the "unreviewed" status serves as an indication that the transaction may need your attention.

Unless automatically marked as reviewed by a [Rulearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
, all automatically imported transactions will initially be marked as "unreviewed". On the other hand, manually created transactions will automatically be marked as "reviewed" by default.

If there are any unreviewed transactions in the active view, you will see a prompt on the right-side of the screen to review those transactions. You can click on it to see a filtered view of all unreviewed transactions for the period:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2F84CLX6L-wGlLSjW9RAGse7xGVbhkLjL10Oqv9o2ZUmmtWwTLJmGUxLE80LCFVjKVJBS3haIeMJK3EGI0g9SL5NMzk8_X0xv9Uy1rBPl9vqvmKxdgy7Fwzw40wOfOOTms21XpNvfnpV2SkER_yxrgqb8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4af5eb6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-reviewed)

**How to mark a transaction as "reviewed"**

To quickly change an individual transaction’s status to "reviewed", head over to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page, and click on the gray check mark icon in the far-right column to turn it green.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#if-you-wish-to-change-the-status-for-multiple-transactions-in-bulk)

**If you wish to change the status for multiple transactions in bulk:**

1.  Select the transactions by clicking the respective checkboxes on the far-left column.
    
2.  In the '_Selected Transactions_' menu on the right side of the screen, click on the "Mark reviewed" button.
    

Alternatively, to mark all unreviewed transactions in the current view as "reviewed", you can click on the green check mark icon at the very top of the column. In the confirmation dialog that appears, click on "Yes, confirm" to confirm the bulk review:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FPTkBk6jpIEXSqLQREYCQHsJNbp88ZXnS20MKcuD_76heivjdjOQ9cbdaiRbPFdqKzcz1nZLDAVLIftcReQ69cTzR-j2sKsLxktPGMgS01fc2CilaVC3jifVswUCzfTnkvgiNW91aUaNtupjrNprbA4o&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0690f0c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-unreviewed)

**How to mark a transaction as "unreviewed"**

To quickly change an individual transaction’s status to "unreviewed", head over to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page, and click on the green check mark icon in the far-right column to turn it gray.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#if-you-wish-to-change-the-status-for-multiple-transactions-in-bulk-1)

**If you wish to change the status for multiple transactions in bulk:**

1.  Select the transactions by clicking the respective checkboxes on the far-left column.
    
2.  In the '_Selected Transactions_' menu on the right side of the screen, click on the "Bulk-edit" button.
    
3.  Under "Update fields", locate and toggle-on the option "Mark all as unreviewed".
    
4.  Confirm by clicking on "Save changes".
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FC66rmXGxh70UERneya0c%252FStatus%2520-%2520Bulk%2520Unreviewed.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbac3b50b-bd0d-478a-8272-c7bbdd3470fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=167ed01e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#automatic-review-settings)

Automatic review settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the Settings page, under ‘User Preferences’, you will find a section called ‘Transaction Preferences’. There, you have two auto-review options that can be enabled or disabled:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeg-BCEpS_DdmeJBvQcszXlMo7EoTWFwahitYsuEk_u3aj9wqfWR6Q45q4GwMD-rpArkmknOxUKjktQF5kJ0Zv0iznIBMVtyUQ8FdJGm0qHztWOPvQVYqqxOLiPHkoRyAsirE0DoD1YeUABvZMhWgH8hoNu%3Fkey%3D3DxWD4D8aYdCGzyHnq2wdg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4919015d&sv=2)

circle-info

These options apply across all budgets on your Lunch Money account. Enabling these options on one budget account will also enable them on all other budgets.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#auto-review-transactions-on-update)

**Auto-review transactions on update**

You can enable this option if you would like to have unreviewed transactions automatically marked as “reviewed” after an update is made. This means that any change made to the Date, Amount, Category, Payee, Notes or Account will update that transaction’s status to “reviewed”.

If you wish to always manually review transactions, make sure to disable this option. That way updates to the transaction will not affect the status, and you can manually set it as “reviewed” when you are ready.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#auto-review-transactions-on-manual-creation)

**Auto-review transactions on manual creation**

While transactions synced from a bank account will always be set to “unreviewed” by default, manually created transactions can be set to automatically clear to “reviewed” status upon creation.

Enabling this option would have new manually created transactions start in a reviewed state, while disabling these options would have them start in an unreviewed state.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#automatic-transaction-status-updates-with-rules)

Automatic transaction status updates with Rules


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While the automatic review settings cover all manually-updated and/or manually-created transactions, Rules can be set up to automatically mark specific transactions as “reviewed” or “unreviewed” based on a certain criteria.

circle-info

Rules will override auto-review settings and the default behavior of synced transactions. This means that a synced transaction can automatically be set to “reviewed” status by a rule, despite the expected default “unreviewed” status.

For example, you can set up a rule for transactions from a specific account to always be marked as “reviewed”, or for transactions from a specific Payee to always be marked as “unreviewed”.

To learn more about rules, please [see here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfKEmBGO5renPO2sG3yjCz_-IzqrwcIdPatd-9pI2Ntyl4qqfA7dQ2ZuOuWa1GKpA3-FGo926p71wpBqcu1mLHEUWaeCA7XyHg2yAf5LTbjBfElr4HN6pTOMGXdfwa60pYpQPWUqNUTxNRGWlkz521HGxg%3Fkey%3D3DxWD4D8aYdCGzyHnq2wdg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34da8c86&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Reviewed vs. unreviewed](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#reviewed-vs.-unreviewed)
    
*   [How to mark a transaction as "reviewed"](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-reviewed)
    
*   [How to mark a transaction as "unreviewed"](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#how-to-mark-a-transaction-as-unreviewed)
    
*   [Automatic review settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-status#automatic-review-settings)

# Revising Recurring Items | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Table view settings**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#table-view-settings)
    
    *   [Grouping](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#grouping)
        
    *   [Sorting (Ascending / Descending)](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#sorting-ascending-descending)
        
    
*   [**Revising recurring items**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#revising-recurring-items)
    
    *   [How to edit an existing recurring item](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-edit-an-existing-recurring-item)
        
    *   [How to merge two recurring items](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-merge-two-recurring-items)
        
    *   [How to delete a recurring item](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-delete-a-recurring-item)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#table-view-settings)

Table view settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you have a large number of recurring items set up on the Recurring page, you may find it easier to organize the table by grouping and sorting the recurring items.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#grouping)

Grouping

The recurring items in the table can be grouped by the following properties:

*   Category
    
*   Cadence
    
*   Account
    
*   Type (Debit vs Credit)
    
*   None
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4jIUEXgTHpImFcqLpaIO%252FRecurring%2520Item%2520-%2520Group%2520by.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac7ceec1-b2f3-4f5d-99da-706dfc2dc51d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d828664&sv=2)

Once you select a property to group by, that property will no longer be represented with a header as a column in the table, but instead, in horizontal tabs that hold groups of similar recurring items together. The tab can be expanded or collapsed by clicking on it.

Some examples:

*   If you select to group by “Category”, your recurring items will be grouped by the categories they share (eg. “Utilities”, “Entertainment”, “Income”, etc.).
    
*   If you choose to group by “Type”, the recurring items will be grouped by debits (recurring expenses) and credits (recurring income).
    
*   If you choose to group by “None”, all recurring items will appear ungrouped, listed all together in the table.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#sorting-ascending-descending)

Sorting (Ascending / Descending)

The data in each column in the table can be sorted by ascending or descending alphabetical or numerical order. To sort the data, simply click on the header of the column. The first click will sort by descending order, and clicking again will sort by ascending order.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4jWrucFuEP689O5ATPRs%252Fa349880f209e93d478d7bd53eb6eef4f.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9c2188c-27cd-4166-881a-c2392cddea45&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf2e1f1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#revising-recurring-items)

Revising recurring items


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When editing an existing recurring item, keep in mind that the changes made will apply to all instances of the recurring item across all periods.

If for example, you change the start date, the recurring item instances before that date will be removed from the Recurring page. The past transactions already linked to the recurring item will remain linked, even if the specific past recurring item instances have been removed.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-edit-an-existing-recurring-item)

How to edit an existing recurring item

Editing recurring items is done from the Recurring page:

1.  Go to Finances > Recurring
    
2.  Locate the relevant recurring item and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit recurring item’ panel that appears on the right side of the screen, you can revise any of the details
    
4.  To confirm the changes, click on “Save” at the bottom
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-merge-two-recurring-items)

How to merge two recurring items

Merging two recurring items together is done from the Recurring page:

1.  Go to Finances > Recurring
    
2.  Locate the recurring item that you wish to merge into another and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit recurring item’ panel that appears on the right side of the screen, scroll all the way down and click on “Merge with existing recurring item”
    
4.  You will now select the other recurring item, to which you wish to merge all existing linked transactions into
    
5.  To confirm the changes, click on “Save changes” at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F89iJMogTpb0XxoRahZ8i%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D078842d9-472b-4070-8f73-2f9d1707e9f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c5ae053&sv=2)

Once merged, the original recurring item will be removed from the Recurring page. The associated transactions will now be linked to the other recurring item with which it was merged.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/revising-recurring-items#how-to-delete-a-recurring-item)

How to delete a recurring item

Deleting recurring items is done from the Recurring page:

1.  Go to Finances > Recurring
    
2.  Locate the recurring item that you wish to delete and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit recurring item’ panel that appears on the right side of the screen, click on “Delete” at the very bottom
    
4.  In the confirmation dialog, click “Yes, confirm”
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F8mnclnf135JtPrIijPnx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df39d9dbe-0d0a-4ffd-bcf3-4ab152992ac7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e27ff20&sv=2)

Once deleted, the recurring item will be removed from the Recurring page. The associated recurring rule will also be removed from the Rules page. The associated transactions will be unlinked and treated as regular transactions again.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

What’s the difference between categories and tags?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both tags and categories are used to organize your transactions, yet they serve different purposes. Check out the comparison table below, outlining the main differences:

Tags

Categories

Transactions can be assigned more than one

✅

❌

Can be set as rule condition

❌

✅

Can be set as rule action

✅

✅

Stats and Trends reports

❌

✅

Query Tool reports

✅

✅

Can be color-coded

✅

❌

Can be budgeted for

❌

✅

To learn more about categories, [arrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags)
[see here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories)
, and [here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#categories)
.

How do I request a new feature for Tags?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#what-is-the-beta-testing-program)

What is the beta testing program?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The beta testing program is a way for users to get early access to new features before they are officially released to the public. Beta testers help continuously improve and shape Lunch Money by providing valuable feedback, identifying bugs, and suggesting enhancements.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#how-do-i-become-a-beta-tester)

How do I become a beta tester?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To join the beta testing program, login to your Lunch Money account, click the gears icon next to 'HELP' at the top of the page, then navigate to the Community page. There, click on the orange button to join the program:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdg6S5TBCmu2vqqGjVpUv8jNvq6VjssAgjl3yiaU3SvBc-wx2Xprcx4mFZFQFqOWhnuBSKGtrfnch0VGQDlo67Px2RQKjIS1qXZPWJ_SarNPEmalRS84NPFz7P6B87r5-rrpXWdsA%3Fkey%3DTsEDydLAOWhZDeOWeY2k-e-w&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17c8dc51&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#how-do-i-access-the-beta-version-of-the-app)

How do I access the beta version of the app?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you’ve joined the Beta Testing Program, you can access the beta build at: [beta.lunchmoney.apparrow-up-right](http://beta.lunchmoney.app/)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#where-should-i-share-feedback-for-beta-features)

Where should I share feedback for beta features?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To share feedback on new Lunch Money beta features, feel free to open an [in-app support ticketarrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/getting-started#step-7-getting-help)
, or join the private beta channel within our [Discordarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/discord)
 community!

To gain access to the beta tester's channel on Discord, you will need to enable Linked Roles. Here's how:

1.  Open [Discordarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/discord)
    
2.  At the top left corner of the Discord, click on the server name at the top ("Lunch Mo...") and then on "Linked Roles":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FriXfWFDNKOeTR5ObjCew%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d28345e-41f4-49f2-9980-b3412f0bc4ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b2e3e26&sv=2)

3\. Next, click on "Beta Tester" to connect with Lunch Money:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FzzSXL0NWzWpaMNUZMKCC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7101660-1e6e-414c-a93b-5d1c477bbf86&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ae41edb&sv=2)

4\. Once you've got the 'Beta Tester' role enabled, you'll be able to find the [**#🧪-beta-testers**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/842337014556262411/1134593799209881621)
 channel on the left side panel.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#will-i-still-be-able-to-access-the-public-build)

Will I still be able to access the public build?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes! The public production build will always be available to you at [my.lunchmoney.apparrow-up-right](http://my.lunchmoney.app/)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#what-will-happen-to-my-transaction-data)

What will happen to my transaction data?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your data (eg. accounts, transactions, rules, etc.) will sync between the public and beta builds. The beta and production builds use the same database and changes made in one environment will reflect in the other environment as well.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/beta-testing-program#how-will-i-find-out-about-new-features)

How will I find out about new features?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As a beta tester, you will receive updates on latest features to test on beta via a newsletter email and/or in the private beta Discord channel.

# Unlimited Budget Accounts | Knowledge Base

Lunch Money supports unlimited budget accounts per subscription!

You can create additional budgets to track different aspects of your life, collaborate with others and even use as a developer sandbox account! The possibilities, like your budgets, are limitless.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#how-do-i-create-a-new-budget-account)

How do I create a new budget account?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the web app, locate the teal circle to the left of the "Logout" button:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FGXQ0usftE7Hq6Xq915In%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccd2adbc-da2b-4136-b0fb-467e76e54981&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87bd1380&sv=2)

This will invoke the "Switch Accounts" pop-up wherein you can view all your budget accounts and create new ones. You will also find any pending invitations to [collaborate](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators)
 on existing budgets here:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F7xNUlD0aiVPy8IMQVtLU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85947c2f-5a10-486e-b42d-7c1dd48b8c37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4daba3a1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#what-are-some-use-cases-for-creating-multiple-budget-accounts)

What are some use cases for creating multiple budget accounts?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some users find it helpful to separate budget accounts by different aspects of their life. For example, you may have your own personal budget, a shared budget with a partner and a budget for your business.

Some developers may also find it useful to create a separate budget account as a developer sandbox account!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#how-does-collaborating-with-others-work)

How does collaborating with others work?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each budget account has one admin user whose paid subscription supports the budget account. Once this budget account is created, they can invite unlimited collaborators to this account.

A budget account is an isolated budget with its own transactions, accounts, categories, tags, etc, and its data cannot be accessed by another budget account.

A user who is only collaborating on other users' budget accounts does not need their own paid subscription. At any time, collaborators may create their own budget, thereby becoming an admin user and requiring a paid subscription. A collaborator who creates their first budget automatically receives a free 14-day trial.

To learn more about collaborators, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators)
.

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

*   [How do I create a new budget account?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#how-do-i-create-a-new-budget-account)
    
*   [What are some use cases for creating multiple budget accounts?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#what-are-some-use-cases-for-creating-multiple-budget-accounts)
    
*   [How does collaborating with others work?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/unlimited-budget-accounts#how-does-collaborating-with-others-work)
    

Was this helpful?

# Accounts | Knowledge Base

In Lunch Money, you can add and keep track of any account or asset, whether it's a bank account, a loyalty card, a physical wallet, crypto, real estate or a vehicle! Accounts are added and managed via the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page, whether synced or manually-managed.

Synced bank accounts are added via the Plaid's Link flow and will allow for automatic syncing of transactions and balances, while manually-managed accounts and assets are added using the manual creation form within Lunch Money and will require manual transaction entry.

It’s important to take into consideration whether an account is synced or manually-managed, as some actions and settings for synced accounts are not available for manually-managed accounts, and vice-versa.

circle-exclamation

**Managing accounts or assets in multiple currencies?**

Make sure to add those currencies under ‘Supported Currencies’ via the Settings page, to ensure that those are available as an option when editing transaction amounts and account balances.

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts#adding-accounts)

*   [How to link a cryptocurrency wallet for automatic syncing](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
    
*   [How to set up manually-managed crypto assets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-set-up-manually-managed-crypto-assets)

# Tags | Knowledge Base

Tags are a great way to further organize transactions beyond categories. Tags are more flexible than categories as they tend to be more specific and associated with less transactions than a category would. Unlike categories, a transaction can be associated with multiple tags! Tags can also be color-coded to help with organization and easier visualization on the Transactions page.

The Tags page is where you can manage all of your tags, from creating new ones, editing existing ones, deleting, or archiving.

Some uses of tags may include tracking transactions associated with a specific event (eg. birthday party, wedding, etc.), a trip (eg. Brazil 2023, Italy 2024, etc.) or a particular project (eg. kitchen renovation, bedroom makeover).

* * *

# Multicurrency | Knowledge Base

Lunch Money supports over 160 global currencies, so whether you're managing expenses across multiple countries, traveling internationally, or dealing with foreign investments, you can seamlessly track everything in one place without the hassle of manual conversions or separate apps.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#primary-currency)

Primary currency


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The primary currency will be the currency in which all totals and summaries are displayed in Lunch Money. For example, if your primary currency is USD and you have transactions in EUR and CAD, your budget summaries, account summaries, charts, and all other totals will show up as USD.

Typically, this is the currency that you instinctively think in, or the currency that most of your money is in. You can change your primary currency at any time from the Settings page.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#supported-currencies)

Supported currencies


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you have more than one currency enabled, all editable amount fields in Lunch Money will display a dropdown. The currencies that are listed in this dropdown are based on the list of supported currencies that you've enabled.

To add or remove supported currencies, head over to the [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page and locate the '_Details_' section. Under '_Supported Currencies_' you can click to add new currencies, or can remove currencies by clicking the 'x' next to them:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F3XFrJTx5ZcIiLuL4OeJU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5936a9b0-4e71-4547-9dbf-dc643f4e3549&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ed2b816&sv=2)

circle-info

Note that you don’t have to have a currency in your list of supported currencies for it to show up in Lunch Money. For instance, if you had EUR as a supported currency at one point and you have a few transactions in euros, and you decide to remove EUR from your list of supported currencies, your euro transactions will not be affected. The only thing that will be affected is the currency dropdown when adding or editing amounts.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#currency-exchange-rate)

Currency exchange rate


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lunch Money uses historic currency exchange rates to calculate amounts in your primary currency. Every day, we fetch the latest exchange rates for over 160 different currencies. This ensures that a transaction made in Feb 2019 and a transaction made in Aug 2019 both reflect the true currency exchange rate of that day.

If for some reason, we did not get a currency exchange rate for a particular rate, we will fall back on the closest day’s exchange rate.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#my-currency-isnt-listed)

My currency isn't listed!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a currency that you’d like to see listed, let us know at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://support.lunchmoney.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9cefe9ececf3eee8dcf0e9f2fff4f1f3f2f9e5b2fdecec)
 and we will do our best to get it added!

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Primary currency](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#primary-currency)
    
*   [Supported currencies](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#supported-currencies)
    
*   [Currency exchange rate](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#currency-exchange-rate)
    
*   [My currency isn't listed!](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/multicurrency#my-currency-isnt-listed)

circle-check

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#before-you-start)

Before You Start


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you can start budgeting in Lunch Money, you need to set up two key elements:

1.  **Categories**: If you need some help, check out our [guide on budgeting categoriesarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/how-to-choose-the-right-budget-categories)
     here. Make sure you have both expense and income categories set up (categories with the '[Treat as Income](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#treat-as-income)
    ' property enabled). You can also check out [a video tutorial herearrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YxqBsqYIdP4&list=PL7uAIYDX_Pk0i8p1X9Qtfh1OVfKPe8hTl&index=15)
    .
    
2.  **Transactions**: Lunch Money supports a number of ways to import transactions, such as [automatic bank syncing](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports)
     or [uploading a CSV or PDF](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv)
    .
    

Lunch Money supports budgeting by category, with each transaction assigned to only one category. This makes it easy to keep track of where your money is going.

Once you have your **categories** set up and **transactions** imported, you'll have a clear picture of how much you've spent and how much you still have left.

Having both pieces in place is the best way to ensure your budget works like it should!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FfdFcFSg58oDKRelXoV7I%252FYouTube%2520SM%2520Posts%2520%2830%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29616f76-27f0-4a28-a56e-d8727ce050a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb25caf1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#setting-your-budgeting-period)

Setting Your Budgeting Period


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At the top of the Budget page, you'll see a time period. By default, this is set to monthly, meaning your budget resets on the 1st of every month. In the screenshot below, you can see the budget is set from Saturday, Feb 1 to Friday, Feb 28:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXe24pHpdR8lS3PXFhikqf35YY2-nEAJN5wVLHkSWF0VxCt0Jmx9Rs-jxPJOe4URrzXoTg7vP5EHuGoYOiyWbcztxsJeRdK7nc_SzkY4qLe8oNUSL9JNhKayL6k6tgnMYxe6vuh_Qg%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e27c21f&sv=2)

But maybe that doesn't fit your life? **For example:**

*   Do you get paid twice a month?
    
*   Want to budget weekly instead of monthly?
    
*   Would you prefer to start your budget on the 15th of every month?
    

No problem! Lunch Money lets you choose your own budgeting period.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#how-do-i-configure-my-custom-budgeting-period)

How do I configure my custom budgeting period?

To set up your budgeting period, click on the ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2) button in the upper right corner of your Budget page and look for this option:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FiTeLQfabEsernwxQRtfo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d6d30f5-41bf-472d-9029-84457dc474b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a561cbc&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#what-does-starting-on-mean)

What does "Starting On" mean?

Let's say you get paid every 2 weeks and want your budget to reset with your payday. Just choose the date of your first paycheck as your starting date. This date becomes the starting point for all future budget periods.

**For example:**

*   If your start date is Jan 1, 2025, and you are budgeting bi-weekly, your budgeting periods would be as follows:
    
    *   Jan 1-14, Jan 15-28, Jan 29- Feb 11…
        
    
*   If your start date is Jan 2, 2025:
    
    *   Jan 2-15, Jan 16-29, Jan 30-Feb 12…
        
    

circle-check

Tip: Want your budget to restart at the end of each month? Choose the last day of any month (such as April 30 or May 31) as your starting date.

triangle-exclamation

**Important:** If you change your budgeting period (like the number of days or the start date), all your old budgets will be deleted. This is because Lunch Money applies the new setting to your entire budget history, and it won't adjust past budgets to fit. Make sure you’re ready before making the switch!

Now that your budget period is set, it's time to decide whether you'll budget with money you have or money you're expecting.

**Watch for a visual more with this tutorial:**

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#managing-your-income-settings)

Managing Your Income Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ask yourself this: will you budget with money you expect to receive, or only with money that's already in your account? Lunch Money lets you choose– including a flexible option that uses whichever amount is larger. This helps you plan in a way that fits your real life.

You can manage your income settings in the 'Other Settings' section of ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2). You have three choices:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FRxufTHjVg8PtAXBIMU22%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a678c0b-639b-44ec-b110-56daff046da7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21a117cd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#expected-income)

**Expected Income**

Plan your budget using the money you think you will receive during this period (from the 'Expected' column).

*   **Good for:** People with steady, predictable income like regular paychecks; those who want to plan ahead for the full period
    
*   **Why you might not want this:** Your actual income might be less than expected, leading to overspending
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FQV2xAHk2GjwirYMz3Tb1%252FBudgeted%2520Income.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De50b5b94-e87c-46d9-9bd3-74161e25c345&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64e83f3b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#actual-income-activity)

**Actual Income Activity**

Budget only with the money you’ve already received during this period (from the 'Activity' column)

*   **Good for:** Living paycheck to paycheck; variable or unpredictable income; freelancers or gig workers; anyone who prefers the security of budgeting only with money in hand
    
*   **Why you might not want this:** Can't plan ahead for the full period; might need to adjust your budget multiple times as income arrives
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FWJsnBcvNMa0FIaN7yWDQ%252FActual%2520Income%2520Activity.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc694d3e2-38f7-468b-9408-f3e9803a1674&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25ab8708&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#larger-of-expected-and-actual-income-activity)

**Larger of Expected and Actual Income Activity**

Uses whichever is bigger– your expected income or what you've actually received.

*   **Good for:** People who get a regular paycheck plus extra money sometimes (like overtime, commission or bonuses); anyone who wants to start planning their budget right away but have more money to budget if they earn more than expected
    
*   **Why you might not want this:** If you often earn less than expected, you might overspend; can be confusing since your “available to budget” might change during the month
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fv7U94OgzsQh6mfk2M2aB%252FLarger%2520of%2520Budgeted%2520or%2520Actual.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87ccb1ed-453c-4b45-a45a-cfc515b17994&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58fc4dcc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#defining-rollover-options)

Defining Rollover Options


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Depending on your budgeting strategy, you'll want to define your rollover options.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#whats-a-rollover)

What's a Rollover?

A rollover is when money from one budget period carries forward into the next. This can happen in two ways:

1.  **For individual categories:** When you don't spend all the money budgeted for a category (like Restaurants), that leftover amount can roll forward. Same goes for overspending– if you spend more than budgeted, that deficit can carry forward too. These amounts show up in the 'Available' column.
    

*   **Leftover money example: Budgeted ($150) - Activity ($100) = Available ($50).** The money you budgeted, but did not spend:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfByeTfsAZSnImQD2ZhwmFuC50n09GZd0317JPQatu0GNkkarJ-srEXrB8tkZSK9ybdrPtqYJG67p4FjbmQmwrAJOneDl3Tefa0Ys6FCMFSQ1zFgpEMSvIcNTaQm7eKX4cyiRih_A%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51ce4b24&sv=2)

*   **Overspending example: Budgeted ($50) - Activity ($100) = Available (-$50).** The money you spent, but did not budget for:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcEzL9s9hTRF1Z9FkmPZ-KoDpky6CwV_N-nLXi8MT6g6PBGdJZUzsTZsv_EAjQrMJK1oGR1LA-CgcZIWPZeIV60qhiDoJb-1KbmVsu0aa2gzAyjQA9lJGpnKe2Ud-ouvckt83eL%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=739351fa&sv=2)

*   **For your overall budget (the "general pool"):** The general pool is your total money available to budget across all categories. If you don't assign all your income to categories, that "Left to Budget" (positive) or “Overbudgeted” (negative) amount can roll into the next period's general pool. This gives you more flexibility in future months.
    
    ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdv4vlzqZsFYytBhJoikTrxzRuac2_54SRRVRDonMoNa88hYzsucdpamTDl8Nl6mJNMpBWNd4rSfrQ7bMSnPBQbwPuQhkhtpQxEE0qEK6i47lgGR1lwsenm1U6exLikjirKcDwY%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e5cc537&sv=2)
    
    For example, if you budgeted all but $410.00 of your income in January, you could roll over the remaining $410.00 to be used in February instead.
    

By default, rollovers are turned off when you first start. Depending on your budgeting strategy, you'll want to define your rollover options. Let's explore how they work!

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#rollover-options-for-the-general-pool-income)

Rollover Options for the General Pool (Income)

In Lunch Money, all income goes into the general pool — this is your full amount of money available to budget for the period. Imagine it like a big pool of cash 💸.

**It includes:**

*   This period's income (activity or budgeted value, depending on your [Income settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#managing-your-income-settings)
    )
    
*   Leftover money (in the 'Available' column) from expense categories that rolled into the general pool
    
*   'Left to Budget' or 'Overbudgeted' amounts from previous periods (if general pool rollovers are on)
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F7b6gqd8m8irk1VXe1s2e%252FGeneral%2520Pool.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D934ae954-c612-4ddd-bdff-d3d96693b91a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e5dba44&sv=2)

General pool rollovers are off by default. When you enable them, any 'Left to Budget' or 'Overbudgeted' amounts will automatically roll over to the next period. There are no rollover options for individual income categories.

chevron-right![Toggle ON](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Ftg8f9mDwfa054WPDh8j9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3d42a23-26b9-4da3-9667-810865510e12&width=87&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15ee2b99&sv=2) **Reasons to Turn ON General Pool Rollovers**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#reasons-to-turn-on-general-pool-rollovers)

1.  You are using a [zero-basedarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/zero-based-budgeting-simplified)
     or [envelope budgeting methodarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/beginners-guide-to-envelope-budgeting-cash-stuffing)
    . These budgeting methods encourage you to create buffers in your budget by carrying forward savings into future budget periods.
    
2.  Useful if your income fluctuates. If your [income changes from month to montharrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/budgeting-for-irregular-incomes)
    , rollovers can help smooth out lean periods by letting you carry forward unspent income from higher-earning months.
    

chevron-right![Toggle OFF](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FunmpSnE3spVbJkreunXg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96e7692d-1b7f-423a-a7d8-b420052e8a4e&width=87&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7066bc6&sv=2) **Reasons to Turn OFF General Pool Rollovers**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#reasons-to-turn-off-general-pool-rollovers)

1.  You are budgeting a set amount every period. If you plan to budget a specific amount each period, say $5,000, regardless of your income, general pool rollovers will only confuse the situation.
    
2.  You prefer a clean slate each month. Some people find it easier to start fresh each budget period without a carryover.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#how-to-turn-on-general-pool-rollovers)

**How to turn on General Pool Rollovers**

1.  Go to ![Budget Settings](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FppBIS3NFQe6hqT5FIIKS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb702a6d-2dc5-4434-a801-85765eb877c3&width=215&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80be418b&sv=2)
    
2.  Find "General Pool Rollover Setting"
    
3.  Toggle on the "Rollover 'Left to Budget' and 'Overbudgeted' amounts":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FNYed3voS4ShPWzgb4wBx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0c90bcb-0933-4997-9602-f13a6eaba103&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9a98b5d&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Add New" under "Adjustments History":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FyKZYCTFBPCiEhpLw8nkk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43301f30-ffa2-4a09-aceb-d9a1e36753cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c537a2c6&sv=2)

1.  Enter your starting balance and date, then click on "Add adjustment". If you're starting fresh as of the current period, set the start date to the first day of the period:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FzLMNBjIGg7uQMZS9wn9q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4526e9a7-3698-4151-8e00-2f920e5b6873&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=936405f5&sv=2)

1.  To finalize, click on "Save changes" at the bottom
    

circle-check

If you wish to start budgeting with an existing available amount (i.e., total cash in your bank accounts), you can set that amount in the 'Reset balance to' field. [Learn more here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/faq#can-i-budget-using-my-total-bank-balance-instead-of-just-recent-income)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#rollover-options-for-expense-categories)

Rollover Options for Expense Categories

Think of your expense categories like jars of money. Let’s say you put $200 in your "Food" jar for May, but you only spent $160. What should happen to that leftover $40?

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FIwFR77jCaUVRKHyr5BLM%252FRollover%2520Options.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da56d6a53-868a-40a1-ab8a-596625e1f522&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b88a849e&sv=2)

In Lunch Money, each category can have its own rollover setting. You have three options:

*   **Rollover to the same category**: Any leftover money stays in the same jar.
    
    *   **Good for:** setting up a sinking fund for [large future expensesarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/how-to-budget-for-periodic-expenses)
        , following an [envelope budgetingarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/blog/beginners-guide-to-envelope-budgeting-cash-stuffing)
         approach, or making up for overspending.
        
    *   **Why you might not want this:** You don’t want overspending in one month to affect your next month or you want to move your leftover money somewhere else.
        
    
*   **Rollover to the general pool**: Leftover money is moved to the general pool for future use.
    
    *   **Good for:** Flexible budgeting. Extra money isn’t locked to one category; you can use it wherever you need it in the following period. It also keeps your categories tidy.
        
    *   **Why you might not want this:** You want to track your progress in a specific category. If you’re saving up for something big, the extra money won't stay in that jar.
        
    
*   **Do nothing**: The leftover money disappears, and you'll start fresh next month.
    
    *   **Good for:** Simple tracking with no carry-over.
        
    *   **Why you might not want this:** You don’t want under- or overspent money to “vanish” next period.
        
    

circle-check

**Tip:** We recommend either rolling over to the same category or the general pool, as you don’t lose leftover money! If you’re unsure of which option to choose, you can start by rolling over money into the general pool. Also, remember that you can [move money](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-4-budgeting#moving-money-between-categories)
 that’s been rolled over to any other category later — it’s never stuck in one place!

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#category-rollover-example)

Category Rollover Example

Here’s what this looks like in action. Below is a snapshot of three budget categories at the end of January, including their rollover options.

**January budget**

Category

Budgeted

Spent

Leftover

Rollover Option

Restaurants

$200

$210

\-$10

Same category

Cafes

$100

$80

$20

General pool

Transportation

$80

$65

$15

General pool

*   **Restaurants:** You overspent by $10, so that category will start with $-10 in February
    
*   **Cafes and Transportation:** You had a total of $35 left over. Since both categories roll into the general pool, the general pool will start with $35 in February.
    

So, for February, your "Restaurants" category will start with a $10 deficit, and your general pool will include any unbudgeted income (including income rolled over from January), and the $35 rolled over from the "Cafes" and "Transportation" categories.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#how-to-turn-on-category-rollovers)

**How to turn on Category Rollovers**

1.  Click on the > icon for the category you want to set
    
2.  Find 'Rollover Options'
    
3.  Choose the rollover option you want for this particular category
    
    ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdNMGu5INit658L198PrCgWC7GsHCgEGj6Nf4jqeluXnxHOBOhGUPTYRtL7PfPrZS_Len6XN-_O3tPqL8g3RuKAc50auiA1_p5M7lu_-eihalfY8bfvOr4BFrSf-u6CGkfkiJNVQg%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=316719f1&sv=2)
    
4.  If applicable, pick a date to start the rollover from. If you're just starting your budget, use the first day of the current budgeting period.
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#enabling-category-group-budgeting)

Enabling Category Group Budgeting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Category groups](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups)
 let you organize related categories together (like grouping Airfare, Hotel and Dining under "Travel"). If you use category groups, you can choose to:

*   Budget by individual categories
    
*   Budget by category group
    

If you budget by category group, you can set one budget amount and rollover option for the whole group. The group acts as one combined jar– all the money rolls up to the group level, and rollovers happen at the group level. You'll still be able to budget different amounts for each subcategory within the group's total.

This works well if you know how much you want to spend in an overall category, such as travel, but don't care about exact amounts for each subcategory, like airfare, hotel, dining, car rental..

Setting a category group budget is optional. If you don't set one, the group budget automatically becomes the sum of all subcategory budgets. You might want to:

*   **Skip setting a group budget** if you want it to simply total your subcategory budgets
    
*   **Set a larger group budget** if you want extra flexibility to move money between subcategories without having to adjust individual budgets
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#how-to-turn-on-category-group-budgeting)

How to turn on Category Group Budgeting

1.  In the Outflow table, click the arrow (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FF2hpwa2Xsyb1m7Vbh0EH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0090dc4-679d-492c-8ffe-f74ce8561949&width=37&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39f1d421&sv=2)) to the right of any category group
    
2.  In the 'Edit Category' panel, scroll down to "Category Group Budgeting"
    
3.  Toggle the option labeled "Enable Category Group Budgeting":
    
    ![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf0mskH3Jg9x6OuCXWBICiTOD-73EWmPSxSrFiy2lfU3gVQhbB4LSbrElpg0Zeqhdj40uMAqX2Rbh8mAJ1SHdoErDOLv0bEjScvRB7cS3SDkSWAVQVh4i1oe1aiXB-5PbPXEvJE%3Fkey%3DsuIPa4HPoah-nCtJhzHxELxU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1da6e160&sv=2)
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#final-setup-checklist)

Final Setup Checklist


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you start using your budget, make sure you’ve covered everything:

*   check
    
    Set up your income and expense categories
    
*   check
    
    Import your transactions into Lunch Money
    
*   check
    
    [Choose your budgeting period](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#setting-your-budgeting-period)
     (default: monthly)
    
*   check
    
    [Select how your income will be handled](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#managing-your-income-settings)
     (budgeted, actual, or larger of)
    
*   check
    
    [Decide on general pool rollovers](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#rollover-options-for-the-general-pool-income)
     (default: off)
    
*   check
    
    [Choose rollover options for each expense category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#rollover-options-for-expense-categories)
     (default: do nothing)
    
*   check
    
    [Enable category group budgeting](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-2-setting-up-your-budget#enabling-category-group-budgeting)
     if needed (optional)
    

All set? Let's explore your Budget page! 👇

# The Basics of Recurring | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**What are recurring items?**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#what-are-recurring-items)
    
    *   [Why should I track recurring items?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#why-should-i-track-recurring-items)
        
    
*   [**Properties of recurring items**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#properties-of-recurring-items)
    
    *   [Categories](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#categories)
        
    *   [Status](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#status)
        
    *   [Active period](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#active-period)
        
    *   [Account](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#account)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#what-are-recurring-items)

What are recurring items?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recurring items represent transactions that reoccur on a regular cadence. Recurring items can represent both income and expenses, with either fixed or fluctuating amounts, and would generally occur on a regular cadence with predictable dates for the payments (eg. twice a month, every 6 months, annually, etc.).

Examples of **recurring expenses** include a monthly streaming subscription, monthly utility bills, a quarterly insurance payment or an annual gym membership.

Examples of **recurring income** include your salary, annual bonus, or interest income.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#why-should-i-track-recurring-items)

Why should I track recurring items?

It’s useful to set up recurring items to foresee expected expenses and income. Setting up a recurring item allows you to track all future and past occurrences of that recurring transaction. This could be useful in a number of ways:

*   If there is a bill you haven’t paid in a while, you will be able to refer to the recurring items to detect discrepancies and prevent fines or having the provided service canceled.
    
*   If you want to cut down on spending, recurring expenses will typically be the first place to look since canceling a monthly subscription can save you a lot of money in the long run!
    
*   If you’d like to figure out your "minimum cost of living", i.e. if you didn't spend a single dime on day-to-day expenses, how much would you need just to survive (rent, utilities, subscriptions, etc.).
    
*   If you’d like to look at your stats and trends disregarding recurring items (eg. to see your most expensive transactions each month while excluding rent from the analysis).
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#properties-of-recurring-items)

Properties of recurring items


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Beyond the basic data for recurring items (eg. merchant name, estimated billing date, repeating cadence), there are a few other helpful properties that are very important to keep in mind!

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#categories)

Categories

By default, you will be able to set categories for recurring items. This is useful if you would like to be able to budget for the recurring items and have the recurring transactions reflected in category totals. In addition, the assigned category is used as an indication for whether a recurring item is treated as income or expense.

If you use an [Income](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories#treat-as-income)
 category, the recurring item will be treated as income, while if you use an Expense (non-Income) category, the recurring item will be treated as an expense.

The option to “Allow categories for recurring items” is managed via the [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page, and while enabled by default, it can be disabled by clicking on the toggle to turn it off. Disabling the categories will mean that all recurring items and the associated transactions are managed in a separate category called “Recurring Items” and cannot be budgeted for.

If the setting for allowing recurring categories is disabled (or if a recurring item is uncategorized), then the recurring item will be considered an income or expense based exclusively on the notation (+/-) of the transaction amount.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FVMym4PFyxJJcGKJZME2U%252FRecurring%2520Item%2520-%2520Setting%2520Categories.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc88d5061-8fc6-4808-b483-7e4aaef3880c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7de2db51&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#status)

Status

Recurring items will always show one of three possible status indicators, visible on the far-right of the row:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MAEfVKXN_9lQ8WZFqZh%252F-MAFCU1kkvxn2R1wCIdK%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-06-20%2520at%25201.31.10%2520PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daaf9e708-026d-463c-b41f-099eddaf77af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=745b1497&sv=2)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FkYAUnuhR7HWZcvzpi3Vc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db904e7cf-c70e-4103-8763-0a26ff077cba&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7d0e5eb&sv=2) The **green** **checkmark** represents that a transaction has been linked to the expected payment for the current month. If this transaction occurred on a date different from the expected billing date, then the “Billing Day” will update to reflect the actual transaction's date.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FKVShhVhUw5LVZeabne11%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd5a1033-2588-4335-b275-1fe5e11642ad&width=43&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e49c0a8a&sv=2) The **orange warning** represents that a recurring item’s expected billing date has passed, but no transaction has been linked. This indicates a potential issue that you should look into! Some possibilities include:

*   The payment hadn’t occurred
    
*   The payment occurred but the transaction wasn’t added within Lunch Money
    
*   The transaction exists within Lunch Money but wasn’t linked to the recurring item
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FRYVPTXU9CXPoWiVFuaPb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa18ed85-0858-4e0b-9df4-91e8d2b705bc&width=41&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=596babba&sv=2) The **grey clock** represents that a recurring item's expected billing date is in the future, so there's no need to worry about its status at this point.

It’s important to keep in mind that the status icon in the table only represents the item occurrence associated with that row’s billing day. This means that if the current month’s expected payment has been linked, but last month is missing, the status icon will still show the green checkmark.

To check the status of previous expected payments, you can either switch to a specific month’s view using the arrows next to the month’s name above the table, or you can click on the arrow to the far-right of the recurring item’s row to open the ‘Edit Recurring Item’ panel. In the panel, you will get a quick view of the status for the expected payment for the previous period, current period and next period:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcOKZwIFO281efJoUALVbURTvfbAliV3rta48cwlTnEh4Q8EBVVVE3gcsCCSfOBWMyfAYR4Ca0CMHX9wTU9js6dYOs8RxegvT2R15uVF4DBZi2PvLOuXsChui6sY16BzJui97kDxun4BEdDwObJr0nBm2I%3Fkey%3D_VQCALLf2VI72xILJ2wvDA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a76b6ad2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#active-period)

Active period

When creating or editing recurring items, it’s possible to set the active period. The active period defines when the recurring item starts and ends. This is an optional property, and you can choose to set a start date, end date, both start and end dates, or neither. A recurring item without a defined active period will be expected for all months.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FkdTBVw2b8fXFzh51a7SR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1652e9aa-40bd-4e8c-9394-12db4764623d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6faaf1bf&sv=2)

For example, if you started a new Netflix subscription in January 2023, then you can set the start date of that recurring item to be January 2023. This means that the recurring item will not be expected in December 2022 or earlier.

On the flip side, if you terminated your Netflix subscription in June 2023, then you can set the end date of that recurring item to be June 2023. This means that the recurring item will not show up in July 2023 or later.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#account)

Account

When setting up a recurring item, you can also select a specific account to associate with the recurring item. The field “Paid from account” will be set to “Cash transaction” by default, yet can be changed by clicking on it and selecting one of the accounts in the dropdown menu.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FENzbwk4wih1GAUR2qx34%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0083a6f3-697d-4bb2-bee6-6bec00fde8af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba9d4e08&sv=2)

circle-info

If you leave it as “Cash transaction”, the associated rule that is created for the recurring item will match transactions by Payee, Amount and Date, regardless of the account on which the transaction occurred. If you specify an Account, then the associated rule will also match for that Account. To learn more about recurring rules, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/recurring-items/the-basics-of-recurring#integration-with-rules)
.

Last updated 1 year ago
