# Collaborators | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**How to invite a collaborator**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-invite-a-collaborator)
    
*   [**How to tell which collaborator added which account**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-tell-which-collaborator-added-which-account)
    
*   [**How to set up email notifications for collaborators**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-set-up-email-notifications-for-collaborators)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#collaborate-on-a-budget-with-your-partner-on-lunch-money)

**Collaborate on a budget with your partner on Lunch Money!**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get started, you will need to create a budget account with a personal Lunch Money account. As the admin of the shared budget account, you'll be inviting others to collaborate through their own personal accounts. That means you’ll be managing the same budget with the same bank accounts, assets and other settings, but each through their own account and login. When collaborating, you’ll also be able to [see and track who linked which account](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-tell-which-collaborator-added-which-account)
 and who added which transaction.

You can collaborate with any number of people on a budget, as the price you pay is per budget, not per person. Only the admin of the budget requires an active Lunch Money subscription, meaning that a collaborator can manage the shared budget without the need for their own subscription.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-invite-a-collaborator)

**How to invite a collaborator**

To invite someone to collaborate on a budget, go to the [_Settings_arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page, and under the _Collaborators_ card, enter their email address and click on "Invite".

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F9HJXYVej2Wi6lqjUw8IH%252FCollaborators%2520-%2520Invite.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29727d65-a704-4199-afd9-606541f4d49d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=728bcbb4&sv=2)

Your invitee will receive the following invitation by email:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F6D5fuogfXDGfrE01q95V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16e1a9a5-3928-425e-b0bc-59d10eefe642&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d25c4fa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-tell-which-collaborator-added-which-account)

How to tell which collaborator added which account

When a new account is added, whether synced or manually created, there is a label that will let you know which collaborator it was was added by. The 'Linked by' label is displayed with the account information in the 'Edit Account' panel:

1.  Open the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page
    
2.  Locate the relevant account and click anywhere in that row to open the 'Edit Account' panel
    
3.  At the bottom of the _Account Information_ section, you will find the 'Linked by' details, as well as the date on which the account was created:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FeBRPYYHw5eZeXXu28KqN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0dfad23-ac9e-4da4-ae81-a59b12f3a143&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=756141c8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/collaborators#how-to-set-up-email-notifications-for-collaborators)

How to set up email notifications for collaborators

All email notifications for automatic imports are managed by rules. You can see the list of email rules on the Rules page, [herearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=email)
.

Email rules are automatically created for budget admins when synced accounts are added, yet collaborators will not receive email notifications for existing synced accounts unless new email rules are set up.

circle-info

Email rules will automatically be set up for the collaborators for any new accounts they add.

A collaborator can set up new email rules via the [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 page:

1.  Click on "Add a new rule" to open the '_Create transaction rule_' panel on the right
    
2.  Under "If..", set the condition to "In account" and then select the relevant account
    
3.  Under "Then..", set the action to "Send me an email"
    
4.  To save the new rule, click on "Create & Apply"
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FjRPcum5EktvBO41GftXf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc892e8b3-5b37-4ef3-8d4f-4e81f0f7cfd0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=426b1498&sv=2)

Last updated 8 months ago

# Budget 🆕 | Knowledge Base

At Lunch Money, we don’t prescribe a specific budgeting method — instead, we provide all the different tools and flexibility you need to budget your way!

* * *

If you're getting started with budgeting in Lunch Money for the first time, we recommend going through the complete Budgeting Guide here:

[bookGuide: Budgeting with Lunch Money](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/budgeting/step-1-intro-to-budgeting)

# Transaction Enhancements | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Categories**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#categories)
    
    *   [How to quickly add or change transaction category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-quickly-add-or-change-transaction-category)
        
    
*   [**Tags**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#tags)
    
    *   [How to assign tags to transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-assign-tags-to-transactions)
        
    *   [How to remove tags from transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-remove-tags-from-transactions)
        
    
*   [**Attachments**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#attachments)
    
    *   [How to upload an attachment](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-upload-an-attachment)
        
    *   [How to view an attachments](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-view-an-attachment)
        
    *   [How to delete an attachment](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-delete-an-attachment)
        
    *   [How to rename an attachment](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-rename-an-attachment)
        
    *   [How to download an attachment](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-download-an-attachment)
        
    

* * *

In addition to the obligatory transaction data (Date, Payee, Amount and Account), transactions can be enhanced with categories, tags, and attachments. These features help you enrich your spending data and give you more power over how you sort and review your data within Lunch Money!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#categories)

Categories


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Categories are set up on the [Categories arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
page, and are an essential way to organize your transactions. Categories also dictate how associated transactions will be treated throughout Lunch Money. To learn more about category properties, please [see herearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories)
.

A transaction can only be assigned one category, and uncategorized transactions are highly discouraged! The category cell for uncategorized transactions will appear in red:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FUFU2wqOuCra3gtW2nlTwUZzGAw1dSInbfeZflPcR-qGgqzKog_NwcmqUZNNnJEg95WslkQHsM9tJ3d-7mtoN0sV1Y2oum7NArMYzmcC_kJpZPZUuIRVN9iGvQp9FhayfJHwW_5jL-DjmeWpeoAaTlhc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45f7d04a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-quickly-add-or-change-transaction-category)

**How to quickly add or change transaction category**

The category of a transaction can be added or changed directly within the table view on the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Locate the transaction in the table and click on the relevant cell in the Category column
    
2.  Once clicked, a dropdown menu will appear with all of your active categories
    
3.  Scroll in the dropdown to locate the desired category, or type to search
    
4.  Click on a category name to set it and it will automatically be saved to the transaction
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FGqTZ3Oz9q40zvybeqWfCHsTqHI1T99VdzcAk3zy32QuGA0RnDOEuXBp1V3WzlnmgHEh74_OWQ6j-FxtpJQC5Cj1KWztGRiXe2htyjsADE3TFx7n6c0JhmVFEIvXw2mYD7VWXSfUkqjhrSGxLhKyVoSo&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c56501c7&sv=2)

If you type to search for a category that you don’t already have set up, the option “Add category” will appear. Clicking on that will open a confirmation dialog to set up a brand new category. Once confirmed, the category is created on the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
 page and the new category is automatically applied to the transaction from which it was created.

circle-exclamation

Please keep in mind that adding a brand new category directly from a transaction will result in the creation of a plain expense category, without any [category propertiesarrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories#category-properties)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#tags)

Tags


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tags are a great way to further organize transactions. Tags are much more flexible to use than categories as they would be more specific and not associated with as many transactions as a category would. Moreover, unlike with categories, a transaction can be associated with multiple tags!

Some uses of tags may include tracking transactions associated with a specific event (eg. birthday party, wedding, etc.), a trip (eg. Brazil 2020, Italy 2021, etc.) or a particular project (eg. kitchen renovation, bedroom makeover).

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-assign-tags-to-transactions)

**How to assign tags to transactions**

If you already have tags set up on the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page, you can easily add tags to any transaction via the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Locate the Tags column and hover the mouse cursor over the cell for the relevant transaction row to see an “Add” button appear
    
2.  Click on “Add” and a drop-down menu will appear with all available tags
    
3.  Locate the tag by scrolling through the menu, or search by typing in the search bar
    
4.  Click on a tag to add it to the selection (you can add more than one)
    
5.  To confirm, click on “Done”, or anywhere outside of the dropdown box.
    

All added tags will then be listed in the relevant cell under the Tags column:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FRjXT9LaMV3buDDd_Yf5MfH4HtOto2JHYW3DCqbTTTh1Qpc0rkuGOeL2FPAJWUUM85YLv4ZEoTbQ-AmIHCGuuuoJhdSLLzgLVqC0xLlIjPfNopmilObVjJgm1esZgbAM7nwUfHFDUwDacylHraMcWP0I&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f5dbca6f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-remove-tags-from-transactions)

**How to remove tags from transactions**

If you already have tags assigned transactions, you can remove them from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Locate the transaction and click the arrow on the far right of the row to open the '_Transaction Details_' panel
    
2.  All assigned tags will display under the '_Transaction Tag(s)_' section
    
3.  Click the small "x" icon next to any tag that you wish to remove
    

To confirm the changes, click on "Save Changes" at the bottom

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F78BXprZTKHFZ5cgittYD%252FTags%2520-%2520Remove.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee17191d-ce9c-4aa6-9520-1a3598f7ea97&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2af95794&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#attachments)

Attachments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In some cases, you may have a document (eg. physical receipt, online purchase confirmation, paycheck stub, etc.) that you would like to include for safekeeping. Typical attachment formats are images (eg. PNG, JPG, HEIF, etc.) or text (PDF, Word, etc.).

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-upload-an-attachment)

**How to upload an attachment**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the '_Transaction Details_' panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Scroll down until you see '_Attachments_'
    
4.  Click on "Select Files" and in the dialogue window, choose the file(s) you wish to upload. Alternatively, you can drag-and-drop files directly into the '_Attachments_' area and the upload will initiate immediately.
    

The uploaded files will appear listed with a name, date, and file size.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FKR7MdnsnKoNzoTbC1qZj%252FAttachments%2520-%2520Upload.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D026e4f6f-1093-4cff-b5fc-cb43043a106f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=197b3b56&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-view-an-attachment)

**How to view an attachment**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the '_Transaction Details_' panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Scroll down until you see '_Attachments_'
    
4.  Locate the attachment that you wish to view and click on the file name
    

If the file is an image, it will display in a popup within Lunch Money. If you’d like to see it in full size, click on "Open in new window" to open it in a new window or tab in your browser.

If the file is a PDF, it will typically open in a new window or tab in your browser.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fu1t5XpLVsCBsFvrCdQ45%252FAttachments%2520-%2520View.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36458a8f-2632-4000-81d2-1060bf66f33c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4c0be2c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-delete-an-attachment)

**How to delete an attachment**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the '_Transaction Details_' panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Scroll down until you see '_Attachments'_
    
4.  Locate the attachment that you wish to delete and click on the three dots icon
    
5.  In the menu, click on "Delete"
    
6.  In the confirmation dialog, click on "Yes, delete"
    

The file will be permanently deleted and removed from the attachments list.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FtDywOfgbhih4zrMIGTc0%252FAttachments%2520-%2520Delete.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb511709-922d-46d9-8584-7640e866fe67&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5874fa1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-rename-an-attachment)

**How to rename an attachment**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the '_Transaction Details_' panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Scroll down until you see '_Attachments_'
    
4.  Locate the attachment that you wish to rename and click on the three dots icon
    
5.  In the menu, click on "Edit name"
    
6.  Make the changes in the 'File name' text box, and click "Save".
    

The name change will be saved and immediately reflected in the attachments list.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FlbrrNdJH3tXLkTEKptgk%252FAttachments%2520-%2520Rename.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e3e127f-3ba2-457c-8ba9-4c3131fa8e96&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34b57a01&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#how-to-download-an-attachment)

**How to download an attachment**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the "Transaction Details" panel on the right side of the screen
    
3.  Scroll down until you see '_Attachments_'
    
4.  Locate the attachment that you wish to download and click on the three dots icon
    
5.  In the menu, click on "Download"
    

The file will download to your computer, to the folder designated by the browser. It will typically be saved to the "Downloads" folder on your computer.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F1QoUACGPauq1JdXZpQug%252FAttachments%2520-%2520Download.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b42c047-05af-429c-a8a7-12f58ff900f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1575cc28&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Creating Tags | Knowledge Base

Creating new tags is possible from the Tags page, or when creating and updating transactions and rules. If you have a list of tags that you wish to create in advance, it’s easier to add them all via the Tags page directly. If you wish to create tags on the go, you can do so while creating or updating transactions or rules.

circle-info

Tags created from the Transactions or Rules page will only be created by name. The tags will not have a description or a color assigned. If you wish to add a description or set a color scheme, you can update the tags via the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page afterwards.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**How to create tags via the Tags page**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-tags-page)
    
*   [**How to create tags via the Transactions page**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-transactions-page)
    
    *   [In the transactions table](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#in-the-transactions-table)
        
    *   [In the ‘Transaction Details’ panel](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#in-the-transaction-details-panel)
        
    *   [With a CSV import](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#with-a-csv-import)
        
    
*   [**How to create tags via the Rules page**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-rules-page)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-tags-page)

How to create tags via the Tags page


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page, you can easily add new detailed tags by clicking on the orange button located above the table:

1.  Open the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     page
    
2.  Click on "Add a new tag"
    
3.  In the table, enter a tag name (required) and a description (optional)
    
4.  Click "Add" on the far-right of the row, OR press Enter on the keyboard
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc5JeFMykbEE4LUBjrf_hgjDS0x1QkFzChAPufVvohV4f9dqhyZTuV0Jybl3ointqNdaeYI5G4-_U7WgAP9uMxBqH4u-KUSN2ekAs1rC9DXuVxxho9pCCg52pN5f3oGP-wxgU64DSMObFkAGuWsI2Nu1EY%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80f2de4d&sv=2)

circle-info

If you then wish to set a color scheme for the new tag, click the little gray square to the right. For step-by-step instructions, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-set-a-tags-color-scheme)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-transactions-page)

How to create tags via the Transactions page


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#in-the-transactions-table)

In the transactions table

From the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page, you can add new tags directly from the table by clicking on any empty cell under the ‘Tags’ column and typing a new tag name:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcwINIXYYEre1lyHB6iaBhaHXlug62Li2xqBsk24JY9sEJ-xv1-Mnb3QgfqB6K162Oj0rEiI2YILiIeZ8ZMDLSSMyvTN7GLekvMcmyRA-nU2Gv0KDQtTjY0je9JLN4poygNiEp61U_UZd6zJMqker_B__Va%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd813b52&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#in-the-transaction-details-panel)

In the ‘Transaction Details’ panel

You can also add new tags from the ‘Transaction Details’ panel by clicking into the ‘Transaction Tag(s)’ field and typing a new tag name:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXefHWrQcoZoW9KHzuLHnCxlzouF-nsZX4tx9iM__ecQNQrCzm-FVpxeWTTZkbFAnKUaeD6yUGYaAA3oJ0wF-5iGccrAdvXe2lso7rreHVgsTm3GmKLfva-CdG8ZLqv2DhF358-6h_2iQPR0raPuL4X53kB2%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b934c05&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#with-a-csv-import)

With a CSV import

Tags can also be created when [uploading a CSV filearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/import)
 containing a ‘tags’ column. This means that you can easily upload automatically tagged transactions, whether the tag(s) already exist in Lunch Money or not.

If the tag name in the CSV file doesn’t already exist in your Lunch Money account, a new tag will be created automatically. If the tag name already exists, the transaction will be assigned the existing tag.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfwqMuIlK6nROfy6OQCNmMwlEqZCeKdL1PIS3-CUBDXksfgwrvKddWT2RmktfBOZWqULqNN4p2hmdZrj-7tPM0h7N3cOeg1JKIbOgzAbn3MNx0-5O8zUG5bsJ1j37NABCoqkh0ZxPwUyt89KJYExmIURp0o%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=319acc26&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/creating-tags#how-to-create-tags-via-the-rules-page)

**How to create tags via the Rules page**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 page, when creating and editing rules with the “Add tags” action, you can add a new tag by clicking the ‘Set tags’ field and typing a new tag name:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdYLhC10mSreE2BD0aZrX-7mt1KB2Lmf_a1tbeKy0j3JzVmCh4cI-ZSaPtlFCGkCUqJmj1UxmGimCebcOxmkVvRnnIquaVZLsnrxlWN4aelSzisg4cueWQLv2G_nZVxaDHSA_uCYBMulexQGz-B0uNBm6g%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=636e2c33&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Analyzing Tags | Knowledge Base

Once you’ve started using tags, you can start analyzing your data by filtering your spending according to tags, or generating tag-based reports and graphs. Filtering transactions by tags can be done from the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 or [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page, while the reports are generated using the Query Tool on the [Analyzearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/analyze)
 page.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**How to filter by tags**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-filter-by-tags)
    
    *   [How to quickly view all transactions associated with a tag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-quickly-view-all-transactions-associated-with-a-tag)
        
    *   [How to quick filter transactions for individual tags](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-quick-filter-transactions-for-individual-tags)
        
    *   [Advanced filtering for one or more tags](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#advanced-filtering-for-one-or-more-tags)
        
    
*   [**How to show / hide tags in the Transactions table view**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-show-hide-tags-in-the-transactions-table-view)
    
*   [**How to generate a tag-based report**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-generate-a-tag-based-report)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-filter-by-tags)

How to filter by tags


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-quickly-view-all-transactions-associated-with-a-tag)

How to quickly view all transactions associated with a tag

On the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page, you can easily access a filtered list of all transactions associated with a specific tag by clicking the magnifying glass icon (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfZfyeGDF3a3HnvPxFu8sh0qucZBqeZA8syirY16iXYWD-m0tDh5V7s2hRAtmK59y3bdFEvUQMOS03XHJRTLKS36HH8xXjwb9215jidCPCed-bX4BDqWI38BZdm1ZErblRtr0VjkebBkoCd3Wy9EI-GEXlX%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=40&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8aa3c70&sv=1)):

1.  Open the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     page
    
2.  In the table, locate the tag that you are interested in and click on the magnifying glass icon located on the second last column to the right
    
3.  A pop-up dialog displaying all associated transaction will appear on the screen
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcwq5PcilCKA-k_xZ-UIqBfvOUsl_Xvlvtqf19zE3TxiMATwzPgT3lo7FqH0eCxKwsgCYrH64p7BG9AFQi43lF3JQOpVJh1dKLcacsJmxjUKMEmqyyhrCvtzdqJq1kne0wjGs-6OgtkXfP3_E5LdwXunVUy%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=800f3627&sv=2)

Alternatively, if you'd like a filtered view for a specific time period or to filter by more criteria (eg. combination of tags and categories), you can do so via the filter options on the Transactions page:

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-quick-filter-transactions-for-individual-tags)

How to quick filter transactions for individual tags

If you have transactions with tags in the active table view, you can quickly filter for an individual tag by clicking on the tag name in the table cell. Any transactions that are not associated with that tag will be hidden from view:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeofnhJD35eSjpGrIXOAuT05LAAswc7qpHHTFDWgqq1sX6pMc5e3e7WmqSHrHTJ_A_GPSk8worDco2ubMsp1-5B-52cVjaq5OCdRXcchavVwYKgHMSzK5pmfmWaIHtl4ZIg6B_k7oI_NVpUggutCclxlcc%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9379ca1&sv=2)

circle-info

Keep in mind that this quick filter method will filter for the specific tag within the active viewing period only. If you are currently viewing the month of August, then you will only see the tagged transactions for that period.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#advanced-filtering-for-one-or-more-tags)

Advanced filtering for one or more tags

For more advanced filtering options, such as filtering by multiple tags, filtering by tag and category, or filtering for a custom date range, you can click on 'Filters' to access the Advanced Filter option:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcnb93tSW174A4LlWl7HGYtaUb4BkjXvy1LrSX63OH_X3Rwz3sHHxNK5ihpidjQltP_Yj2195QxWg9AwIRZZqFCjRNR-QBgYls794JK0U7m5-Kfqr5ThW8itmVyJpN1ODh03w-tWtkSjgkBcG3_70zNXCwP%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fff5102c&sv=2)

For example, if you have a tag for a specific trip and wish to filter to see all-time spending in food categories (eg. restaurants and supermarkets), your filter criteria may look like this:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdhZ1wSlMK_9nXEumE7c6lkWr8qX0zwGncQAYK4vTVKSGZJ8RAvOCp5SD9A7lMJXGRHABR1Tj0OAqyQQej6VW0aBN0UY2pu1AE75mJJWN3BeciUzOoDFnOlOdeA7C65xO39ii28pxrXQFiAdzvDmxKBzgur%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d3ad126&sv=2)

For complete instructions on using the Advanced Filter, [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#advanced-filter)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-show-hide-tags-in-the-transactions-table-view)

How to show / hide tags in the Transactions table view


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
 page, you can choose whether to show or hide the 'Tags' column from the table view. For transactions with multiple tags, you can also choose whether to display just the first tag, or all of them.

To access these options, click the 'Options' icon (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeOR9jikLnZmze56nMBJRSukWiEQDV25Y-NSYaJ4MEQw4EloOXkzQgvTZrWysrB7LnvjxdflCnnNyFTc_lAXEOtbZjkLjma6WgGcBV4moIdQPgj24wd-h6GkgxFQ9euvy3sgb2QwPvhjQEm1GrCjs0Gh70%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=44&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ba4f3e6&sv=2)) located above the table to the right:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfX6uWc2wNTZxtPTP6aMW-7FlJVlEut7QKpjwpwH10xrsJEYoit44t01_rQs_Nau_n6atKGz26jLBDeJoZh4d7t4MA-zuzPLg9dOuhqsxopE-8_SyZI9eyfHkjB-fKaPOtiNg-debsL1c8wd2kHL1befnXY%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1199b1a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#how-to-generate-a-tag-based-report)

How to generate a tag-based report


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To better visualize your spending habits and statistics, you can generate tag-based reports, charts, and graphs using the Query Tool on the [Analyzearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/analyze)
 page.

On the top-right above the table, you will find the display options and can change the view by clicking on any of these options at any time:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcK0EdH8FKHZL-gQfutlHTXHhQV-rAiiSWvfkivKqfpO8Q1FVx-HkamHDMg9oM8ALHaEtmPz4Psfg6o0PLB0idrmG7RNUAfDerwrjM2BbfAGZcrWGCDvwNVUaSipiWOx1_jZWGPVboZcZ7aP_bryb8dISbs%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de4ba579&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#set-the-breakdown-option)

Set the breakdown option

To display the tag data in the Query Tool, there are four breakdown options to choose from:

1.  Breakdown by tag will create a report that displays spending per tag.
    
2.  Breakdown by tag/category will create a two-level report that displays spending per tag, with further breakdown for the categories assigned to transactions using the tag.
    
3.  Breakdown by category/tag will create a two-level report that displays spending per category, with further breakdown for any tags assigned to transactions in the category.
    
4.  Breakdown by account/tag will create a two-level report that displays spending per account, with further breakdown for any tags assigned to transactions in the account.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcWxl_EogFwXLAVN-_XjvU7RQLEJtIna63x-bksTtHNPEjuRsn4rDCYkpPq44n3A4rTPBqc2w5Ocf6-x4OHnO32Q6oBmI3z-_hl_u6nJl_4jPhqoU7nLsYuSpMRH8ZpPdYuUl-PWVMA-ZgLaSSmk3TWnNI%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=845bc72&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

The two-level breakdown will only reflect in the tabular report view. For the pie chart, bar graph, line chart, and stacker bar chart, only the first level will display. For example, if you have the breakdown set to “tag/category”, only the “tag” breakdown will be displayed in the charts and graphs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/analyzing-tags#filter-specific-tags)

Filter specific tags

You can also filter to include or exclude certain tags from the report and charts, by clicking the filter icon (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FPzQd0i7j9BcIx0UL5CnM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2aa57640-804d-40f2-9543-930910b4dfe1&width=40&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cccefb09&sv=2)):

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXerGHGQ49Pg57_DRMrUr5oW4PTp6wZYyLvN4p9AJrF35aOFv4Al-ct3FUrsHGh7UkUC8mpl42U4Kh2FnLeBP7Lg_DHG40OPlJYkJgKvecz6xd0WWtEJ48n1uYahfHtijiKmaqXVz6h1pG0_qPwGmqThWXZC%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e56ec202&sv=2)

# Developer API | Knowledge Base

The Lunch Money API was created to enable the user and the community to build rich plug-ins to complement their Lunch Money experience. The Lunch Money developer API is currently in open beta!

For more details and documentation, visit [lunchmoney.devarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.dev/)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/developer-api#how-do-i-create-an-api-access-token)

How do I create an API Access Token?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An API access token is a digital key that authorizes communication with your budgeting account via the API, without requiring that you enter your username and password every time.

To create a new access token, follow these steps:

1.  Go to [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
     by clicking on the gear icon at the top of the page
    
2.  Click on '[Developersarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/developers)
    ' from the menu at the top
    
3.  In the 'New Access Token' card, enter a descriptive label and your reason for creating the API key
    
4.  Click on 'Request new access token':
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F5qMKaWDmcErVaWTPzioK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db810dd40-3186-47bd-bfbd-0ab63f59aad2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c3edc6&sv=2)

1.  Your access token will now display in the 'New Access Token' card. Click on 'Copy':
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FrZpBlGV330xKMvjPWcNt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa41c96e-0fbd-4800-9436-4aa924445955&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=970bed5a&sv=2)

circle-check

Note: access tokens are per budgeting account, so if you have multiple budgeting accounts set up, the access token will only be valid for the budgeting account from which it is created.

All access tokens that you create will be listed in the 'Active Access Tokens' card. Here, you can rename them, check last activity, and revoke them:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F7nPKv5WkOQK2XFEFICX6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c076190-953d-4f7d-bf4d-0159eef00d1b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3f03b4f&sv=2)

Last updated 8 months ago

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We accept a variety of payment methods, including:

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/payment-methods#managing-your-subscription-and-billing-details)

Managing your subscription and billing details


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can view your subscription details, switch plans, view invoices, manage your payment details, and pause or cancel your subscription from the [Billing pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/billing)
 (accessed via "Settings").

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FsOJUj6TvQ4ROOkD3skS0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De657991e-6b92-43f6-863f-f715554e0bb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c54ad8b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/payment-methods#pausing-your-subscription)

Pausing your subscription


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Need to take a break for whatever reason, but don't want us to delete your data? You can pause your subscription indefinitely with the 'Pause my subscription' option, available on the [Billing pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/billing)
 (accessed via "Settings").

When pausing your subscription, you will no longer be charged and a pro-rated credit for unused time will be applied to your account, to be used towards future billing dues. While paused, you will not be able to access the account data. Once you un-pause the subscription, you will be able to get back to using Lunch Money from where you left off.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fi46OeCS4Cnjbav25e0nc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2863e593-2b9a-4f63-8ae6-5e5489f83c96&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a379dfb7&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

Pausing your subscription means giving up your curent plan and locked-in price. When you return and unpause, you'll be able to choose from the plans and pricing available at that time.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/settings/payment-methods#cancelation-and-account-deletion)

Cancelation and account deletion


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can find the option to cancel your subscription and delete your account from the [Billing pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/billing)
 (accessed via "Settings"). If you choose to cancel your subscription, your Lunch Money account and all associated data will be purged and unrecoverable within 48 hours.

For more information, please see [Lunch Money's Terms of Servicearrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/terms)
.

Last updated 4 months ago

# Transaction Types | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Split transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#split-transactions)
    
    *   [How to split transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-split-transactions)
        
    *   [How to unsplit transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-unsplit-transactions)
        
    
*   [**Group transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#group-transactions)
    
    *   [How to group transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-group-transactions)
        
    *   [How to manage an individual transaction within a group](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-manage-an-individual-transaction-within-a-group)
        
    *   [How to add transactions to an existing group](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-add-transactions-to-an-existing-group)
        
    *   [How to ungroup transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-ungroup-transactions)
        
    
*   [**Recurring transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#recurring-transactions)
    
    *   [How to link an existing transaction to a recurring item](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-link-an-existing-transaction-to-a-recurring-item)
        
    *   [How to edit or unlink a transaction from a recurring Item](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-edit-or-unlink-a-transaction-from-a-recurring-item)
        
    *   [How to create a new transaction for a recurring item](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-create-a-new-transaction-for-a-recurring-item)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#split-transactions)

Split transactions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Split transactions are transactions created from a single original transaction, where the original total amount is broken down into two or more parts. Splitting allows for better organization of transactions where the total amount is made up of smaller amounts that need to be categorized individually. Some use cases include:

*   Splitting a big general store purchase into categories (eg. food, hygiene, pets, etc).
    
*   Splitting dinner shared with someone else
    
*   Splitting rent with roommates
    
*   Splitting an lump-sum payment from contractor by project
    

Transactions can be split evenly, in custom amounts, or in equal payments over time.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-split-transactions)

**How to split transactions**

Splitting transactions is done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Click the arrow to the far right of the transaction’s row to open the '_Transaction Detail_s' panel on the right side of the screen.
    
2.  Scroll down to the '_I want to…_' section, and click on the "Split transaction" button.
    
3.  Next, select how you’d like to split the transaction.
    
4.  Review the data and update the details if needed. At the top, you will see the original amount and the total left to split to help you distribute the total. You will not be able to proceed if the split amounts don’t add up to the original amount.
    
5.  Click on "Save changes" to finalize the split action.
    

Each split amount will then appear as a single entry in the Transactions page (eg. if the original amount was $100 and it was split evenly by 2, you will see two transactions for $50 each).

A symbol will appear within the Amount field for each split transaction to indicate that it was split from an original transaction. Hovering over the icon will provide details about the original transaction amount, and all other transactions it was split into.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Flcdkq7L-Tw6HTB6X8JBlsAiP3l4u3Wv8ne3vwb9zlKKUFjP-jm6qvsu6LVzhPlxzUcP6P4KV-K4EQRPHuYigfp0R26t051yEhBviOb45QEsQHvnGZUZPU9pavMz6Uq9Bzixfg6cEcBGCJ65q9WK0Tvw&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e10cd4d2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-unsplit-transactions)

**How to unsplit transactions**

Splitting transactions is done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Click on the Amount field of any of the split transactions that you would like to merge back together. This will open the '_Split Transaction_' panel on the right side of the screen.
    
2.  At the bottom, click on the red "Unsplit" button.
    
3.  In the confirmation dialogue, click "Yes, confirm".
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F7jzPydRGbxfqOyPcjZof%252FSplit%2520Transactions%2520-%2520Unsplit.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14e16352-ae47-4fd7-b3a3-a55db84200a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d95ea31&sv=2)

Once unsplit, the original transaction will reappear as a single entry on the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page with the original total in the Amount field (eg. if it was split to $50 and $50, it will now appear as a single transaction of $100).

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#if-youd-like-to-unsplit-multiple-split-transactions-in-bulk-you-can-also-do-the-following)

If you'd like to unsplit multiple split transactions in bulk you can also do the following:

1.  In the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page, select any split transactions that you'd like to unsplit.
    
2.  On the right side of the screen, click on "Delete".
    
3.  In the dialogue that appears, select "I want to unsplit and keep the parent transactions"
    
4.  Confirm by clicking "Yes, delete".
    

circle-exclamation

Make sure to select the correct option to keep the parent transactions, otherwise the original unsplit transaction will be deleted and cannot be recovered!

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FYq3Q0eshBh4wREVszI2j%252FSplit%2520Transactions%2520-%2520Bulk%2520Unsplit.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24e0418e-d8ef-4e08-84c7-e5ea95200e6c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77acb140&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#group-transactions)

Group transactions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Grouped transactions are used to keep things organized. While categories and tags help with budgeting, filtering and tracking data, grouping transactions is a way to reduce clutter and maintain associated transactions together.

There is no limit to the amount of transactions that can be grouped together.

Grouping transactions will not change the individual transactions’ data. The group transaction can have its own properties (date, category, payee, notes and tags), while the individual transaction’s maintain their original properties in the background. The individual transactions will be hidden from the default table view on the Transactions page, but can still be filtered for in the Transactions page or viewed in the Analyze page, with their individual properties.

By default, filters on the Transactions page will only display results based on the group transaction’s properties, ignoring the individual transactions grouped within. If you would like to filter for individual transactions within groups, you will need to include the filter option for "Type is part of group":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FWiMFsuPVYtPmPZr94xKejHfp4cD_WCh-WScZw-ExoC9-Dhw3w6E25q4ZYxyMtL8HU1jOio5gr1el-opp10kgpydkptWpxBxdnpBzvfp6C86ROyQX28Cp1DYb81qG93jBquV67P3DOY8SVbafCz9NLmE&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f8f636e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-group-transactions)

**How to group transactions**

Grouping transactions is done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Begin by selecting the transactions that you’d like to group together. To select a transaction, click on the checkbox to the far left of the row.
    
2.  On the right-side of the screen, you will then see the '_Selected Transactions_' menu. Click on the "Group" button to open the "Create new transaction group" panel. Review the information and fill in any missing data.
    
3.  To create the group, click on "Save changes".
    

The selected transactions will now display as a single entry in the table on the Transactions page, with an icon within the Amount field to indicate that it is a group of transactions. Hovering on the icon will reveal information about the individual transactions contained within the group:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FIewkPQxwukHeNBFI-RmHAKMdLv3uLnUfoOPONpBFGMcmPd8DQeDj0kwfDvQHij-Gk3Hh6J_xIjfURnCqvQvPbKFxifXmGmMD07KgVv3tW3fdYpISm3wSeDxFhQ9oDpImGb0X17FAON33uaTvyxowRKg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30f8027&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-manage-an-individual-transaction-within-a-group)

**How to manage an individual transaction within a group**

Editing or removing individual transactions from an existing group is done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Click on the Amount field of the transaction group to open the '_Edit transaction group_' panel on the right side of the screen.
    
2.  The total number of transactions in the group will appear at the top. Below it, all individual transactions will be listed. Hovering on a transaction will reveal two icons:
    
    *   "**Edit transaction**" - This will allow you to change the individual transaction’s data, such as Date, Payee, Amount, Account and Notes. To save any changes, click on the “Save changes” button at the bottom.
        
    *   "**Remove transaction from group**" - This will remove the transaction from the list, but the change is not confirmed until you click the “Save changes” button at the bottom. If you accidentally clicked to remove a transaction, click on the “Cancel” button to start again.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-add-transactions-to-an-existing-group)

**How to add transactions to an existing group**

Adding additional transactions to an existing transaction group can be done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Click on the Amount field of the transaction group to open the '_Edit transaction group_' panel on the right side of the screen.
    
2.  The total number of transactions in the group will appear at the top. Below it, there will be a search bar allowing you to "Search by payee name, amount or notes".
    
3.  Click on the search bar and start typing. If a transaction matches the search, it will appear in the drop down menu. Click on the transaction you would like to add.
    
4.  Once clicked, it will be added to the list of transactions in the panel. To confirm the change, click on "Save Changes" at the bottom.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fl9hf2ZI2wLENums6AIk-AX24kQxgwl989WME31HjrZBRIiSInrJbs-gxPxEzpPiki3_YhmsvECBv6N04TynI2N2JiDGB4LdU3gVJrfFq_RmrfZrhDC_2aB_lA6Lq427YPgjAzQM4HtQWOhevqn5Vp8s&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2afe778f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-ungroup-transactions)

**How to ungroup transactions**

Ungrouping transaction groups is done from the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Click on the Amount field of the transaction group to open the '_Edit transaction group_' panel on the right-side of the screen.
    
2.  At the bottom, click on the red "Ungroup" button.
    
3.  In the confirmation dialog, click on "Yes, confirm".
    

All individual transactions from the group will now display on separate rows in the table on the Transactions page, with their individual properties for Date, Category, Payee, etc.

To ungroup multiple transaction groups in bulk, you can follow these steps:

1.  Begin by selecting the transaction groups that you’d like to ungroup. To select a transaction group, click on the checkbox to the far left of the row.
    
2.  On the right-side of the screen, you will then see the '_Selected Transactions_' menu. Click on the red "Delete" button.
    
3.  In the confirmation dialog, verify that it is set to "I want to ungroup the selected transaction groups only".
    
4.  To finalize, click on "Yes, delete".
    

circle-exclamation

Make sure to select the correct option to only ungroup, otherwise all groups and associated transactions will be deleted and cannot be recovered!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#recurring-transactions)

Recurring transactions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transactions that repeat regularly are represented with Recurring items. Transactions associated with recurring items don’t necessarily need to be the same amount, but would generally occur on a regular cadence and the next expected payment should be predictable (eg. twice a month, every 6 months, annually, etc.).

Recurring transactions can be either recurring expenses or recurring income:

*   **Examples of recurring expenses** include a monthly Netflix subscription, a quarterly insurance payment or a yearly gym membership.
    
*   **Examples of recurring income** include your salary or interest income.
    

It’s useful to associate recurring transactions with recurring items to easily find them when needed. Examples:

*   If there is a bill you haven’t paid in a while, you will be able to refer to the Recurring Items to check and prevent fines or having the provided service canceled.
    
*   If you want to cut down on spending, Recurring expenses will typically be the first place to look since canceling a monthly subscription can save you a lot of money in the long run!
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-link-an-existing-transaction-to-a-recurring-item)

**How to link an existing transaction to a recurring item**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Locate the transaction that you wish to link and then click on the arrow on the far-right of the transaction row
    
3.  In the "Transaction Details" panel that appears on the right side of the screen, scroll all the way down until you see the different actions under "I want to..."
    
4.  Click on "Convert to a recurring item"
    
5.  You will now be able to see a list of all recurring items that have not yet occurred for that month. Click on the recurring item that you'd like to link the transaction to.
    
6.  To finalize, click on "Save Changes" at the bottom.
    

The transaction will now be linked to the Recurring Item, an icon will appear next to the Amount field of the transaction to indicate that, and the text in the row for that transaction will be colored in turquoise for quick identification.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FUeTGUl_cnBgFLzBeFlcuElmwdZNkJApv8GdatNz3zITRcL1_A9iO0nAVxVX1jw0akXVW_JGTq8EAxvQFpGYg08PSD8cu26JYL-vkyK5-Ud_p-n8Om1xldXoieuau5uVr01d5Y2XI6zM7wzvCCsXJg2U&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=976ce58a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-edit-or-unlink-a-transaction-from-a-recurring-item)

**How to edit or unlink a transaction from a recurring item**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Locate the transaction that you wish to link and then click on the arrow on the far-right of the transaction row
    
3.  In the '_Transaction Details_' panel that appears on the right side of the screen, scroll all the way down until you see the different actions under '_I want to...'_
    
4.  Click on "Edit recurring item"
    
5.  You will now be able to edit the Recurring Item, replace it with a different Recurring Item, or unlink the transaction from the Recurring Item.
    
6.  To finalize, click on "Save Changes" at the bottom.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-types#how-to-create-a-new-transaction-for-a-recurring-item)

**How to create a new transaction for a recurring item**

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  On the left-side above the table, click the arrow next to "Add to cash"
    
3.  In the drop down menu that opens up, click on "Create from Recurring"
    
4.  A panel will open up on the right side of the page and you will now be able to see a list of all Recurring items that have not yet occurred for that month. Click on the Recurring item that you'd like to create the transaction for.
    
5.  To confirm, click on "Create".
    

The new transaction will be created and added to the Transactions table, an icon will appear next to the Amount field of the transaction to indicate that, and the text in the row for that transaction will be colored in turquoise for quick identification.

Last updated 1 year ago

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#view-change-history)

View Change History


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Whenever changes are made to a transaction (eg. data is added or removed, transaction is split or grouped, transaction is linked to a recurring item, etc.), those changes are saved in a change log with a timestamp. This is helpful when you wish to confirm if a change was made and when (eg. if a change was automatically applied based on a [Rulearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
).

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#how-to-view-a-transactions-change-history)

**How to view a transaction’s change history**

1) Open the [Transactions arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
page

2) Click the arrow to the right of the transaction row to open the Transaction Details panel

3) Scroll down to the I want to... section and click on "View change history", which will open the “Transaction Change History” panel, showing the most recent change at the top.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#exporting-transactions)

Exporting Transactions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction data can be downloaded from Lunch Money in CSV file format. The CSV file will be created with all transactions within the active visible view. If you are on a filtered view, the CSV file created will only contain the transactions from that filtered view.

The CSV file exported will include the following columns: Date, Category Group, Category, Payee, Amount, Currency, Notes, Tags, Account Name, Original Name (if split or grouped), Transaction number, Type (split, group, or recurring), Parent ID (if split), Recurring ID (if linked to a Recurring Item), and 'Created At' Timestamp.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#how-to-export-a-csv-file-with-transaction-data)

**How to export a CSV file with transaction data**

Exporting a CSV file is done via the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  First, make sure that all transactions that you’d like to export are displaying in the current table view
    
2.  On the far right of the screen, above the table, click on the Export to CSV icon. The download will begin immediately and save to your computer.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fjth15OALycPCiQL0oTMtUz7HNFHzdVUYO3316OCj4YaE2ygmiGa1dUMquLbX04ISud0oQrlGFcefKPzDpzBhxtihraJQr4RDicsys3l36I1uCptrMK0Q-T1-fkQQQsUypI2pO6H8w1iXwif1jRQQYdU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ebdf6ffc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#filters)

Filters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Applying filters on the Transactions page is a way to search and achieve a view that will only include transactions based on defined conditions. Filtering will hide irrelevant data from the table, so that you can work with a curated list of transactions.

There are three main ways to filter transactions: Quick search, Quick filter, and Advanced Filter.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#quick-search)

Quick Search

The quick search is located right above the Transactions table. The quick search can be used to get a quick filtered view of transactions that correspond with the search value entered.

For example:

*   “Groceries” to filter all transactions in the Groceries category
    
*   “24.99” to filter all transactions with an amount of 24.99
    
*   “Netflix” to filter all transactions with “Netflix” as the payee name
    

If the search term is found in multiple fields (eg. Payee and Notes), both matching transactions will appear in the filtered table view.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FPAeN-l-5D2Hej_UgCW3OvxoB113zC3ICmiT4lj-RXW16J3y_FKVgAh5uo1-aFD4OmhDb8I-Rxm7p3D2kUlk4Bf6D0VST4LL0bjtMlDpt3LcNeAWXpwCVfH_8iVkjo6bt2YTFxv7S9uZBSl1kwnQxdko&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c92bf4e0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#quick-filter)

Quick Filter

The quick filter is located right above the Transactions table, next to the quick search bar. This is a dropdown menu that includes some of the most common time frame filter options. The active month’s view will always appear first in the list, followed by the previous month, the current year, last year, and an All Time filter:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2F_g8jeUkw6o_0UZQTz7g2oGvCaFTBR1nY8RrD337n-uP2wilFpmZpUzOZPtl7Tu_CoRMOacbrJwC6NPNpVommgRrtxVXuy8Vyv4D2rszhUzldgy5sTXiDzGZzBTXi43CI0IP8l1q1QNuA2es9BgVYWgU&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=493d13e0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#advanced-filter)

Advanced Filter

The advanced filter tool is very powerful and allows for a combination of many different parameters in order to achieve a filtered view of the exact transactions you are looking for.

The advanced filter option is accessed by clicking on the "Filters" button, located on the right side of the page above the '_Review Transactions_' section.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FcX3Lo0YOAVsM7BLepv5XT_1kF9RPN90U-km5NAai7BspK-41ElV29-gmb2jpYmjF8kf5MHIbrwoWf1URD5yst0YQtprAZlSmUoZhypBZuijwU2aqqlms5m8jaTxG1YcmUVxkbKL26N_XempKENxBmzM&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46639548&sv=2)

Once clicked, the advanced filter setup dialog will appear. At the top of the setup dialog, you can select whether you want the filter to match with all or any defined conditions. At the bottom of the setup dialog, you will select the time frame within which you want to search (clicking on the dropdown menu will also allow you to set a custom range).

To add a condition, click on the "Choose filter" dropdown menu and set the value. To add another filter, click on “Add another filter” or the duplicate button next to the dropdown menu.

To remove a condition, click the red 'x' button.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fw8-y2DQze_UFupG_nuI-pSPFk4MkkLbcNy4XVb_BDSdh3WDUL64aO76yKkY8SLdprx9uyCYIjYY34p1Lg1sb38EHOiaW_V3sJNTY0do8j0RVCPP_NsSCxGr5HS657c2LmWfrWtSVd8u5veuTTJ-KuV0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9c4ca86&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#sorting-ascending-descending)

Sorting (Ascending / Descending)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The data in each column in the table can be sorted by ascending or descending alphabetical or numerical order. To sort the data, simply click on the header of the column. The first click will sort by descending order, and clicking again will sort by ascending order:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F4hiviG658z0tCUG1GoyQ%252F2f8a573cb2056d1b8bea31de3e44826a.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55bff259-8823-4253-a4e6-3bb6127b9285&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=268e9a71&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#adjusting-column-width)

Adjusting Column Width


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If the default column widths do not perfectly contain your data (such as with longer category, payee names or notes), you can change the column width by clicking and dragging the vertical dividers in the header row:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fkpr65WPIEtCNn2syaBY0%252Ff0965aeb6eff68764801ede81250ece5.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9497a7bd-cd27-4273-b937-0c93996bf341&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=437bf722&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#show-hide-columns)

Show / Hide Columns


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In some cases, you may want to hide certain columns from the Transactions table in order to have a cleaner view of the transaction data. In Lunch Money, you have the option to hide the Notes, Accounts, and Tags columns from view.

Toggling to show or hide columns from view is done via the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page, by hovering over the Options button on the far right side of the screen, above the table.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FuIVrNs0TLGG8APdEZRqPiXQqX_JTeAJ8wSWcxGgB1Qx6l7dNa0dnaw85gMTTzMx2qdFbfoWB7noCbwkCgm5pcdbS72-06IAxcul5KICKlsAGzCKeFEFtZgYTU6kgcT1UouM0-CrjOQ4JxiP7PMdsKC0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8d5d1ba&sv=2)

In addition to toggling the columns to show or hide from view, if you have more than one tag for some of your transactions, you can choose whether you’d like to see all tags in the table, or just one of the tags.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#deduplication-tool)

Deduplication Tool


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In some cases, you may find duplicate transactions appearing on the Transactions page. To easily go through duplicates and remove them, we recommend using the Deduplication tool.

The Deduplication Tool will search through the active transaction list view to locate similar transactions based on your choice of 2 or more criteria. With that said, it is recommended to use at least 3 criteria to get the most accurate results.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#some-things-to-keep-in-mind)

Some things to keep in mind:

*   The Deduplication Tool is a one-time action, meaning that it will not continue running in the background. If you wish to run a new search in a different filtered view (eg. for a different month), you will need to change the view first, and then rerun the Deduplication Tool again.
    
*   The Deduplication Tool will only search through standalone transactions. Split or grouped transactions are skipped and not taken into account when searching for duplicates.
    
*   The Deduplication Tool will only select the duplicate items, but not automatically delete them. You will be able to decide what you wish to do with the selected Transactions.
    

triangle-exclamation

Always double-check before deleting as you may have legitimate multiples of the same transaction!

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#how-to-use-the-deduplication-tool)

How to use the Deduplication Tool:

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Set the transaction list to a filtered view in which you'd like to search, as the Deduplication Tool will only process through transactions on the active filtered view (eg. if the view is set to "May 2024", the Deduplication Tool will only search through transactions in that month).
    

circle-info

If you wish to look for duplicates across multiple months or with the "All time" filter, make sure to select "Date" as one of the criteria on step 4 below, to lower the risk of legitimate transactions being marked as duplicates.

1.  Click on the Options icon on the right side of the page, and then click on "Deduplicate transactions" at the bottom of the menu:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FIya4Che5zeekF_t8o4762wpgm_PUAXYrTdKvybZ1BIgLJFkejTk5TPlVzoFqbaZUz-F4QXCTlFbAUzl1Wcvns7UW0JJWVZihAN6jXBDsDgIVca3O4LDdnpbrAO2afrh_3puMTDCVJbuKY2iwpGHItf0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b680e1c&sv=2)

1.  In the dialogue window that appears, you will now select 2-4 criteria to be used to identify the duplicate transactions: Date, Account, Amount and Payee. It is recommended to select at least 3 values for effective results.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2F5XKe0cp59jLtduOw96eamdrqkc_HaHz6Mz9hj6Zp91iN5alwhyrN-xS4ExHsbwAouteYHyGGek0VAJSwPdciT10F-p5oYtcZS1OaSj8Q7OFirYC6mcSa6xOEjd1Uy4flBwMI3p58np9PnC2iOCKnLfA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4783d08e&sv=2)

1.  Next, you will select whether you wish to keep the most recently added transaction or the earliest added transaction for any duplicates:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FlTuJhdYa3qjuygJjb-7upVeruOAUGU7OZ9udjSFA1m5t3cY9zap4F5Ns-hfmm9OY2rs_IaK3xba7VLFXCF9GW0Lx02Si2nJKd17MiNnJ8XZSgh8InuAwS4cdn3NIgySpQFJnHDFRTyZIDQKg6vIcluM&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22cc1519&sv=2)

circle-info

"Most recently added" vs. "earliest added" refers to when the transaction was created within Lunch Money, not the date of when the transaction took place. This is important to consider if you already had transactions in Lunch Money and suddenly see duplicates. Selecting to "keep the earliest added transaction" will remove all the duplicates that suddenly appeared, based on when they were added to Lunch Money, keeping the original transactions.

1.  Click on "Select transactions to delete" to continue. You will now return to the list of transactions and if any duplicates were found, you will also see transactions selected for deletion.
    

circle-exclamation

Pay attention to the "Selected transactions" box on the right side of the screen to see how many transactions are selected and make sure to carefully review all of them to ensure there are no legitimate multiples of the same transaction.

1.  Once you've double checked all transactions and are ready to delete them, click on the red "Delete" button on the right side of the page:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2FE5hn_kvNG1vnZNfC4h_pmYtP50Uk9Hidltkl56xHJ9V5iOzHfBaZFFmVP2nkyH7ouMiWhIWwfZ8pKQJzomtURTvLkk7LYCggYxpuyOR6L9RFQQJOx5zMUAlOesklosTHm9V0OAD3Rdv4LIa4qGAAVsE&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f420725c&sv=2)

# Managing Tags | Knowledge Base

Once you've already set up some tags on your account, whether you need to update tag details, archive or delete them, existing tags are managed via the [Tags arrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
page.
