Updating tags


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-edit-a-tags-name-or-description)

How to edit a tag’s name or description

You can change a tag’s name and/or description at any time by going to the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
. To edit a field, click the table cell, make the desired changes and press Enter to save:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FCoCUMfHWhKlhHMvYgf8E%252Fedit_tags_table.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53d844ac-9a7a-431a-9547-b7bfc36265bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=455f29c2&sv=2)

Alternatively, you can also manage the name and description via the side panel:

1.  Head over to the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     (_Setup > Tags_)
    
2.  In the table, locate the tag that you wish to edit and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit Tag’ panel that appears on the right, you can click on the text fields to change the tag name and tag description
    
4.  Confirm your changes by clicking on "Save" at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdTmIiP5GouMJ58wstisVHXtYPBSTjlfmcHgFw_xLDzXu3Xu3mE-qlYZMC4edJJGnvGEouuKocAeugdchKa8iwaRdS7wRSsopwEVY-YsZ331D4KbHEzZ0cuC8QUsivOi_ug7Ewd4SYKFpsWJm9mp63c1lMS%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e4ce419&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-set-a-tags-color)

How to set a tag's color

In Lunch Money, you have full control over how your tags look. You can choose a custom background and font colors, and see them reflected consistently across the app, from transaction reports to sidebar overviews!

You can personalize a tag's color from the Tags page:

1.  Open the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     (_Setup > Tags_)
    
2.  In the table, click the desired tag under the 'Styling' column to the right
    
3.  In the pop-up, use the color pickers, or click on one of the preset color options below
    
4.  Check the preview, and click on "Save changes" to save your tag's new look:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Frm4GB6pF9f1E17yXnhsK%252Fset%2520tag%2520color.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a916a2f-6bd7-4022-a0f4-02b718d07cb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e33e33e9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#archiving-tags)

Archiving Tags


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-archive-a-tag)

How to archive a tag

If you are no longer planning to use a tag (i.e. a specific event or trip you tracked is over), you may choose to archive it. Archiving the tag will prevent it from showing up as an option when creating or updating transactions, yet you will still be able to access the tag for filtering purposes and analytics.

1.  Open the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     (_Setup > Tags_)
    
2.  In the table, locate the tag that you wish to edit and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit Tag’ panel that appears on the right, click on the toggle to enable the “Archived” property
    
4.  Confirm your change by clicking on “Save” at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdY2zK0KKhneDluqFUMV6LlBp_p8PNa66DHcc79aYlYQyipU9SZ4-v7J5GhvNXy90ikhziGo_m-ILGnx5sPYpHKhhM__ZEalGLt4Lf363CIUf_dGMmx6LFLnDwnEyu3CqT0U02oU61ReroMcviLtCk7pRNg%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a393310&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-unarchive-a-tag)

How to unarchive a tag

If you wish to unarchive a tag so that you can assign it to transactions again, you can do so by disabling that tag’s "Archived" property via the 'Edit Tag' panel:

1.  Open the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     (_Setup > Tags_)
    
2.  At the bottom of the table, click on 'Show archived tags' to expand them into view
    
3.  Locate the tag that you wish to edit and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
4.  In the ‘Edit Tag’ panel that appears on the right, click on the toggle to disable the "Archived" property
    
5.  Confirm your change by clicking on "Save" at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdXt5-8jYYWNHUuZsT5K9QJXUtGmvQvRnyC4UWh6Cu2b3eepsLx8cVngSnEEFM23_InhOEHtqWW3BG5m0TSobzA6tJYFec6W29bUSpX7iOLr0yea4pniw60B24Bcmtaef0Iakcwca2QFZBNgcLyRwvlYBu6%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=912cc355&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-show-hide-archived-tags)

How to show/hide archived tags

By default, archived tags may be hidden from view. To view your archived tags, scroll down to the bottom of the Tags table and click on “Show archived tags”. To hide the archived tags again, click on "Hide archived tags":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F0r4yNCFgd5eWjPdugd11%252Fshow_hide_archived_tags.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc218b87b-37a2-42a3-a069-99ff36bc7719&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1fdf52d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#deleting-tags)

Deleting Tags


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/managing-tags#how-to-delete-a-tag)

How to delete a tag

You can delete a tag via the 'Edit Tag' panel on the Tags page:

1.  Open the [Tags pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
     (_Setup > Tags_)
    
2.  In the table, locate the tag that you wish to edit and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the 'Edit Tag' panel that appears on the right, click on "Delete"
    
4.  If the tag is associated with any rules or transactions, you will see a confirmation dialog appear. To proceed with the deletion, click on "Yes, I still want to delete this tag":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeUu_a1rLVc-SkdFlxfojWsF09M5zs59vYgXNd0k3YGkKB5Xk-dqRtT2N4xCpaOQ1e2V_1256EX89VoDikU3MrycjWzkf90aKfXz9Mql0aodrUMZYoLe80AuVJACi4HvQLqBkcyEa0qL7ItLhvkie3srGE%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36de4c36&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

Deleting a tag is a nuclear action and cannot be reversed. The deleted tag will be removed from any associated transactions (other tags assigned to the transactions won’t be affected), and any associated rules with only a tags clause will be deleted.

Last updated 2 months ago

# Affiliate Program | Knowledge Base

Lunch Money offers a flexible and powerful solution to budgeting and financial management. As our partner, earn money spreading the delight of our personal finance tool!

Whether you're writing a review, comparison or producing a video, you can earn commission for promoting Lunch Money.

**Join the Lunch Money affiliate program to** **earn $15 for every new paying user** **you refer!**

[arrow-rightJoin the affiliate program](https://partners.lunchmoney.app/?utm_source=knowledgebase)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/affiliate-program#how-it-works)

How it works?

1.  **Partner with us** [Sign uparrow-up-right](https://partners.lunchmoney.app/?utm_source=knowledgebase)
     with FirstPromoter to get your custom referral link. When someone signs up and becomes a paid user with your custom link, you'll get credit.
    

circle-info

We manually review all applications, so please fill out your profile fully to show us how you'll promote Lunch Money.

1.  **Spread the word** You can post your custom referral link on your own blog or website, social media, or run paid ads to it. We'll provide assets to help you promote Lunch Money and start earning.
    

🎁 Their special offer

💸 Your referral reward

Your followers get an extra free month of trial when they subscribe with your promo link– that's **two months of free trial** total!

You earn **$15 for every new paying user** on both monthly and annual subscriptions.

1.  **Cash out** Payouts via ACH or IBAN to your bank account after a US$30 minimum is reached.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/affiliate-program#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/affiliate-program#id-1.-whats-the-difference-between-the-affiliate-program-and-the-referral-program)

1\. What's the difference between the Affiliate Program and the Referral Program?

The [Affiliate Programarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/affiliate-program/?utm_source=knowledgebase)
 and [Referral Programarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/referral/?utm_source=knowledgebase)
 are similar in that they both provide the referred users one (1) extra month of trial. The main differences between the Affiliate program and Referral program are who can sign up, how the reward is calculated, and how it is paid out.

Affiliate Program

Referral Program

Earn US$15 for every new paying user you refer to Lunch Money

Receive account credit equal to 10% of your friend's invoice each time they pay

Anyone can sign up, including people who are not Lunch Money users

Only Lunch Money users can refer users

Rewards are paid out in monetary form via ACH or IBAN to your bank account

Rewards are applied to your next invoice

Payouts only happen after a minimum of US$30 in accumulated reward is reached

No minimum number of referrals required

Rewards accumulate with each new referred user that turns into a paid subscriber

Rewards are calculated based on a snapshot of your active referrals 24 hours before your subscription renews

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/affiliate-program#id-2.-should-i-use-the-referral-program-or-affiliate-program)

2\. Should I use the referral program or affiliate program?

The [Referral Programarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/referral/?utm_source=knowledgebase)
 is recommended for individual paying subscribers who wish to invite friends and/or family to earn account credit toward their subscription. This would allow you to take advantage of the rewards right away. Some users might find they benefit from a high discount on a monthly subscription instead of an annual subscription.

The [Affiliate Programarrow-up-right](https://lunchmoney.app/affiliate-program/?utm_source=knowledgebase)
 is recommended for people, publications or businesses with a larger sphere of influence. This would allow you to cash out rewards in monetary form.

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/affiliate-program#id-3.-how-do-i-sign-up-to-be-an-affiliate)

3\. How do I sign up to be an affiliate?

We are using FirstPromoter to provide you with a very detailed dashboard of your up-to-date stats, self-serve ways to manage payouts and ability to create multiple custom referral links.

To become an affiliate, click the following below:

[arrow-rightJoin the affiliate program](https://partners.lunchmoney.app/?utm_source=knowledgebase)

circle-info

We manually review all applications, so please fill out your profile fully to show us how you'll promote Lunch Money.

Last updated 5 months ago

# Rules | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**What is a rule?**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#what-is-a-rule)
    
*   [**Rule conditions vs. Rule actions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#rule-conditions-vs.-rule-actions)
    
    *   [Supported rule conditions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#supported-rule-conditions)
        
    *   [Supported rule actions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#supported-rule-actions)
        
    
*   [**Rule creation**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#rule-creation)
    
    *   [How to create a Category Rule](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#how-to-create-a-category-rule)
        
    
*   [**Applying rules**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#applying-rules)
    
*   [**Using one-time rules**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#using-one-time-rules)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#what-is-a-rule)

What is a rule?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rules are created to automatically update certain fields of a transaction based on some criteria. The purpose of a rule is to help you keep your transactions organized and categorized in the way that you choose. Rules can also be used to send you email notifications (i.e. when new transactions come in).

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#rule-conditions-vs.-rule-actions)

Rule conditions vs. Rule actions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A rule is made up of two parts: the criteria (conditions) and the effect (actions):

*   **Conditions** determine which transactions a rule should apply to. A transaction will only trigger a rule if it matches the set conditions (i.e. if the payee name is an exact match, if amount is greater than $500, etc.)
    
*   **Actions** define what happens once a rule is triggered. These actions can be transaction updates (i.e. set the category, add a tag, update the payee name, etc.), or even having an email sent to you!
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F2KQ7EfbfiGUnsNlCwYd1%252FCreate%2520transaction%2520rule.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91fc2f82-6aac-4325-a57f-0e148d67f086&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db3086a5&sv=2)

**Example**: If we want to automatically set the category to `Ridesharing` for transactions where the payee name contains the word `Uber` (because every Uber transactions is named differently, but always contain the word Uber), then the rule condition would be `payee name contains 'Uber'` and the rule action would be `Set category to Ridesharing`.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#supported-rule-conditions)

Supported rule conditions

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FZwe4cTugnwlrRH7jiC92%252Frule%2520conditions.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D634b9bcc-69e8-4c55-9fe5-f7c272e93f7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d54c5bad&sv=2)

**We support the following conditions for building your rule criteria:**

*   Payee name (`contains` / `starts with` / `matches exactly`)
    
*   Category
    
*   Notes (`contains` / `starts with` / `matches exactly`)
    
*   Amount type (`expense/debit` / `income/credit`) and amount range (`between`, `>`, `>=`, `<`, `<=`, `=`)
    
*   Day range (supports date wrapping as well)
    
*   Account
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#how-do-the-rule-condition-operators-work)

**How do the rule condition operators work?**

**Criteria**

**Name**

**Will match**

contains 'Market'

Farmer's Market

Yes

contains 'Market'

FRESH MARKET CO.

Yes

contains 'Market'

Marketing Class 101

Yes

starts with 'Uber'

UBER BV

Yes

starts with 'Uber'

Uber Eats

Yes

starts with 'Uber'

SQ\* UBER

No

matches exactly 'Walgreens'

Walgreens

Yes

matches exactly 'Walgreens'

WALGREENS

No

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#supported-rule-actions)

Supported rule actions

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fm6OTUdiDQxi76tDVMFmL%252Frule%2520actions.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82c9e6c2-f566-4522-8168-8acf0b2f1687&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2498505&sv=2)

**We support the following rule actions:**

*   Set a new payee name
    
*   Set notes
    
*   Set category
    
*   Set uncategorized
    
*   Add tag(s)
    
*   Link to a recurring item
    
*   Don't link to recurring item (disable recurring suggestions)
    
*   Don't create a rule
    
*   Split transaction
    
*   Mark as reviewed
    
*   Mark as unreviewed
    
*   Send me an email
    
*   Delete (this) transaction\*
    

circle-info

\*The "Delete transaction" action is only accessible when creating a rule via an existing transaction directly. The action will delete that specific transaction when the rule is triggered. This can be useful if you wish to delete a manually-entered temporary transaction once the official transaction automatically syncs in at a later date.

circle-check

You may also use a rule to split a transaction. If using the "Split transaction" action, please note that splitting and updating the original transaction properties are mutually exclusive, meaning you may only do one or the other!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#rule-creation)

Rule creation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A rule can be created in various ways:

1.  A category rule is automatically created with a “match exactly” rule whenever you change the category of a transaction. This can be turned off in the Settings.
    
2.  A suggested rule is automatically created when you rename a payee.
    
3.  When you edit a transaction, you'll also be presented with an option to create a new rule based on the changes you just made. You can always edit these later in Rules.
    
4.  When a new recurring expense is created, a system rule is automatically created to match transactions to recurring expenses. We do not recommend editing or deleting these, but the option is there if you need to make some adjustments to ensure they match your recurring transactions.
    
5.  Lastly, you can create a new rule manually by clicking “Add a new rule” in the Rules page.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#how-to-create-a-category-rule)

How to create a Category Rule

If you’d like your transactions to be categorized automatically, you can create Category Rules. These rules only need to be set up once, and will automatically apply to any new transactions that match the conditions you’ve defined. To set up a new category rule, follow these steps:

1.  Go to the [Rules pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
     (_Setup > Rules_)
    
2.  Click on 'Add a New Rule'
    
3.  In the 'Create transaction rule' panel, enter your conditions and effects, example: _**If..**_ _payee name contains "Pizza";_ _**Then..**_ _set category "Restaurants"._
    
4.  To save, click on 'Create' (or 'Create & Apply' if you'd like to retroactively apply this rule to existing transactions as well).
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FyJSHm0cTHbzougxdSKdq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D574d0097-1160-43f0-8ace-97b0f6750ee3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6eb05425&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#applying-rules)

Applying rules


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A rule in Lunch Money is automatically applied to all synced transactions and transactions manually-added via the Transactions page or the [CSV/PDF import tool](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/import-via-csv)
, while the default for transactions added via the [developer API](https://support.lunchmoney.app/miscellaneous/developer-api)
 is to not apply rules. The CSV/PDF import tool and the developer API allow toggling this preference on or off.

To have rules automatically apply when updating existing transactions, you will need to have the "Run rule on transaction updates" setting enabled for the rule:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FAV9gL1bhuY29A3V70fo2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9be36b29-2887-4cb7-b063-b7545568feff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60a50716&sv=2)

**Auto-created rules when updating payee names**

If you have the 'Auto-create suggested rule when updating payee' preference enabled on the [Settings pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
, then you will see a notification at the bottom left corner whenver you edit a transaction whose payee name matches others. From that notification, you'll have the option to apply the same changes to all other similar transactions. If you click on "Apply to 50 similar transactions", it will open a pop-up where you can review and decide exactly which transactions to apply the changes to, and which ones not to:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fx7AcTpDtjfMFaWihqCFJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D507a9374-00d4-4246-90ed-f0ab0f0f62b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=253a502d&sv=2)

These payee rules are also saved on the Rules page, and can be reviewed and approved via the [Suggested Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=suggested)
 view. Once approved, you will also have the option to apply rules retroactively using the “Save and Apply” button in the 'Edit Rule' panel. Before applying, Lunch Money will let you know which transactions will be updated with the option of de-selecting some.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#using-one-time-rules)

Using one-time rules


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules#one-time-rules--delete-transaction-rule-action)

**One-time rules + "delete transaction" rule action**

The use case here is for folks anticipating an imported transaction, but wanting to see the transaction amount adjustments right away. Create a manual transaction that auto-deletes once a corresponding pending/posted transaction is imported.

**Steps:**

1.  Create a manually-managed transaction
    
2.  Click into the transaction and select "Create Rule"
    
3.  Set your conditions (i.e. new transaction with payee 'Walmart' in account 'Bank of America credit card')
    
4.  Choose 'delete transaction' as an action– this auto-selects the current transaction. Note this feature is only available via "Create a rule" from the Transactions details view.
    
5.  The option to 'delete rule after use' is automatically selected in this case.
    

Last updated 1 month ago

# Auto-Categorization | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [The status icons](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#the-status-icons)
    
*   [How to assign an individual category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-assign-an-individual-category)
    
*   [How to set up all available categories for auto-categorization in bulk](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-set-up-all-available-categories-for-auto-categoriation-in-bulk)
    
*   [How to re-run categorization rules on uncategorized transactions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-re-run-categorization-rules-on-uncategorized-transactions)
    

* * *

If you already connected a banking institution and have transactions synced, the “Set Autocategorizations” button will be made available on the right-side above the table on Categories page:

!["Set autocategorizations" button](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F8RPwPbbBUAGKPVPONDwn%252Fset_autocategorizations.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4235a4a-bc15-4a8a-a204-39a7fc80894a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e114f7e&sv=2)

Clicking on “Set Autocategorizations” will take you to the ‘Auto-Categorization Settings’ page. On the left side of the page, there will be a list of general categories and clicking on any of them will display a table with a list of various detailed subcategories with names, descriptions and an option to create or assign categories.

The categories and subcategories that you see here are the same ones used by Plaid, our third-party bank syncing partner. When transactions are imported, Plaid pre-assigns one of the categories listed on this page. To ensure all your transactions are categorized within Lunch Money, you will need to map your own categories to Plaid’s predefined ones.

circle-info

The first category in the list (the one without a description) is a general “catch-all” category. This means that if that’s the only category that you set up and assign, all transactions that match any of the unassigned subcategories below it will fall into the general “catch-all” category instead. If a transaction matches a subcategory that you assigned however, it will be prioritized over the general “catch-all” category.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXei01oebrW8mB2O3K7WMOZhbH8Ry0iBxEatd_dCibB3glTBFL0Ql2--X6HBrri6dlNCGthe-UCDviX5RTnyp7I6DICtqwJBu0soCq9epi0TT4fK825be6s4m56KMMj9DHKis5XZzwpuX98-0d0W3rrGyS0%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2019b87b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#the-status-icons)

The status icons

On the Auto-Categorization Settings page, there are status icons next to the list of general categories on the left. The status icons are used to guide you and let you know where there is a category that needs your attention to be assigned.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcz5o1vHYWKcC0xNT_SvnbyqiPwsfwk8c3QBbDBecE4JIispNAV5xaDpvrx_ndbrk138j89ncg-lwEWm2ouAMxywJGYeOKT0Fw54OvarTwLll25Zek-AikxoKd_z6VI-JGNcHaS64q1HFo1yfKWZNCUuDAa%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=39&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ddf33c3c&sv=2) — No categories have been or need to be assigned.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXftV91VnQ0xyVM0ffDQ1OQnSz98F2VUU4WffERXlwbQTE_pVN9TU9EPYRnR4jO7OP2rQtLEz53d5AuXSChWeBNVNGMqCxRgnnVT3hWUDh50DXFOakoVSviX7qRdfiK9uSrsWAFJMsNQ9QtT3mVDypvKOAPs%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=39&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8b6faab&sv=2) — There are subcategories that need to be assigned, or uncategorized transactions that match and need to be categorized.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdGNFb05coULF0ueor0LJ3H8tfZoNEv4L2GMZBknwHfa1qMnuiD-vKNriQ45IRmrhBpiBuUsJbbJqRavr7b5WuoDn4WrkdtrIZNYO-yG91ryk0ZtrWhTFZfrxELxHzYv-pmC8n8PT9iOp4lWMIfNn9bMmFZ%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=42&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=471e0226&sv=2) — There are subcategories assigned, but the general "catch-all" category isn't assigned.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfrvGUB98ht5zoLCXg6-HqgoWbbm8vb0MZIl27AFaH10UzVIGAlNpwutW-ypMfJ1_7LURPdg2Sx4E-q3SfAtr07BhfbK2fnHBTxs5H37DTHfNXjLpRy_SXS4xlCYvvHsc5FLFv-XeuW2Mh80xL2KBw7Cjc_%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=40&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5298853&sv=2) — All the subcategories that needed your attention have been assigned, as well as the general "catch-all" category.

If there are subcategories that need to be assigned, you will also see an information icon next to the subcategory name revealing additional information such as how many uncategorized transactions are associated with it:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf5V8ujT11cf0vWjmbDmCCkr9AcZ64SYONmyA1-0ReXCt3Un0GYpX1a0jr72kWMaFXjHXcexjY52lVI60JFPuoxtqHvmiwFFQSx9Ik7uSNDHpPL8bDYZk9fw9zdXDl9-U1zVpGjzT2hdIB8GhV1lf0eEnc%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf0d5494&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-assign-an-individual-category)

How to assign an individual category

To assign a Lunch Money category to the pre-defined categories, you can either click on “Create” or choose one of your existing categories by clicking the drop-down menu under the “Assign to Category” column in the table:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeM5f5R1Hs9Yf27x_k7J1VGfWTQR4E7HY_EO3I39KpSaIofbfx9ca03vzYR41JD7eGhvCCxxyGU253Z1ACPOCTWXnWyXiVkrWvBXIBx_2d8W6cUtxAq7r2jXIowXgIIACIdb4dT0gDDHohjxq-0wYgFPFdt%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4769210&sv=2)

Clicking on “Create” will create a new category with the same name on the Categories page and assign it to the pre-defined category listed.

Alternatively, if you want to have a different name for the category, or already created your own category for categorizing these types of transactions, you can click on the drop-down menu and type the category name there.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-set-up-all-available-categories-for-auto-categoriation-in-bulk)

How to set up all available categories for auto-categoriation in bulk

To have the categories created and assigned for you automatically, click on "Create missing categories" at the top of the table. Once clicked, categories that have matched uncategorized transactions will be created and mapped, and a green confirmation message will appear at the bottom-left of the screen.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FwsKWSu9jRpsfJzegzZW9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74fb7c52-0278-449c-b702-fd0113115dc6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8cf6bed&sv=2)

If you have uncategorized transactions associated with one of the the set up categories, a prompt dialog will also appear to let you know how many uncategorized transactions there are, with the option to run the auto-categorization rules. Clicking on "Run rules" will show you the list of all affected listings to review and confirm.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FQGMYdHnZuOkny6H7oocS%252FCategories%2520-%2520run%2520rules.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0190008-c567-49f0-86b9-5f3fd9e647a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b92742f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization#how-to-re-run-categorization-rules-on-uncategorized-transactions)

How to re-run categorization rules on uncategorized transactions

In some cases, you may have uncategorized transactions that match your assigned categories, but haven’t been assigned that category. To quickly update the category on those transactions, click on the “Re-run categorization rules” button above the table:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcGejMGzkqZDDOX0eUzR-PilfgXKdu07BDAKWvorUZyhYS6S8oBhcDw8hq67TpL4Ozg36-1XnVD0Jp_NZpgnAFYhrW8cjOynl84VVIl7W9qAoCBT8G8ekV3ReGBQ4OK6fug1imD8IZoCf3kloHqSaTlnB8%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27fe94ea&sv=2)

circle-info

Auto-categorizations are run before rules. This means that any other category rules that you have set up on the Rules page will overwrite your auto-categorizations.

Last updated 1 month ago

# Category Groups | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [What are category groups](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#what-are-category-groups)
    
*   [How to create a new category group](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#how-to-create-a-new-category-group)
    
*   [How to add categories to an existing category group](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#how-to-add-categories-to-an-existing-category-group)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#what-are-category-groups)

What are category groups


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you have a large number of categories, you may find it easier to organize your categories into groups. To do this, you will create a category group, and then nest categories within them.

Category groups cannot be assigned to transactions, as their purpose is to help organize your categories. Only the categories nested within the category group can be assigned to transactions.

Category groups must also be composed of at least 1 category. When creating a new category group, you will be able to choose one or more of your existing categories to add to it, or create brand new categories to add.

circle-info

Note that a category can only exist as part of one category group at a time. If you choose to add a sub-category from another group to a new group, the sub-category will be removed from the original group in favor of the new one.

Category groups are not only used to organize the categories in the Categories page, but also across the different areas within Lunch Money. For example, on the Transactions page, you will be able to quickly filter to see transactions associated with a group. In the Overview page, you can see your spending breakdown by individual categories, as well as by category group.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#how-to-create-a-new-category-group)

How to create a new category group


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Category groups are created on the Categories page:

1.  Open the Categories page
    
2.  Click on the arrow next to "Add new category" and select "Add category group" in the dropdown menu:
    

!["Add new category" button and drop-down options](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FMEHFVlHzU6Iu20RYHRiu%252Fadd_new_category_menu_categorygroup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd69f2b2e-a1cd-40bd-9e74-c400cc9bb38d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c519d57&sv=2)

1.  In the 'Create Category Group' panel that appears on the right, enter a group name (required), a group description (optional), and enable any relevant category properties.
    

circle-info

All sub-categories nested within the category group will inherit that group’s properties.

1.  Next, under 'Categories to include', select all that apply. If you'd like to add a new category, click on the first option and a new entry will be created with an empty name field for you to type the name of the new category. You can repeat this as necessary.
    
2.  To confirm and create the new category group, click on "Create".
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#how-to-add-categories-to-an-existing-category-group)

How to add categories to an existing category group


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add a category to a category group, the quick way is to click and drag it using the re-order icon at the end of each category row, and drop it under the relevant category group in which you wish to nest it:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf3gItxLdbgzeHaW0b05c_yfvnZ_LiPHqiS1pxpMpj0mdkFR9CU-ufNSH1MshzOXRM9SlQj_etHBdMzkQagsocbzckP7WwNkMA1Q6--S6ALHqQlajsv60rmQu6RYVenFXCC6ee65k9fCsXGCLTn0PRg5rqT%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3b7e4c1&sv=2)

The category will have a nested line icon added before the name to let you know that it is now nested under a category group.

circle-info

The same drag-and-drop action can also be used to remove a category from a category group.

Note that a regular category cannot be made into a category group, and vice-versa. This is because the essence of each is different. Category groups are made to hold other categories, while regular categories are made to hold transactions. Since transactions cannot be assigned to a category group, you will not be able to set an existing category to be a category group.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#adding-categories-from-the-edit-category-group-panel)

Adding categories from the 'Edit Category Group' panel

Another way to add a category to a category group, is from the ‘Edit Category Group’ panel:

1.  Open the Categories page
    
2.  Locate the category group and click on the little arrow icon on the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit Category Group’ panel, click on the “Modify categories in group” button
    
4.  You can now check and uncheck categories, or add new categories as desired
    
5.  To confirm the changes, click on “Save changes” at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfDCYYhvOLufc0Tq2zyGXMaAOrJDV8OuVCrenkVB1J5haRuo-ZjocMMGGJTHjKvp5uvv_Svw9d6D90BpT22FSy6weJNzBRzAxTDIgX10mxo30GZ0hiWt1N2fB8Rb_TayXm3ZOGYpZ0GIBXTqk4aoNk-o7jG%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8e2093a&sv=2)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [How to create a new category group](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-groups#how-to-create-a-new-category-group)

# Category Properties | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**The Category Properties**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#the-category-properties)
    
    *   [Treat as income](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#treat-as-income)
        
    *   [Exclude from budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)
        
    *   [Exclude from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#the-category-properties)

The Category Properties


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before setting up your categories, it’s important to note the function and purpose of the category properties, as they dictate how transactions assigned to the categories are treated throughout Lunch Money.

In Lunch Money, there are three category properties:

*   **"Treat as income"**
    
*   **"Exclude from budget"**
    
*   **"Exclude from totals"**
    

A category can have any combination of category properties, for example:

*   An regular expense category (eg. “Restaurants”), will likely have no properties enabled.
    
*   An income category (eg. “Salary”), will likely have just the “Treat as income” property enabled.
    
*   A transfer category (eg. “Payment, Transfer”), will have both “Exclude from budget” and “Exclude from totals” enabled.
    

circle-info

Sub-categories (categories nested within a category group) inherit these properties from their parent category! To update the properties of sub-categories, you must revise the properties of the category group.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#treat-as-income)

Treat as income

Throughout Lunch Money, you will see in overview and summaries a line item called "Income" and another called "Expenses". The "Income" line items are calculated from transactions assigned to categories marked as "Treat as income". A category without the “Treat as income” property will be treated as an expense category.

For example, if you have a credit transaction (eg. +$500) assigned to a category marked with “Treat as income”, the transaction will appear as “Income” in overview and summaries:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfNGoPX9_JSGxlPPiaCfk9mVoiPMKmjnDhPmhlbeD18ht6VRtbT5TRve7NYNr6hHSJGVD02b6vdehZsdVN2cPiwommCPPZBNnXhCUipNWhPsURCB51e6ffpTMKJldEdpZ5nzQSwwnjlo8YZzLkT9aJqKAiV%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcb99392&sv=2)

Alternatively, if you have a debit transaction (eg. -$500) assigned to a category marked with “Treat as income”, it will still be deducted from your "Income" totals:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcf1lK-InySgOpjcnwVkGlH599e9PcCGv8ViBXHPmiLa2xvJwh5BqBQh8_ymH21cCYSOO2yk1GQVB87GiQUCMidZ6JiRHz7fRJUIunoTspbXK3QJC3Ud_ktCCZ70sE1MaWOZipDr4UUYoPjXcHzeSoIo6m-%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b422a924&sv=2)

On the other hand, if you have an uncategorized transaction, it will be treated as "Income" or “Expense” based on the amount notation. If the uncategorized transaction has a credit notation, it will appear as “Uncategorized Income”:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfVYq5ACKV1Hg5vziwqrjpxc-i9QyGEB8OTwx-6chx-ST_6hfG0PAArwVJvq5nTdZGA1W3_uF8NDxHoVu-RpyRlaHh9E9Umca_9zSdwujV3VLcEFzmefMS7BdqxTvP6h02dEMqCCJO9ukTcdLZlk2r6Zakf%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e5505d&sv=2)

You can use “Treat as income” on more than one category. For instance, you can break down your different income streams by creating a number of income categories, eg. "Interest income", "Part-time job", "Tutoring job", "Passive income', etc.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdF5H6oMrBbZjhfxe7b78Sk9FLbBtfJtopCeh2l4dqJcl9D-eTpezCR3ThGYtia4mFwYIZYyKmFfr39SNAufqVcldOrmPKdBTKei2aNwYwdHAI7BObs0lTokMW7uuXQJqR3RhsOcGIIa4ID0jOYuEb_8ug%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4188ee57&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)

Exclude from budget

Categories with the "Exclude from budget" property enabled will not be part of the budgeting aspect of Lunch Money. You won't be presented with an option to set a budget for these categories on the Budget page.

A common use for this is on categories used to track reimbursable items, emergency expenses, and transfers between accounts.

circle-info

When looking at the Budget Breakdown on the Overview page, you will be able to select whether to show or hide categories with the “Exclude from budget” property as part of the view.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfrxJRUWs4c-kSFy7XbJGFFm53ov-tlE3KMCSg0XlbrTFAexx4oAo08Ig5Cfh3hSBxyyMN6UMBZ5xY-f5go2ohr2u24vN32Xo01EppCGjEE0a3pG9RQOJ3YozXpJKTD0Oj6sT58hGWn3MA9nBs6ZQI0yk5y%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e87e4af4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)

Exclude from totals

Transactions in categories that have the "Exclude from totals" property enabled will not be counted towards total spending or income calculations and summaries throughout Lunch Money.

This is useful for categories that are used to track payments and/or transfers between accounts, or reimbursable items.

circle-info

In the settings for the Spending Breakdown on the Overview page, you will be able to select whether to show or hide categories with the “Exclude from totals” property as part of the view. When looking at the Stats, Trends, Calendar and Analyze pages, you will have the option to include transactions from “Exclude from totals” categories as part of the reports and totals in the calculations.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf2V65fCxDOozrqMZEuKCnU5bfmMusghjKyDaJwHyeU3N-36sVdRQ8-Th9hWkwKP2bdif17zywPPTDqIlxppzx5IdAZ2xa9wRlxE_DXPeC4B14H6Wm1FDEmBXAg_47QjQ4VA6MYTbl05FqKbJhbt2cFMykm%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc8dd0e7&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# FAQ | Knowledge Base

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#whats-the-difference-between-categories-and-tags)

What’s the difference between categories and tags?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both categories and tags are used to organize your transactions, yet they serve different purposes. Categories dictate how the transactions will be treated throughout Lunch Money (expense vs. income, or excluded from totals), and are also an essential part of the budgeting aspect, as budgeting works on a category basis.

On the other hand, tags are used to further organize transactions for personal analytics. Tags are much more flexible to use than categories as they would be more specific and generally not associated with as many transactions as a category would. Moreover, unlike with categories, a transaction can be associated with multiple tags!

Some uses of tags may include tracking transactions associated with a specific event (eg. birthday party, wedding, etc.), a trip (eg. Brazil 2020, Italy 2021, etc.) or a particular project (eg. kitchen renovation, bedroom makeover).

To learn more about tags, [see here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags)
 and [here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transaction-enhancements#tags)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#what-are-category-rules)

What are category rules?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Category rules are used to automatically categorize transactions based on defined parameters. These rules can be set up via the Rules page, and will appear under the '[Category Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=category)
' section of the Rules page:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcvCOdfpuMz0E1Bd2_-LZXykDD9IFWdU_cz4CK9eJ_QzBvaKYFoUcKho439n_btSBCb4HKoQuyCOptQ-juAX0PMbkn_1RiCko94EabEbhklb-B8mu4v0WeSsOX74be0hT5v7kAkKb-nE1wjrEujx0WefWI%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=454f9f6e&sv=2)

For example, you can set up a rule that says: "If a transaction’s Payee name matches 'Pizza Hut' then set the category to 'Restaurants'".

To learn more about Rules, [see herearrow-up-right](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/rules)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#how-can-i-view-all-transactions-assigned-to-a-specific-category)

How can I view all transactions assigned to a specific category?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are various ways to get a filtered view of transactions associated with a certain category. On the Categories page, this is done by locating the magnifying glass icon on the far-right of the row for any of the categories.

By clicking on the magnifying glass icon (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfZfyeGDF3a3HnvPxFu8sh0qucZBqeZA8syirY16iXYWD-m0tDh5V7s2hRAtmK59y3bdFEvUQMOS03XHJRTLKS36HH8xXjwb9215jidCPCed-bX4BDqWI38BZdm1ZErblRtr0VjkebBkoCd3Wy9EI-GEXlX%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=40&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdb62388&sv=2)), a popup dialog will appear listing all transactions using that category. If needed, you can make changes to transactions directly in this view, or alternatively, click on the green “View transactions” button to open this filtered view on the Transactions page.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdbOH2WVrRDaiw61_tsRyZcvVjZt1_CytqxUosq7r1pqvk5LFG4AvHwXALcx3bowQYu4eCKGsOa2iq5VsZTOX0Xru34C8-JFF2thJBfn-T2nkUNhCoiROqoCQtnUWRNIxzeKEry98Tgkjao7n-QDBrwd2uX%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=346d08bb&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#how-can-i-export-and-share-my-category-setup)

How can I export and share my category setup?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Whether you're looking to share your categories with others, load them into another budget, or simply save the category setup for safekeeping. You can export your categories by copying them to your clipboard!

**Here's how:**

1.  Go to the Categories page
    
2.  Click on the arrow next to the 'Add new category' button
    
3.  In the drop-down menu, click on "Export Categories"
    
4.  Click on "Copy to Clipboard" at the bottom of the pop-up
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FI75XulyKuirrOBYyQn6c%252Fcategories_export.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12e6b67b-0e93-4924-9de9-e23aef13aadb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1be1fb5&sv=2)

circle-info

Your categories will appear listed, one per line. A dash ("-") indicates subcategories. Category properties appear in square brackets after category names. These include: _income_, _exclude\_from\_budget_, and _exclude\_from\_totals._

Once copied, you can send the category setup to friends, [share it with the Discord communityarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/842337014556262411/1143315755673333860)
, or [import it as a custom category set](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-or-import-custom-categories-in-bulk-advanced)
!

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#why-does-my-category-selection-change-after-adding-a-transaction)

Why does my category selection change after adding a transaction?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you notice the category selection changing immediately after adding a new transaction, the most common culprit would be a rogue rule that is overriding the category selection every time.

To resolve this, go to the [Rules pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 and click on '[Category Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=category)
' from the left-side menu to filter the page to display all rules affecting transaction categories. Look for the relevant rule, and you can then either click on it to update the rule criteria, or use the checkbox to the left to select and delete it.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FV8NBO1ZoE55DWeZVlndG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D116fb149-f392-4ff0-a2fa-326eb08b2f8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3abf223&sv=2)

If you are unable to identify the rule that is causing this, you can also check the [Transaction's Change History](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#view-change-history)
 log to identify the cause of the category change. If the category change was caused by a rule, it will display the text 'by rule' and you can click on 'rule' to quickly view and update the rule:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FQswMuHK6EG12JDcMIwEu%252F03404e90a4717b47ce28885e7c6d28ac.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D785e542a-2f17-459f-b227-790ee713397a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5eb4ab8e&sv=2)

circle-info

By default, Lunch Money will auto-create rules when updating categories. To disable this, you can head over to the [Settings pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 and toggle-off the 'Auto-create rule when updating category' preference.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/faq#how-do-i-request-a-new-feature-for-categories)

How do I request a new feature for Categories?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are always looking for feedback on new features, and recommend opening a feature request ticket on the Feedback Board here: [https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/categories-tagsarrow-up-right](https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/categories-tags)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcD0LsLop62vc_5X0Yy9pADwT9IVsdkLfi_THQjfSQElEI3pKrS0y__TQULlqaeI3bUjDnOyE7LB1eeFmDV0C5X8Z7T0YkKh31ElKrs_p5Hod7vLR8swdC3G-Ahjh2dsUa99RupYKDiqn5WE_UB3lmPJqlS%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ebc0970&sv=2)

Last updated 4 months ago

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-often-should-i-expect-new-transactions-to-get-imported)

How often should I expect new transactions to get imported?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's important to note there are 3 parties involved in getting your bank data: Your bank, Plaid (our third-party banking importer) and Lunch Money. We interact with Plaid to get the latest from your bank.

Updates between your bank and Plaid can take anywhere between 1 and 3 business days. Once Plaid receives an update, they notify us and we re-sync your account immediately. Other than that, our system also syncs up with Plaid at least once every 2 days to ensure nothing fell through the cracks.

If there are missing transactions or incorrect balances, that's usually an issue between your bank and Plaid. If that's the case, let us know and we can look into it for you :)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#what-is-the-difference-between-the-different-account-types-cash-credit-loan-etc)

What is the difference between the different account types (cash, credit, loan, etc)?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The difference between these account types for both manually-managed and synced accounts is in how the balances contribute to net worth.

For loans and credit accounts, positive balance denote amount owed and is deducted from net worth.

For cash, real estate, crypto, etc, positive balance denotes amount owned and is add to net worth.

For manually-managed accounts, you can update the account type as you wish. For synced accounts, the account type is set by Plaid. If you find that your account types are incorrect, for example, a loan account is denoted as a cash account, please get in touch with support as this is a syncing issue between Plaid and your bank.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#i-opened-a-new-account-with-my-bank.-will-this-show-up-automatically-in-lunch-money)

I opened a new account with my bank. Will this show up automatically in Lunch Money?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes, if you have new accounts with your bank and it's set up for automatic syncing, the system will automatically detect this. In some rare cases, this could take a few days to show up. Do not add a new bank connection as this will result in duplicate accounts.

If your account is taking longer than expected to show up, reach out to support and we will reach out to Plaid, our third-party banking importer, for further support.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-de-activate-or-remove-a-synced-account)

How do I de-activate or remove a synced account?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Deactivating or removing a synced account means you no longer want us to fetch the latest transactions and balance for it.

You can click into the account you want to deactivate and click "Remove this account". This gives you the option to remove _only_ that account and the choice to keep or remove associated items (transactions, balance history, etc). The removed account will still show up in your list of accounts as 'inactive' but you can use a View filter to hide it from the Accounts list.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FtQyHaMOKWK7NoUxqEGM5%252Fb89e50f0e5a362d4a2cce6e86061fbdc.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac2b3885-c6cb-4c29-9031-c06f2d421fc6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d0baa40&sv=2)

Use filters to remove inactive and closed accounts from view

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-remove-inactive-synced-accounts)

How do I remove 'inactive' synced accounts?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To answer this question, we first need to provide a bit of context as to how syncing works:

When you connect to your bank, we get an access token which gives us read access to all of your accounts. Every time we fetch new data for you, we'll check each of these accounts for updates.

When you mark one or two of these accounts as inactive, it means you don't want these balance and transaction updates. So, even though we have access to read that data, we skip them due to your preferences. However, that doesn't invalidate the access token as a whole, and at any point you can re-activate these accounts to track in Lunch Money which is why they still show up, albeit as "Inactive".

There isn't a way to "remove" inactive accounts associated with an active connection, yet you can hide the inactive accounts from your view, using the Filters options at the top of the Accounts page:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-MZBG_9N1Dq3pnvsjG-o%252F-MZBHcafdR3UsMAbm1ad%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-03-24%2520at%25204.18.02%2520PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b251ff8-57b7-44b9-874b-4ead8e563362&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6705ec99&sv=2)

Use view filters to hide inactive accounts from your view

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-are-manually-managed-account-balances-updated)

How are manually-managed account balances updated?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manually-managed account balances are updated automatically when you add, remove or update a transaction assigned to that account.

For instance, if you import transactions via CSV, manually add a new transaction or use the developer API to bulk-insert transactions, the associated account balance will update accordingly.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#can-i-manually-update-an-accounts-balance)

Can I manually update an account's balance?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In some cases, such as after uploading historical transactions, you may need to manually re-adjust the current balance of your manually-managed account. You can do so via the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
 page by following the steps below:

1.  Go to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page
    
2.  Click on the relevant account in the list to open the "Edit Account" panel
    
3.  Scroll down to the "Balance" section and enter a new amount under "Current Balance"
    
4.  Click on "Save Changes" at the bottom of the panel
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FpsVUGn1WjP09jSsvdPiQ%252F16d6a14df3e72c95cd11f005a1427c3d.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2d67a9c-69f6-4ff7-be36-54d6b8ea73ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d582a8f&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

Note: Making a manual update to your account balance will not create any new transactions.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-merge-a-manually-managed-account-with-a-synced-account)

How do I merge a manually-managed account with a synced account?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#why-would-i-ever-need-to-do-this)

Why would I ever need to do this?

It may be that at some point, your bank integration ran into some issues and you had to switch to a manually-managed account to continue getting your transactions into Lunch Money.

Once the bank integration was fixed, you're now left with two accounts representing the same bank account– one which is synced, and one which is manually-managed. At this point, there is no longer a need for the manually-managed account.

At this point, you can use the **Merge Accounts** feature to combine both accounts into one. Note, this is an irreversible process so do ensure you pick the right accounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-merge-accounts)

How do I merge accounts?

Please [click here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#how-to-merge-accounts)
 for the step-by-step instructions to merge your accounts.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#my-partner-and-i-have-joint-accounts-and-they-are-showing-up-twice-with-duplicate-transactions.-how)

My partner and I have joint accounts and they are showing up twice with duplicate transactions. How do I handle this?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our account removal flow can help with this!

Get started with this button in the details pane of the duplicate account you'd like to remove:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-M64jDL4mfvFyAmSRKa3%252F-M64jMCkcZXJPssn_8RC%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-07%2520at%252011.35.53%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32763aa4-4bda-4414-ad83-d91bb81c140f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41a57cbb&sv=2)

You'll be asked if you want to remove all accounts associated with the bank or just one account.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-M64jDL4mfvFyAmSRKa3%252F-M64jkSeLwO_r53vLJt1%252Funnamed.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D073e4bd7-5185-4881-8f57-89e2f921d461&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55fe40a8&sv=2)

After that you'll have the option to keep and transfer all existing transactions or remove them all.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-request-a-new-accounts-feature)

How do I request a new Accounts feature?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are always looking for feedback and recommend checking out the Feedback Board to vote on existing feature request tickets, or create your own: [https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/accounts-assetsarrow-up-right](https://feedback.lunchmoney.app/accounts-assets)

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXebpbTkdUriJ66fMytVh5pXX76JUK6LS2THhhCYtwK-0FAWCwmLJrlXi2u3vq7ydEx7YOUZ5kFbBqKyv0aFirTlD3SkDJ-PWgurgdh-y8Hiuq0EKqohqBNn-lyxh2_JjO8Pm906rF_Lp4OYglegdqDmUtVy%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b80103a0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-open-an-in-app-bank-syncing-support-ticket)

How do I open an in-app bank syncing support ticket?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For bank syncing issues, we highly recommend [creating a bank syncing support ticket directly in the apparrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)
. This helps us quickly gather all the details we need to know in order to investigate the issue.

[Open a new bank syncing support ticket ➜](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings?sync_support=true)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#if-you-have-already-connected-the-account-in-question)

**If you have already connected the account in question:**

1.  Go to the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
    
2.  Click on the account in question to open the 'Edit Account' panel
    
3.  Scroll down and click on 'I need help with this account':
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FKden2Jd14wTWCL0Wpdzp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83cc6176-de36-40d6-9ab6-84555124441c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=371674fe&sv=2)

1.  Select the relevant issue and fill in the requested information to submit the ticket:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Ffruupc9ngcJmC05tr77T%252F6a54191a51bf54ca64742e8a4a8e10c7.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63c04731-d0ef-4a45-a596-eca651491e43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=471d5730&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#if-you-have-not-been-able-to-connect-the-account-in-question)

If you have not been able to connect the account in question:

1.  Create a general bank syncing support ticket by clicking on 'Help' at the top right corner of the app:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F69qTC1Eg53GU6sgqRuZZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0a9beb4-3dcc-4d42-8a65-58f189c090b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c77f9a&sv=2)

1.  Select 'Open bank syncing support ticket'
    
2.  Choose 'I am having trouble with a new connection'
    
3.  Select the associated recent connection attempt from the listed options
    

circle-info

If the recent connection attempt doesn't appear in the list, please attempt creating the connection again before submitting the ticket. Still having trouble? Please open the ticket using the 'Submit a bug or feedback' option instead.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FazRKHIom1Qs0L1ek123x%252F2130e0b7e0301c0639c643a2056db6ff.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De98ce344-980e-4449-9b51-be5f0c623899&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=994b1dbe&sv=2)

Once you've submitted the ticket, our awesome customer support reps will reach out directly to Plaid on your behalf and get in touch with you from there! 🙂
