# Category Creation | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [How to create a category from the Categories page](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-a-category-from-the-categories-page)
    
*   [How to create a category from the Transactions page](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-a-category-from-the-transactions-page)
    
*   [How to create categories in bulk using category sets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-categories-in-bulk-using-category-sets)
    
*   [How to create or import custom categories in bulk (advanced)](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-or-import-custom-categories-in-bulk-advanced)
    

* * *

If you choose the "Start fresh" path when first setting up your Lunch Money account, you will be prompted to select and customize categories to get you started. If you don't have categories set up yet or if you wish to add or adjust your categories, you can add new categories at any time via the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
 page.

On the Categories page, categories can be set up individually, or in bulk using category presets. Categories can also be created when adding or updating transactions via the Transactions page, or as part of the CSV import process.

circle-info

An [auto-categorization](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/auto-categorization)
 feature is also made available once you’ve had at least one transaction synced from a connected banking institution.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-a-category-from-the-categories-page)

How to create a category from the Categories page

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Click on the orange "Add new category" button:
    

!["Add new category" button](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F8PeyqSxUV8fb4Sq5kTis%252Fadd_new_category.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a9da66f-6c29-4670-ab11-f363c5fd2cdc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82ff892e&sv=2)

1.  In the table, a new row will be created. Type a category name (obligatory), type a description (optional), and enable any of the category properties if relevant.
    
2.  To save the new category, click on the little green "Add" button on the right side of the row, or press 'Enter' on the keyboard.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-a-category-from-the-transactions-page)

How to create a category from the Transactions page

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions)
     page
    
2.  In the table, click on the category cell for any of the transactions and type the name of the new category. Given that the name of the category doesn't already exist, an option to add the category will appear:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfOViQrpdjwxSepLQ7Wg7JnVYB57HBeJHAS7NI1eKrUseuJabI6oB-ng9lrWXHEZGxRvGhMELLtOmXKWg9Fza31qBPP6fMI4Q1TGegsIFuXku3W6uTbEzPnZhMGJGW1oBCKTqNti1nUsKfxolXsyh-2E_w%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=533a3c3&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Add \[New Category Name\]" and a confirmation dialog will appear.
    
2.  In the confirmation dialog, click on the green “Yes, Create” button to confirm.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-us.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfL7Z-a_U_XQrjywljvl02hxZF4OxU03rY-ldNG6lsiDifuCC3YGaTO6ehttmnLWT8YlHdTa50hOnosuMUJfYUgYhlrny69-Bb7VQ6q8K3e95C_m2gI9Jz3gozvaiQb0qTsvK6NQyo0UjHrjeyxinINvX_a%3Fkey%3Dtb-5DGGaZOe9ZSDJnA95sg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9145f4a8&sv=2)

The new category will be created and assigned to the transaction from which it was created.

circle-exclamation

Please note that new categories created from the transactions page will always be treated as basic expense category and will not have any of the category properties enabled.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-categories-in-bulk-using-category-sets)

How to create categories in bulk using category sets

If you're not sure which categories to set up, or if you simply wish to speed up your category creation process, you can select one of Lunch Money's preset category sets, and customize it.

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Click on the arrow next to "Add new category" and select "Add preset categories" in the dropdown menu:
    

!["Add new category" button with drop down options](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FAQUBfqEkteTaAlJS2kGj%252Fadd_new_category_menu_presetcategories.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7195cc37-db74-452c-b784-88476b9ec508&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7d0596f&sv=2)

1.  In the 'Create Preset Categories' panel that appears on the right, click the drop-down menu to choose a category set:
    

![Create preset categories menu](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FkbzeijnO5exMt9pCKoEx%252Fcreate_preset_categories_options.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D124d08ad-7864-40f9-9aa9-40183d3f0da5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4327d9a&sv=2)

1.  Once you choose a category set, you can now select which categories from the set you wish to include. You can either manually check individual categories, or click "Select all" at the top to select all of them.
    

circle-check

For category sets with category groups (ie. 'Detailed categories'), make sure to select the category group names as well. If you only select subcategories, they will be created as standalone categories.

1.  Once you've made your selection, click on "Create".
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-creation#how-to-create-or-import-custom-categories-in-bulk-advanced)

How to create or import custom categories in bulk (advanced)

If you wish to add a custom set of categories, you can do that using the 'Custom (Advanced)' preset categories option:

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Click on the arrow next to "Add new category" and select "Add preset categories" in the dropdown menu:
    

!["Add categories" button with dropdown options](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FAQUBfqEkteTaAlJS2kGj%252Fadd_new_category_menu_presetcategories.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7195cc37-db74-452c-b784-88476b9ec508&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7d0596f&sv=2)

1.  In the 'Create Preset Categories' panel that appears on the right, click the drop-down menu and choose "Custom (Advanced)":
    

![Create preset categories panel with the 'Custom (Advanced)' option](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FciZpeK7P1s8LX07ZfcLb%252Fcreate_preset_categories_customadvanced.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da79968e7-4f0b-420a-8e28-86bb6b18f938&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e42dc068&sv=2)

1.  In the text field, enter your categories, one per line. Use a dash ("-") to indicate subcategories. Optionally add category properties in square brackets after category names. Supported tags are: _income_, _exclude\_from\_budget_, and _exclude\_from\_totals_.
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FwadFSzyMCJGC7rkKmLHJ%252Fcustom_advanced_categoryset.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea7e71f7-5650-4aa2-8034-c98ab101bce4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8df8962b&sv=2)

1.  In the "Preview of categories", review the list to make sure your categories, category groups, and subcategories were all entered correctly.
    

circle-exclamation

If you see red warning icon (![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FZ3YFs1qvJY1vaSNWhkhk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5606de96-549f-4793-a707-6d6664c98c1c&width=35&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58c229f2&sv=2)), it means that the category name is already in use. In this case, it is recommended to change the name to something else, otherwise the category name will have a numbered suffix added to it, ie. "Category (1)".

1.  To proceed with creating you categories, click on "Create".
    

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

# Editing Categories | Knowledge Base

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**Reordering**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#reordering)
    
    *   [How to reorder the categories](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-reorder-the-categories)
        
    
*   [**Archiving**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#archiving)
    
    *   [How to archive a category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-archive-a-category)
        
    *   [How to change a category's 'Archived on' date](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-change-a-categorys-archived-on-date)
        
    *   [How to unarchive a category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-unarchive-a-category)
        
    
*   [**Merging**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#merging)
    
    *   [How to merge and delete a category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-merge-and-delete-a-category)
        
    
*   [**Deleting**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#deleting)
    
    *   [How to delete a category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-delete-a-category)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#reordering)

Reordering


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The order in which the categories are listed on the Categories page, is also the order in which they will appear in the drop-down menu when selecting a category for transactions, recurring items, or rules, as well as the order in which the categories appear listed on the Budget page.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-reorder-the-categories)

How to reorder the categories

You can easily change the order of the categories using drag-and-drop on the Categories page. Simply click and drag a category up or down the list using the re-order icon (the second icon from the right), and drop the category into place by letting go of the mouse.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FoVIZvhTRPten7DqPpBla%252FCategories%2520-%2520Reordering.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82efa8f7-26ed-47f5-87fe-013a5469541d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d4d55b9&sv=2)

circle-info

If you drag-and-drop a category group, all nested categories will be moved together with it.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#archiving)

Archiving


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If there is a category that you no longer use, but still wish to keep for reference as it is associated with past transactions, then you’d be looking at archiving the category.

Archived categories will not show up when creating or updating transactions, in budgets, or in the overview spending summary, yet will still show up as an option for filtering on the Trends, Stats and Analyze pages.

circle-exclamation

Archiving a category group will also archive all its children categories.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-archive-a-category)

**How to archive a category:**

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Locate the relevant category and click on the arrow icon to the far-right of the row
    
3.  In the ‘Edit Category’ panel that opens on the right, click on the orange “Archive” button.
    

A confirmation message will appear at the bottom left of the screen, and the category will be moved to a collapsed section at the bottom of the list of categories. You can click on “show archived categories” to expand the section and see the archived categories:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FGVPduRWNeZC8HXQFfVWY%252FCategories%2520-%2520archived%2520show%2520hide.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1199281-3c31-4963-93f4-9c0580b3e515&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f289e5d5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-change-a-categorys-archived-on-date)

**How to change a category's 'Archived on' date:**

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  At the bottom of the list of categories, click on "Show archived categories"
    
3.  Locate the relevant category in the list and click on the arrow to the far-right of the row
    
4.  In the 'Edit category' panel, click on the 'Archived on' date to change it
    
5.  Click on the orange "Save" button at the bottom
    

![The 'Archived on' date field in the 'Edit Category' panel](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fj9z1v740aR0E1sQ2diSL%252FDin%27s%2520%2520Newsletter%2520%2526%2520Blog%2520Images%2520%284%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad626e6e-644f-4f17-ae4e-757c2644f2aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47a69def&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-unarchive-a-category)

**How to unarchive a category:**

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  At the bottom of the list of categories, click on "Show archived categories"
    
3.  Locate the relevant category in the list and click on the orange "unarchive" button
    

A confirmation message will appear at the bottom left of the screen, and the category will be moved into the list of all active categories.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#merging)

Merging


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have two categories that you wish to merge into one, you can use the “Merge and delete” option. Any transactions, rules or recurring items using the merged category will be updated to use the new category instead, and then the merged category will be deleted.

circle-info

The budget associated with the merged category will be deleted. Budgets do not get merged into one, and the budget of the category you had merged into will remain unaffected.

For example, let’s consider that you have two categories: “Movies” and “Cinema”. If you merge “Movies” into “Cinema”, then “Movies” will be deleted. The transactions, rules and recurring items that used the category “Movies” will be updated to use the category “Cinema” instead. The budget for the “Cinema” category will remain unchanged.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-merge-and-delete-a-category)

How to merge and delete a category:

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Locate the relevant category and click on the arrow to the far right of the row
    
3.  In the 'Edit category' panel, click on the red "Merge and delete" button
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252FP1zIrEzjUl8blFe9kyFh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c5c9afe-0134-4d60-b190-bbbff513516a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=820da5db&sv=2)

1.  Next, under "Re-categorize Transfer items to", click to select the category that you would like to merge into
    
2.  To confirm, click on the "Merge & Delete" button
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#deleting)

Deleting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you accidentally created a category or no longer wish to track a certain category, you can delete it. Once a category is deleted, the associated transactions and recurring items change to “uncategorized”, and the category’s budget is deleted along with any rules that use the category.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/editing-categories#how-to-delete-a-category)

**How to delete a category:**

1.  Open the [Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/categories)
     page
    
2.  Locate the relevant category and click on the arrow to the far right of the row
    
3.  In the 'Edit category' panel, click on the red "Delete" button
    
4.  In the popup confirmation dialog, click on "Delete this category" to confirm
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F1riuuXT3ZMuA4z4ge78D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18e735d7-b4fd-438b-a00c-d9dc5c4d88e5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cefaa010&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

As deleting a category is irreversible, please make sure to first review and consider the merge and archive options before proceeding with the deletion.

Last updated 5 months ago

# Assigning Tags | Knowledge Base

Once you've created your tags on the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page, you can start assigning them to transactions. Transactions can be tagged with as many tags as you need, added manually during transaction creation or revision, or automatically by setting up [Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [**How to manually tag transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-manually-tag-transactions)
    
    *   [From the transactions table](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transactions-table)
        
    *   [From the 'Transaction Details' panel](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transaction-details-panel)
        
    *   [From the Bulk-Edit menu](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-bulk-edit-menu)
        
    
*   [**How to auto-tag transactions with Rules**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-auto-tag-transactions-with-rules)
    
    *   [How to create a tag rule](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-create-a-tag-rule)
        
    *   [How to view all tag rules](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-view-all-tag-rules)
        
    
*   [**How to remove tags from transactions**](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-remove-tags-from-transactions)
    
    *   [From the 'Transaction Details' panel](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transaction-details-panel-1)
        
    *   [From the Bulk-Edit menu](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-bulk-edit-menu-1)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-manually-tag-transactions)

How to manually tag transactions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tags can be assigned to transactions when creating or editing them on the Transactions page.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transactions-table)

From the Transactions table

If you already have tags set up on the [Tagsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/tags)
 page, you can easily add tags to any transaction via the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
 page:

1.  Locate the Tags column and hover the mouse cursor over the cell for the relevant transaction row to see an "Add" button appear
    
2.  Click on "Add" and a drop-down menu will appear with all available tags
    
3.  Locate the tag by scrolling through the menu, or search by typing in the search bar
    
4.  Click on a tag to add it to the selection (you can add more than one)
    
5.  To confirm, click on "Done", or anywhere outside of the dropdown box.
    

All added tags will then be listed in the relevant cell under the Tags column:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeCaUD0-yOs1Uy9NANZwdiKBbmSTlvv1KrUHDOTSjpD5VSDmzkZyEiwu7QVqCSZZxtknYOScr7P4Sz3ln6aPpvqrzxZC8bWfNi9Y9etPpFmj2EIMYGVP70PGkdapHOvy2gsY6CgVnPcmUZap_JROIPHpq05%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=770fbd3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transaction-details-panel)

From the 'Transaction Details' panel

Additional tags are assigned to transactions via the 'Transaction Details' panel:

1.  Go to the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Locate the transaction and click the arrow on the far right of the row to open the 'Transaction Details' panel
    
3.  In the 'Transaction Tag(s)' section, click the empty field to search or add new tags
    
4.  If you have existing tags, they will appear in the drop-down menu. Alternatively, type a new tag name and the option to add the tag will appear.
    
5.  Once you are done making changes, click on "Save Changes"
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeFSL0EZKja8T-DwuDvVfsI3S57uKB4dQTrWPPNDbqAPAthEctFKOr6D5VCHQ9Ga4S9-MCRSb3WO-ZcMVOD4M-MmRvwB2JhD7E9d-uCYGheflUWkV2N_jOfiFe-NBTJKHk22ckp1jRM1gA-LCvEi2QAIIEB%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35c91f4b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-bulk-edit-menu)

From the Bulk-Edit menu

If you are looking to add the same tag(s) to multiple listings in bulk, you can use the Bulk-Edit tool:

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Select all relevant transactions using the checkboxes in the far-left column
    
3.  On the right side of the screen, click on the 'Bulk-Edit' button
    
4.  From the Bulk Edit menu, select "Add tags" and choose the tag(s) that you wish to assign
    
5.  Click on "Save changes" to confirm
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdWI0XCqlcmFYv4Q7bVF2WCpPirktQTu4C-8UFXEc9wxcBW9c3i-H1O8IfTUlgZUm-HFTh7OmwAEnpM4_sljGDa3Ane03lQeGAhtJVE0LHLK7PCEcD2-f1qrVDwIV9XVzufjA__Wru6dlZ3CnlHBziC3NYK%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8609464&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-auto-tag-transactions-with-rules)

How to auto-tag transactions with Rules


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A tag rule can be set up to automatically assign tags to transactions that match any specified conditions.

circle-info

Tag rules can only be used to add tags to transactions, and this action is cumulative. A rule cannot be used to replace or remove existing tags.

For example, if you have a tag to track a kitchen renovation in your home, you can create a rule that will automatically assign the “Kitchen Renovation” tag to any transactions associated with your contractor, by using the “matches payee name” condition. This way, whenever you make a payment to the contractor, the transaction will automatically be tagged.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdpsapSqgM2GVfrn-HkUJi1gt4p6E6mmbrSkvRSoUI36hjqlAN1z1AiArp4eOTBgAAC48l6BukGGol4C2IyBnh26ciqytLGCPxjQwNZPvyUE4ZVqWEiM4QSIEK6BziUS96lD6isG68UU8XaK9YaCqzoNfQ%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a7c1982&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-create-a-tag-rule)

How to create a tag rule

All rules are created via the Rules page:

1.  Open the Rules page
    
2.  Click on "Add a new rule"
    
3.  In the 'Create transaction rule' panel, you can now add your "If.." conditions and "Then.." actions. The option "Add tags" is found in the actions drop-down menu:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfv7FwXcKuLttJDDP8Z8hIQWxrayv_HB9RYst5rZvAufXR8pRoimaXwSCDndfcxiHIfV2ZwwZrBs6vwBu_6DxJYeO_cywYRO6CMGv4JVU1yNbrj7lQ7_eWQYOWMWxu7txB2RXItWjzeIEfkV0mJW4k383eo%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d3c2384&sv=2)

1.  You may also choose to enable certain rule properties under the "Finally.." section. A common one to enable is the "Run rule on transaction updates" property:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcBc3sTeXlxnIVmbyb3YepBDQDsr8NQ1EZ9_8dXvlHf3To8lB5XYbfX6EAoX5nvIlyY3-ET_1KbDxEFaUMH7RmzJ597EJ8mEaijECtVSZv6DCiGMAQIww04P3C6sgY18aVV5o07UhytfNW0oD9PUl--hm5F%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e187c0c&sv=2)

1.  To finalize, save the new rule by clicking on "Create" at the bottom and the rule will then start running on any new transactions. If you wish to create the rule and also apply it to any already existing transactions, click on "Create & Apply" instead.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-view-all-tag-rules)

How to view all tag rules

To view all existing tag rules that you have set up in your account, you can go to the Rules page, and then click on "[Tag Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=tags)
" from the left-side menu:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdHAstfOYZ2F26BMsWO_ZNZELRhEufwydgqzfxywFgPdHzPaTK9DmURanwkEePG7EQAmdrez-TsKx4yiOvKaKOjyzQQaD3i0WkNsk7Iqe0xO8hOkI1H83RUJ8mhfo-BY4Sf6L1NovMvklWcunKYw14ESMuu%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9e41cf7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#how-to-remove-tags-from-transactions)

**How to remove tags from transactions**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-transaction-details-panel-1)

From the ‘Transaction Details’ panel

If you already have tags assigned transactions, you can remove them via the ‘Transaction Details’ panel:

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Locate the transaction and click the arrow on the far right of the row to open the 'Transaction Details' panel
    
3.  All assigned tags will display under the 'Transaction Tag(s)' section
    
4.  Click the small "x" icon next to any tag that you wish to remove
    
5.  To confirm the changes, click on "Save Changes" at the bottom
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf_fNLeXp4uO6mgI7-cxvHh_N59qLSyCobELrO61GMGccfMAFkVTGetJkdYK4jTfrIROONIpL7c9OlyB-XtPwPZ_cV9qCtHmJL3HfxnnyO6uzfYQqBGLXQrPjttd_99lQkAFifOrV-AfB4H_onKAQb9QAg%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9271dae&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/tags/assigning-tags#from-the-bulk-edit-menu-1)

From the Bulk-Edit menu

If you are looking to remove all tags from multiple listings in bulk, you can use the Bulk-Edit tool:

1.  Open the [Transactionsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/)
     page
    
2.  Select all relevant transactions using the checkboxes in the far-left column
    
3.  On the right side of the screen, click on the 'Bulk-Edit' button
    
4.  From the Bulk Edit menu, select "Remove all tags"
    
5.  Click on "Save changes" to confirm
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcy6-uinyiDtRLxuKrPg_KOt5fPxG6cTXtCviHUHqRqomoOZMmLkQVOi29D9EuTEDhqjvVf5ZavsCRc08KM0hu5tGERzseAWgvzZSjek5RZeC7enb-tAQp6o0vajvxkShSocST0F8-dOlWh9XeGRANSHOZz%3Fkey%3Dy8qoCvdOxd3ltTV1bl6vYA&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35c4264c&sv=2)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Managing Accounts | Knowledge Base

Whether you are looking update the display name, override the synced currency, update a manually-managed balance, or merge and delete accounts, all account details, advanced settings and actions are managed via the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
!

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [Updating account details](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#updating-account-details)
    
    *   [Advanced settings for synced accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#advanced-settings-for-synced-accounts)
        
    *   [Advanced settings for manually-managed accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#advanced-settings-for-manually-managed-accounts)
        
    
*   [Merging accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#merging-accounts)
    
    *   [How to merge accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#how-to-merge-accounts)
        
    
*   [Removing accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-accounts)
    
    *   [Removing manually-managed accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-manually-managed-accounts)
        
    *   [Removing synced accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-synced-accounts)
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#updating-account-details)

Updating account details


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clicking anywhere on the account’s row in the table will open the 'Edit Account' panel on the right-side of the page. From this panel, you can see detailed account information, manage account settings, and perform a range of actions.

circle-info

Keep in mind that the fields, settings and actions displayed would differ depending on the account type (synced, manual, or crypto). The institution name and balance fields cannot be edited for synced accounts.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdkvAL4fKPb5XvAr8SFyCLG8RHAWV3LKZURr9B_4swV1xL8sXgvUYwdYUyvSu-loAlnGd7Su-UQqcRbeIG6_QHTatRT7zG7NQnIPLF9b0dvSryVWHveU-TfeBQkFCHc4tM7OP47Ck31X7iW9QMIfbyLi8Q%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d660e0b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#advanced-settings-for-synced-accounts)

Advanced settings for synced accounts

For synced accounts, there are a number of advanced settings that can be enabled or disabled to define how the synced transactions in that account will be imported, managed and displayed:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXd-ujpyI012PAIyyGCGY3dNn9Ohf_yU496ezFniZhWLhA_ziDRniYvCGFuCrlAnj0AatcUceDBfZEsu07HZc-gwHi92YpsUUw7GMUftEpLf2vth6nMVPy4fmnEBMSCISpjIv9YM4orsN4dj0UrOgsxXg_qA%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b506ab2f&sv=2)

*   **Do not import transactions** - Toggle this on to disable importing transactions to the account, regardless if they are supported. Balance updates will still occur, but transactions will no longer import
    
*   **Earliest import date** - If set, transactions before this date will not automatically import. Updating this field will not remove existing transactions, but may trigger a fetch for new transactions from the set date to the present.
    
*   **Allow modifications to transactions** - By default, synced accounts do not allow manual transaction creation. Toggling this setting on will enable adding manual transactions and editing transaction amounts for automatically synced accounts. Please note that the balance of the account will not be modified from these changes and will continue to be synced and updated exclusively via Plaid.
    
*   **Use original transaction name** - By default, synced transactions will display Plaid’s cleaned-up merchant name. By toggling this setting on, transactions will instead display the original, raw transaction name. You will be prompted to choose whether to apply this retroactively, or enable it for future transactions only.
    
*   **Use authorized date** - By default, Lunch Money uses the authorized\_date field to populate the date field of imported transactions. Toggle this off to use the normal date field instead. You can view this information by clicking into an imported transaction and then clicking on "View Plaid metadata".
    
*   **Override synced currency** - If synced transaction amounts aren’t matching the account’s currency, use this setting to select a currency that will override the currency of the account returned by Plaid.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#advanced-settings-for-manually-managed-accounts)

Advanced settings for manually-managed accounts

For manually-managed accounts, the advanced settings can be enabled or disabled to define how the account will be treated and used within Lunch Money:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf5laJXzeakr35AFoCPvfZqBHe8P2tfT1rAU8aHzREDqqjh1w91ZQNDD6_h0nz-EoJMUuKVTNLG9DCWYsXGKSWem74fjyNzWvR2L5wVRI7r_f03lk-Ff9vCQtKm-pvXsrW8o_eP2_PORb0pLFV2Nc_R_fL4%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf2fc5ba&sv=2)

*   **Set as default account** - Enable this to set this as the default account when adding new transactions. This means that instead of new manually-added transactions defaulting as "Cash transaction" for the account, they will be set to this default account selected.
    
*   **Do not track transactions** - Enable this to only track the balance for the account. The account will no longer show up under the dropdown of accounts to choose from when creating or updating transactions and other items.
    
*   **Mark as closed** - Enabling this option will mark the account as closed and you will be able to set the exact date it was closed on. Transactions and balance history will remain intact and will still show up in the Net Worth Tracker and for filtering purposes and analytics, yet the account will no longer appear in the drop-down menu when creating or updating transactions.
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#merging-accounts)

Merging accounts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Whether you started out with a manually-managed account and now wish to start syncing it, or accidentally ended up with the same account twice, you can use the merge feature to combine two accounts into one!

When your accounts are merged, the transactions, recurring expenses and associated rules will migrate over to the new account that you are merging into. You will also be able to decide which account's balance to keep.

triangle-exclamation

As this is an irreversible process, please make sure to carefully pick the correct accounts to merge.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#how-to-merge-accounts)

How to merge accounts

The option to merge accounts is accessed via the 'Edit Account' panel:

circle-exclamation

Note that the steps may differ slightly depending on whether you are merging a manually-managed account or a synced account. The steps below are following the merge flow from the 'Edit Account' panel of a synced account.

1.  Go to the Accounts page
    
2.  Click on the account that you wish to edit to open the 'Edit Account' panel on the right
    
3.  Scroll down to 'Actions' and click the button that says "Merge into another account":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdWi3-sfGCt4b47s1X0QroRhzGswdTg20kcHkvBq0cT3OzaT43vQI5IyMwweaWz-z07R7t37d8uHMzLkbT50Gfmc7tUOrOG6repDXUXrL6FfbLhO5Zpiy2EpYwS5hNcc2Oo8_ifiBhR3K4DCBj8fEFrnsMF%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c109ab94&sv=2)

1.  Next, you will choose the account with which you wish to merge. You may only choose from a list of currently active accounts (that is, healthy connections). You will also be able to choose whether to keep the source balance or the destination balance:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfqgeTpOKHM1DMKeUpVEwaBTL5KEFB-wI0b3Zb0SnBE6YOjUKJrkNF2Fc88l5hIJQFJLkmIkjBVM8u8Jm2_BNhKbwjYSW4pi_SRlHJp6iysJA_SbNU-7DDkwluFGcgf7i0-2IZCSD9aAoa_ot7iShESdf03%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bce48481&sv=2)

circle-info

Since each account has it's own set of historical balances, when there's a month for which both accounts have a balance history, the balance that is kept will be based on the preference you've selected in this step. To help you decide this, you can head over to the [Net Wortharrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/net-worth)
 page to review the balance history for each of your accounts.

1.  To complete the merge, click on "Save Changes" and wait a few seconds for the merge to complete and for the changes to reflect on the Accounts page.
    

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-accounts)

Removing accounts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you no longer wish to see an account within Lunch Money, you can choose to remove it. Removing accounts is done via the 'Edit Account' panel of an account on the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
.

circle-exclamation

While the removal process is similar for all accounts, there are a number of different options when it comes to synced accounts, compared to manually-managed accounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-manually-managed-accounts)

Removing manually-managed accounts

1.  Go to the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
    
2.  Click on the manually-managed account to open the 'Edit Account' panel
    
3.  Scroll down and click on the red "Remove this account" button:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeaA2-FRTALdRxdaQXiNo9ga-82opsbws79YvMXLioXjIq_M9l7sQFvP-TDl70hTNxWtehNP9FzXH5xYa28YzKJJ5GbgE_kWYA3YS3-RUNEY9AlEI_XE0L756izj6nHCHIkf78EOg%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=464af51d&sv=2)

1.  If the account has transactions and recurring items associated with it, you will need to choose between these two options:
    
    1.  **"I want to keep my associated transactions and recurring items"** \- you will select another account to which you wish to assign your transactions and recurring items.
        
    2.  **"I want to remove all associated transactions and recurring expenses"** - this will permanently delete all transactions and recurring items associated with the deleted account.
        
    
2.  If you have a balance history associated with this account, will need to choose whether you wish to keep or remove the account’s balance history.
    
3.  Finally, review the operations and click on "Save Changes" to confirm the action.
    

The changes may take a few seconds to complete, and the account will be deleted and removed from the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#removing-synced-accounts)

Removing synced accounts

1.  Go to the [Accounts pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
    
2.  Click on the synced account to open the 'Edit Account' panel
    
3.  Scroll down and click on the red "Troubleshoot or remove account" button:
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXduYI3PtFLy7qVRLwqTkcjhqDg9dDlNO__TXW2xvsAg6iWWDoYoCJ7x8o4bS4-_WCtgImgAVOgyqy7t5mVRSEn7MO7C12JRBKwGgLiuharB7uFnyoSi5Nv8yKlbj2skTUKH-xLcaA%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75011d31&sv=2)

1.  Once you click on “Troubleshoot or remove account”, you will have the following options:
    

chevron-right**Remove account and delete all associated data**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#remove-account-and-delete-all-associated-data)

If you have other accounts under that same Plaid connection, you will need to scroll down to choose whether you only wish to apply this action to the one account, or to all accounts under the same connection.

Click "Confirm", and you will be prompted with a confirmation dialog. Review the information and click on "Confirm changes" to proceed with the action.

⚠️ _Please note that as long as a Plaid connection contains active accounts, it's not possible to completely remove individual accounts under that same connection (as that will revoke the access to the remaining accounts). This means that the associated data will be deleted, yet the removed account may remain listed on the Accounts page with "Inactive" status. You can hide inactive accounts from your view using Filters,_ [_click here to learn more_](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-remove-inactive-synced-accounts)
_._

chevron-right**Remove account and keep data in a new manually-managed account**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#remove-account-and-keep-data-in-a-new-manually-managed-account)

If you have other accounts under that same Plaid connection, you will need to scroll down to choose whether you only wish to apply this action to the one account, or to all accounts under the same connection.

Click "Confirm", and you will be prompted with a confirmation dialog. Review the information and click on "Confirm changes" to proceed with the action.

⚠️ _Please note that as long as a Plaid connection contains active accounts, it's not possible to completely remove individual accounts under that same connection (as that will revoke the access to the remaining accounts). This means that you may end up seeing two accounts after this action: the new manually-managed account, as well as the original synced account now listed with "Inactive" status. You can hide inactive accounts from your view using Filters,_ [_click here to learn more_](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-remove-inactive-synced-accounts)
_._

chevron-right**Merge account data into another existing account**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#merge-account-data-into-another-existing-account)

When you choose this option, you will select the account to which you wish to merge. You may only choose to merge with an active synced account (that is, a healthy connection), or a manually-managed account. You will also be able to choose whether to keep the source balance or the destination balance. Since each account has it's own set of historical balances, when there's a month for which both accounts have a balance history, the balance that is kept will be based on the preference you've selected in this step. To help you decide this, you can head over to the [Net Wortharrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/net-worth)
 page to review the balance history for each of your accounts. To complete the merge, click on "Save Changes" and wait a few seconds for the merge to complete and for the changes to reflect on the Accounts page.

⚠️ _Please note that as long as a Plaid connection contains active accounts, it's not possible to completely remove individual accounts under that same connection (as that will revoke the access to the remaining accounts). This means that after merging, you may still see the original account listed on the Accounts page with "Inactive" status. You can hide inactive accounts from your view using Filters,_ [_click here to learn more_](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/faq#how-do-i-remove-inactive-synced-accounts)
_._

chevron-right**Temporarily pause syncing this account**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#temporarily-pause-syncing-this-account)

This option will only display for synced accounts in an "Active" state. Once you select this option and click on "Confirm", the account status will change to "Inactive".

When paused, the account will no longer sync balance updates and transactions. To resume syncing, click on the account to open the 'Edit Account' panel, click on 'Resume syncing this account' and then click on 'Start reactivation'. The account's status should change to 'Active'.

chevron-right**Trigger a refresh for this account to get the latest transactions and balances**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#trigger-a-refresh-for-this-account-to-get-the-latest-transactions-and-balances)

This is an option for active accounts that haven't received updates from Plaid for a while. This option will force a refresh to get the latest transactions and balances from Plaid. Note that an update from Plaid does not guarantee new data to be imported. It is simply a way to trigger Lunch Money to go to Plaid and inquire on any new data available.

chevron-right**Get help from customer support**[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/managing-accounts#get-help-from-customer-support)

If you are unsure about the best option to go with, feel free to reach out to us for assistance! Simply select this option and click on "Confirm" to open the 'Bank syncing support' pop-up menu.

Last updated 1 month ago

# FAQ | Knowledge Base

### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions

1.  [How do I track transfers between my own accounts?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-track-transfers-between-my-own-account)
    
2.  [How do I handle transfers between accounts of different currencies?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-transfers-between-accounts-of-different-currencies)

4.  [How do I handle mortgage payments?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-mortgage-payments)
    
5.  [How do I handle the case where others pay me back for a large bill that I paid for?](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-the-case-where-others-pay-me-back-for-a-large-bill-that-i-paid-for)

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-track-transfers-between-my-own-accounts)

How do I track transfers between my own accounts?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Lunch Money, internal transfers between your own accounts (including credit card payments, mortgage payments, etc.) would consist of one debit transaction and one credit transaction, categorized in a dedicated transfer category. In Lunch Money, we recommend using the default '_Payment, Transfer_' category for any transfers between your own accounts. This category has the '[Exclude from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)
' and '[Exclude from budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)
' category properties enabled, to ensure that the transactions in the category won't affect your total income and expenses.

circle-info

If you don't have the 'Payment, Transfer' category set up on your account, you can set it up yourself via the Categories page. Just make sure to enable the 'Exclude from totals' and 'Exclude from budget' [category properties](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties)
.

Let's say you transfer $500 from your checking account to pay off your mortgage. You will log this by creating two transactions: A debit of \-$500 in Account A, and a credit of $500 in Account B. Both categorized in the '_Payment, Transfer_' category:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F2JpuWZ6pf0QE3G96MzA6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2312c03f-8125-4da9-ad69-9d2accbbc634&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4289a0f9&sv=2)

In the 'Account' column for each transaction, you will indicate the affected account. When paying towards the mortgage, the credit transaction should have the account set to the Mortgage account (as that is the account receiving the money). By setting the accounts associated with the debit and credit transactions, the account balances will automatically update.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-transfers-between-accounts-of-different-currencies)

How do I handle transfers between accounts of different currencies?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you track transfers between two accounts of different currencies, then the debit and credit transactions of the transfer should each be tracked in a different currency. You will need to enter the transactions in the currency that matches the account they are associated with.

Let's say you are moving money from Account A (**USD**) to Account B (**EUR**). You will have two transactions as follows:

*   Debit transaction in **USD** from Account A
    
*   Credit transaction in **EUR** to Account B
    

As long as you record the transactions in the same currency as the accounts they are in, the balances of the accounts will also be reflected correctly.

Both transactions should be categorized in the default 'Payment, Transfer' category which has the '[Exclude from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)
' and '[Exclude from budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)
' category properties enabled, to ensure that the transactions in the category won't affect your total income and expenses.

circle-exclamation

**Note:** If you group the two transactions, you won't end up with a total of 0.00 as you typically would with transfers transactions of the same currency. That is because the conversion rate used may differ from the conversion rate at your bank. We suggest leaving the two transfer transactions ungrouped in this case.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-credit-card-payments)

How do I handle credit card payments?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For credit card payments, usually made up of one debit to your cash account and one credit to your credit card, we recommend using the default [category](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories)
 "**Payment, Transfer"**. This category is set to be [excluded from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories#exclude-from-totals)
 and [excluded from budgets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories#exclude-from-budget)
, so these transactions should not affect your overall numbers or budget. Transactions in this category should also total up to $0 at the end of the month.

For instance, let's say you spend $10 at the grocery store and $50 on a few other purchases, all on the same credit card. You'll have expense transactions like the following:

Category

Amount

Amount Type

Account

Groceries

$10

Debit

Credit card

Shopping

$20

Debit

Credit card

Restaurants

$30

Debit

Credit card

You will end up making a credit card payment of $60 to cover all those expenses. This will be represented by two transactions:

1.  Debit of $60 on your cash account denoting an amount paid from your cash account
    
2.  Credit of $60 on your credit card denoting an amount received from your cash account
    

The two transactions should be categorized as "**Payment, Transfer"** (or any other category marked with the '[exclude from budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)
' and '[exclude from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)
' properties):

Category

Amount

Amount Type

Account

Payment, Transfer

$60

Debit

Cash account

Payment, Transfer

$60

Credit

Credit card

circle-info

To keep finances organized, you can group the two transactions. Grouped transactions will appear as a single entry on the transactions table, and in the case of credit card payments, will display with a total of zero as the debit and credit transactions cancel each other out.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-mortgage-payments)

How do I handle mortgage payments?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Similar to credit card payments and other transfers between your own accounts, mortgage payments should be made up of one debit transaction and one credit transaction, categorized in a dedicated transfer category. In Lunch Money, there's a default 'Payment, Transfer' category, which is what we recommend to use for any transfers between your own accounts. This category has the '[Exclude from totals](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-totals)
' and '[Exclude from budget](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties#exclude-from-budget)
' category properties enabled, to ensure that the transactions in this category won't affect your total income and expenses.

circle-info

If you don't have the 'Payment, Transfer' category set up on your account, you can set it up yourself via the Categories page. Just make sure to enable the 'Exclude from totals' and 'Exclude from budget' [category properties](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/categories/category-properties)
.

Let's say you move $500 from your checking account to pay off the mortgage. You will log this by creating two transactions: A debit of \-$500 from Account A, and a credit of $500 to Account B. Both categorized in the 'Payment, Transfer' category:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252F2JpuWZ6pf0QE3G96MzA6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2312c03f-8125-4da9-ad69-9d2accbbc634&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4289a0f9&sv=2)

In the 'Account' column for each transaction, you will indicate the affected account. When paying towards the mortgage, the credit transaction should have the account set to the Mortgage account. By setting the accounts associated with the debit and credit transactions, the account balances will automatically update.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-handle-the-case-where-others-pay-me-back-for-a-large-bill-that-i-paid-for)

How do I handle the case where others pay me back for a large bill that I paid for?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We generally recommend using our grouped transactions feature for this use case. Assuming you footed the bill and your roommates end up paying you back their portion, group together all of these transactions and you should be left with a transaction that represents how much you paid. You can then treat this as a high-level transaction and assign a category to it.

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252F-M4qoiT1TayjXzf3X11E%252F-M4qrjb1p1A-NDEXiWb7%252Fgroup-gif-2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23bb087a-f9cb-4993-b878-4a7918ed9bf0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0e8c6d0&sv=2)

If you don't want to bother recording your friends' payment, you can **split** the transaction and simply categorize the portion paid by your friends to a new category called "Reimbursed" which is excluded from totals and excluded from budgets. This ensures that amount is not counted towards your own expenses.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#is-there-a-limit-on-how-many-transactions-i-can-add)

Is there a limit on how many transactions I can add?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are limits to how many transactions you can upload on a single request but there isn't a limit on total transactions you add. This limit differs depending on the upload method (CSV or API).

For analytics and whatnot there's currently a hardcoded limit of 20,000 when fetching transactions, so if you have transactions over 10+ years, you may not be able to see the full picture if you do an "all-time" analysis.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#what-are-some-ways-i-can-stay-on-top-of-manually-adding-transactions)

What are some ways I can stay on top of manually adding transactions?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some suggestions from our users on how to stay on top of manually adding transactions!

1.  A recurring task in Things (my task manager of choice) that forces me to spend 5-10 minutes at the end of each week rounding things up.
    
2.  My partner and I live in a primarily cash-based society. We keep a little pile of receipts in the office and every few days when it stacks too high, one of us will take it and input transactions manually. Takes about 10 minutes each time!
    
3.  A Lunch Money user, Derek Reiff created [Milk Moneyarrow-up-right](https://milkmoney.club/)
    , a mobile-friendly solution for quick add on-the-go. ([Github sourcearrow-up-right](https://github.com/dareiff/quick-add)
    )
    
4.  Create a Google form for inputting transactions, and every week or so, export the data as CSV and import it into Lunch Money
    

Finally, there is a secret, undocumented feature which we should really take time to improve upon– the [Lunch Money Quick Add screenarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/transactions/new)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#why-cant-i-update-the-category-for-my-recurring-transactions)

Why can't I update the category for my recurring transactions?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The issue is that recurring items all share the same category. So all transactions linked to the same recurring item will inherit that recurring item's category and merchant name. As such, updating the category of a transaction is a non-action as it gets overridden by the recurring item's category anyway.

If you want to change the category of that transaction, you will need to update the category of a recurring item from the [Recurring Itemsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/recurring)
 page, thereby updating the category of all linked transactions. You also have the option on the [Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/settings)
 page of foregoing categories completely for recurring items and having them all be categorized as "Recurring".

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-deal-with-duplicate-transactions)

How do I deal with duplicate transactions?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In some cases, you may find duplicate transactions appearing on the Transactions page. To easily go through duplicates and remove them, we recommend using the Deduplication tool.

The Deduplication Tool will search through the active transaction list view to locate similar transactions based on your choice of 2 or more criteria.

For a step-by-step tutorial on how to use the Deduplication Tool, please [see here](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/other-features#deduplication-tool)
.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/finances/transactions/transactions#how-do-i-unsubscribe-from-the-automatic-imported-transactions-emails)

How do I unsubscribe from the automatic imported transactions emails?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The emails you receive for newly imported transactions are sent out by Email Rules that are triggered when new transactions sync into Lunch Money. These Rules are managed on the [Rules pagearrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules)
 (Setup > Rules). On the Rules page, you can click on "[Email Rulesarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/rules?filter=email)
" on the left side of the screen to filter the view to only display Email Rules. Finally, select all undesired rules and click on "Delete selected" to remove them.

Last updated 1 month ago

# Adding Accounts | Knowledge Base

In Lunch Money, you can add and keep track of any account or asset, whether it's a bank account, a loyalty card, a physical wallet, a crypto asset, real estate or a vehicle!

circle-exclamation

**Managing accounts or assets in multiple currencies?**

Make sure to add those currencies under ‘Supported Currencies’ via the Settings page, to ensure that those are available as an option when editing transaction amounts and account balances.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#jump-to)

Jump to:

*   [How to add synced bank accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-add-synced-bank-accounts)
    
*   [How to add manually-managed assets or accounts](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-add-manually-managed-assets-or-accounts)
    
*   [How to link a cryptocurrency wallet for automatic syncing](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)
    
*   [How to set up manually-managed crypto assets](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-set-up-manually-managed-crypto-assets)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-add-synced-bank-accounts)

How to add synced bank accounts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lunch Money supports [automatic imports](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports)
 from [supported banking institutions](https://support.lunchmoney.app/guides/automatic-imports#support-for-international-banks)
 via Plaid. To connect a bank account for automatic syncing, follow these steps:

1.  Open the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page and click on the orange "Add account" button
    
2.  In the 'Add Account or Asset' panel on the right, click on "Auto-import from my bank"
    
3.  Select the relevant country and click on "Continue" to load the Plaid Link flow
    

circle-info

For the US & Canada, investment accounts (including Wealthsimple, Questrade, Fidelity, etc.) are now available to connect by selecting the country and then enabling the option "I want to sync an investment account" at the bottom, before clicking on "Continue":

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfuj6w4FBSKSOrShqFpFGnrMfl6adZrMLGg0COserhN-woAsF5kNjcBrqGElF975KrspyhybV6OsjBHEipB3NenGqGl7-ulSrUVuCZM-o0B6DXtUxynIYSLM8xToA4GtOsWbOSrTndJ7tsjPhgjVMdp3sJA%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ed23abd&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Get started", and then click on "Continue as a guest"
    
2.  Search and select your institution, and then enter your credentials to log in
    
3.  Next, if prompted, select all accounts that you wish to sync and click on "Continue":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcK6dUTNUPl7gj7qVzY2cfv0KcZQCc0QFJi-sQ2hbJd4qfKYPJ6S7hDP4WiJR9hqVJy4E06gl3wUFA7mk0Hf4f43yk8fvRUucnYAmtPk4iEN2FfKb4mJA4K5YWC03E9lpF9--0ERBRsT44rDJI_W0ik25Ue%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8991b7f6&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Continue" again to reach the 'Setup Account' prompts
    
2.  Select the relevant account settings and click "Next" (repeat for each account):
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc-psK23QfBNmwgFHOgfEcELDh9eAjyEGki9tK0MzLn1txMvmYwYBlZ9svQv9GWd2QfNRbqG9jhiwnJLhX8xbe_3mieOcEPaM_TRvr1W0lSQUZNokqMocWTEK9_V924JHmAZ0CwsJRTMF7jOCIe1Orxsei_%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b21874dc&sv=2)

All set! Your newly added synced accounts will now be listed on the Accounts page, and the balance will automatically update. If you chose to import transactions for the accounts, they will start syncing as well.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-add-manually-managed-assets-or-accounts)

How to add manually-managed assets or accounts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add a manually-managed account or asset, follow these steps:

1.  Open the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page and click on the orange "Add account" button
    
2.  In the 'Add Account or Asset' panel on the right, scroll down to 'Create a manually-managed asset:', select the relevant account type (eg. Credit) and click on "Next":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F160037560-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-M2W9WT63LQTW7JYT64B%252Fuploads%252Fb2EmAoxEnbA7U4vzNEly%252Ff34c8f74e84fade88985df2a9a8f5282.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad1e2560-d85a-48cb-91dc-0b40cc40244a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=523b5d21&sv=2)

1.  Select the account subtype from the available options, and click "Next"
    
2.  Fill in the account name, institution, and display name, and click "Next"
    
3.  Enter the current account balance and click on "Save & Close" to confirm
    

Once added, the account will be listed on the Accounts page. You will then be able to manually add transactions to this account via the Transactions page, and the balance will be adjusted accordingly. You will also be able to manually update the balance via the Accounts page when necessary.

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-link-a-cryptocurrency-wallet-for-automatic-syncing)

How to link a cryptocurrency wallet for automatic syncing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Depending on the wallet, the connection between Lunch Money and the cryptocurrency wallet is established either using an API Key and Private Key, or a Wallet Address.

1.  Go to the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page and click on the orange "Add account" button
    
2.  In the 'Add Account or Asset' panel on the right, click on "Link my cryptocurrency wallet"
    
3.  Select your cryptocurrency wallet and fill in the required information to connect
    

circle-info

Not sure where to locate the required keys or wallet address? Follow the links below:

*   How do I generate a Coinbase API key?
    
*   Where do I find my Ethereum wallet address?
    
*   How do I generate a Kraken API key?
    

Once connected, you will see your connected cryptocurrency accounts added to the Accounts page. The balance will automatically sync and display both the source amount and the fiat balance in your primary currency:

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcvnfHefmeekxLxz-KezXeaXvCWd_dYFEBBebBF9Am8ooiQQFRX7u0PCsBH6wxisPdnQOayXA1pErGmbuFDASxGOkItPAroMFoc6kKK2WUbaonoAJH1jJpasuVLF44SOSgVtjN8dBcc1QD0La1zmyte41cU%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26f3f423&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://support.lunchmoney.app/setup/accounts/adding-accounts#how-to-set-up-manually-managed-crypto-assets)

How to set up manually-managed crypto assets


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting up cryptocurrency for manual tracking is available for over 300 supported cryptocurrencies, with more being added every week by user demand!

circle-info

If you don't see your cryptocurrency supported, please [let us knowarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts?show_feedback=cryptocurrency-request)
 and we'll work on adding it! 🙂

1.  Open the [Accountsarrow-up-right](https://my.lunchmoney.app/accounts)
     page and click on the orange "Add account" button
    
2.  Next, scroll to the bottom section labeled 'Create a manually-managed asset:', choose "Cryptocurrency", and click "Next":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfxqThFGwIG_Dd3aq8jEjrvTS9vlSt29ReKGvf-WLYohkoN0fkTAPng1VWaGk87-upC2C-2EsKorhJk2_lSB8HmbwabRTvUYnGJVClvxrKEOTgxKXVhle5_og4tBDByYFD8utiKuUPgseEXrbN-3LJYnY48%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad8c066b&sv=2)

1.  Select your cryptocurrency from the dropdown menu, and click "Next":
    

![](https://support.lunchmoney.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdyGwCGHQ3G1mC0IUFzW2brqoOvf10HDf2VzEQBRvfm9LR16mtvNwiLyDcbAG4lw3JodfAJY9uC9aa-i1oy9wgggFuVF5AT3mJ87CFg9cYrxes-bC97tAIB67gSF2XodxhprY3Wl5WXxsTzVedTc5Kgbb3k%3Fkey%3DoQeghgURANzNNR0vDuJ6tg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28c06be8&sv=2)

1.  Fill in the account name, institution, and display name, and click "Next":
    
2.  Now you will enter how much of the token you hold. This is the number of tokens you hold and not the fiat balance (we will automatically calculate that for you based on your primary currency).
    
3.  To confirm the creation of this new asset, click on "Save & Close"
    

Once added, you will see your manually-managed cryptocurrency account listed on the Accounts page with the balance displaying both the source amount and the fiat balance in your primary currency.

Last updated 19 days ago

# Transaction Actions | Knowledge Base

####
